# physics.optics [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [In-plane vector-field imaging of propagating surface phonon polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27030)
*Richarda Niemann,Dorothée S. Mader,Gonzalo Alvarez-Pérez,Ana I. F. Tresguerres-Mata,Aitana Tarazaga Martín-Luengo,Stefan Partel,Joshua D. Caldwell,Niclas S. Mueller,Martin Wolf,Javier Martín-Sánchez,Pablo Alonso-González,Alexander Paarmann*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于非线性红外-可见光宽场和频产生（sum-frequency generation）显微术的新方法，能够选择性地探测面内极化激元场分量，弥补了传统散射式近场光学显微术主要探测面外分量的不足，并通过空间干涉测量实现对极化激元矢量场的完整成像与色散测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统散射式近场光学显微术（scattering-type near-field optical microscopy）受限于纳米针尖的细长几何结构，主要探测光学近场的面外（out-of-plane）分量，而面内（in-plane）场分量通常只能间接推断而非直接测量，因此需要一种能够直接且选择性地探测面内极化激元场分量的互补方法。

Method: 采用非线性红外-可见光宽场和频产生（wide-field sum-frequency generation）显微术：利用非线性信号的短波长可见光提供高空间分辨率以访问红外消逝模式；借助非线性过程的对称性选择定则（symmetry selection rules），通过空间干涉测量（spatial interferometry）实现对两个面内极化激元场分量的偏振选择性成像。

Result: 以金天线激发的AlN-空气界面表面声子极化激元（surface phonon polaritons）为实验体系，成功验证了该方法的可行性。一个简单的半解析模型复现了独特的传播模式。通过可调谐窄带激光进一步实现了高光谱成像（hyperspectral imaging），获得了极化激元的色散关系（polariton dispersion）。

Conclusion: 该宽场显微方法在红外纳米光子结构（infrared nanophotonic structures）的深入、高通量研究中具有广阔前景，能够更完整地获取极化激元系统的矢量场信息。

Abstract: Polariton interferometry through optical near-field microscopy has become a powerful tool in nanophotonics, enabling direct spatial access to the propagation characteristics of strongly confined, evanescent polariton modes. Scattering-type near-field optical microscopy has matured as the prime tool for such studies, yet mostly the out-of-plane components of the optical near fields are probed, owing to the elongated geometry of the nanotip. Here, we demonstrate a complementary far-field nonlinear microscopy approach which allows to selectively probe in-plane polariton field components. Accessing the full vector field is interesting when studying complex mode patterns such as hyperbolic polaritons or skyrmions, where the in-plane field components are typically only inferred from the out-of-plane component but not measured directly. To this end, we use nonlinear infrared-visible wide-field sum-frequency generation microscopy, where the short visible wavelength of the nonlinear signal provides the high spatial resolution to access evanescent modes in the infrared. The symmetry selection rules of the nonlinear process further enable polarization-selective imaging of both in-plane polariton field components through spatial interferometry. The concept is demonstrated experimentally using surface phonon polaritons at the AlN-air interface launched by a gold antenna. A simple, semi-analytical model reproduces the peculiar propagation patterns. Hyperspectral imaging with a tunable narrowband laser further gives access to the polariton dispersion. The wide-field methodology holds high promise for in-depth and high-throughput studies of infrared nanophotonic structures.

</details>


### [2] [Observation of Non-Hermitian Skin Dynamics in the Liouvillian Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27043)
*Shu Yang,Yeyang Sun,Lingrui Hong,Yi Yang*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文在光子网格晶格中实现了一个可调开放系统量子行走平台，通过控制相位噪声和增益-损耗不平衡，连续调节从相干量子行走到非相干经典行走的转变，并利用非厄米趋肤动力学作为探针，定量揭示了退相干对非厄米输运的主动重塑作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放量子系统通常无法完美保持相位相干性，耦合到不可控环境需要基于Liouvillian框架的密度矩阵描述，因此在一个可编程平台上实现并探测此类动力学，对于连接相干物理学与实际耗散环境至关重要。

Method: 在光子网格晶格中实现可调开放系统量子行走：通过受控相位噪声产生可调退相干（dephasing），通过非互易增益-损耗不平衡提供独立可调的非厄米驱动，从而在相干量子行走与经典随机行走之间连续插值；使用非厄米趋肤动力学（non-Hermitian skin dynamics）作为探针，测量质心漂移随相干性和非厄米参数的变化。

Result: 实验观察到从相干性增强到退相干增强输运的交叉行为，与量子信道模拟结果定量吻合；进一步编程空间和时间界面，展示了界面累积效应以及由瞬时信道决定的长时漂移行为。

Conclusion: 建立了一个可控光子平台用于模拟开放量子动力学，证明退相干可以主动重塑非厄米输运（non-Hermitian transport）。

Abstract: Open quantum systems generally do not perfectly preserve phase coherence: coupling to uncontrolled environments requires a density-matrix description based on the Liouvillian framework beyond pure-state wave evolution. Realizing and probing such dynamics in a programmable platform is therefore essential for connecting coherent physics to realistic dissipative settings. Here we implement a tunable open-system quantum walk in a photonic mesh lattice, where controlled phase noise produces adjustable dephasing and non-reciprocal gain-loss imbalance provides an independently tunable non-Hermitian drive. This allows us to continuously interpolate between coherent quantum walks and incoherent classical walks, and to observe how directional transport evolves in the Liouvillian regime. Using non-Hermitian skin dynamics as a probe, we measure the center-of-mass drift over both the coherence and non-Hermiticity parameters, revealing a crossover from coherence-enhanced to decoherence-enhanced transport in quantitative agreement with quantum-channel simulations. We further program spatial and temporal interfaces to demonstrate interface accumulation and a long-time drift governed by the instantaneous channel. Our results establish a controllable photonic platform for simulating open quantum dynamics and show that decoherence can actively reshape non-Hermitian transport.

</details>


### [3] [Accessing both electrochemical SEIRA and SERS with ultrasensitive metamaterials for enhanced molecular identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27367)
*Nicolas Spiesshofer,Tabitha Jones,Sarah May Sibug Torres,Zoltan Sztranyovszky,Caleb Todd,Shijie Zhu,Yeeun Roh,Rakesh Arul,Alexander Squires,Ivana Qianqi Lin,Angela Demtriadou,David O. Scanlon,Viv Lindo,Jeremy J. Baumberg*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 提出一种电化学可清洁的超材料（metamaterial），首次实现在流动体系中同时进行实时表面增强红外吸收（SEIRA）和表面增强拉曼光谱（SERS）的多模态光谱电化学检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表面增强红外吸收（SEIRA）和表面增强拉曼光谱（SERS）是互补的超灵敏化学指纹识别技术，但缺乏一种可重复使用的基底来有效结合这两种技术，从而限制了非侵入式光学传感的实用性。

Method: 设计了一种电化学可清洁的超材料（metamaterial），将其作为可重复使用的基底，在流动体系中同时实现实时的SEIRA和SERS检测。

Result: 该超材料能够研究表面吸附物种和扩散层；纳米间隙折射率变化引起1400 nm/RIU的光谱位移；实现超灵敏分析物检测；通过结合SERS和SEIRA，揭示了分子（电）化学转化过程，并追踪了分析物-电极界面处选择定则（selection rules）与对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）的变化。

Conclusion: 这种增强的多模态光谱电化学（multimodal spectro-electrochemistry）技术适用于理解电极上的电荷传输机制（charge transport mechanisms）与界面动力学（interfacial dynamics），并能够对多种分子过程进行实时流动监测。

Abstract: Surface-enhanced IR absorption (SEIRA) and surface-enhanced Raman spectroscopy (SERS) are complementary techniques that allow for ultrasensitive chemical fingerprinting. Non-invasive optical sensing would be significantly improved by a robust implementation of a reusable substrate that combines these techniques. Here, we present an electrochemically-cleanable metamaterial that enables combined real-time SEIRA and SERS in flow. This metamaterial facilitates the study of surface-adsorbed species and diffusion layers, elicits spectral shifts from changes in nanogap refractive index of 1400 nm/RIU, and delivers ultrasensitive analyte detection. Combining SERS and SEIRA clarifies molecular (electro)chemical transformations and tracks changes in selection rules and symmetry breaking at the analyte-electrode interface. This development in enhanced multimodal spectro-electrochemistry is suited for multiple domains, including understanding charge transport mechanisms and interfacial dynamics at electrodes, and is capable of real-time flow monitoring for a wide range of molecular processes.

</details>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Observable strong field effects of extra spacetime dimension in the braneworld black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26152)
*K. K. Nandi,R. N. Izmailov,R. Kh. Karimov,A. A. Potapov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于Randall-Sundrum膜世界图像中的DMPR黑洞解，研究潮汐电荷参数Υ对强场引力透镜观测量和回音准正则模频率的影响，发现Υ可显著修正Schwarzschild黑洞的透镜观测量和QNM频率，且DMPR−黑洞的Pretorius-Khurana临界指数更低，表明更强的Lyapunov不稳定性及更亮的吸积盘；最后以SgrA*黑洞为例探讨了EHT阴影观测对Υ的可能约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弦理论（string theory）启发的膜世界图像（braneworld picture）引入了超出四维时空的额外维度，可能在短距离（强场）引力实验中产生可观测的非平凡效应。本文旨在研究Randall-Sundrum膜世界框架下DMPR黑洞解中潮汐电荷（tidal charge）Υ对强场透镜观测量和回音准正则模（quasinormal mode, QNM）频率的影响，并探讨其与Schwarzschild黑洞的差异。

Method: 采用Dadhich、Maartens、Papadopoulos和Rezania（DMPR）导出的精确膜世界黑洞解，该解形式上类似Reissner-Nordström黑洞但在物理上不同，其中潮汐电荷Υ是来自第五维度的印记，允许Schwarzschild度规（Υ=0）的幂律修正项±Υ²/r²取正负两种符号（对应DMPR±两种变体）。研究在强场极限下分析Υ对透镜观测量的影响，并在eikonal近似下比较DMPR−与DMPR+的回音QNM频率。

Result: 潮汐电荷可显著修正Schwarzschild黑洞的透镜观测量和QNM频率。DMPR−黑洞的Pretorius-Khurana临界指数γ低于Schwarzschild黑洞，表明更强的Lyapunov不稳定性（Lyapunov instability），这意味着DMPR−黑洞的吸积盘（accretion disk）会更亮。以SgrA*黑洞为例，事件视界望远镜（EHT）对其阴影大小的观测可用于对Υ施加可能的约束。

Conclusion: 膜世界中的潮汐电荷Υ能够显著改变强场透镜观测量和QNM频率特性，其中DMPR−黑洞表现出更强的轨道不稳定性与更明亮的吸积盘，这为通过天文观测（如EHT的阴影观测）检验额外维度理论提供了可能的途径。

Abstract: Inspired by the string theory, the braneworld picture introduces extra dimensions beyond the four that may have observable non-trivial effects in short distance (strong field) gravity experiments. A case in point is the Randall-Sundrum braneworld picture that projects the $5d$ bulk Weyl tensor onto the $3d$ brane providing a stress tensor in the effective Einstein field equations on the brane. Dadhich, Maartens, Papadopoulos and Rezania (DMPR) derived an exact braneworld black hole solution of the brane vacuum field equations. The solution formally resembles that of Reissner-Nordström but is physically different from it since the "tidal charge" $Υ$ in the solution is not the electric charge but an imprint from the fifth dimension allowing both signs in the power law modification $\pm \frac{Υ^{2}}{r^{2}}$ to the Schwarzschild metric $\left( Υ= 0\right)$. The corresponding black holes are designated as DMPR$\pm$. We study here the effect of $Υ$ on strong field lensing observables and compare in the eikonal limit the ring down quasinormal mode (QNM) frequencies of DMPR$-$ with those of DMPR$+$, the two variants of tidal charge modified Schwarzschild black hole ($Υ= 0$). It turns out that the tidal charge can significantly modify the Schwarzschild lensing observables and QNM frequencies. In particular, we find that the Pretorius-Khurana critical exponent $γ$ of circular null orbits in the DMPR$-$ black hole has a lower value than that for the Schwarzschild black hole, which indicates a stronger Lyapunov instability suggesting that the accretion disks of DMPR$-$ black holes would appear brighter. The case of the SgrA* black hole is considered for a possible constraint on $Υ$ from the EHT observation of its shadow size.

</details>


### [5] [Charged Axially Symmetric Exponential Metric: Exact Solutions to the Einstein-Maxwell Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26160)
*S. Habib Mazharimousavi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦（Einstein-Maxwell）框架下，通过直接求解场方程和哈瑞森变换（Harrison transformation）等精确解生成技术，构造并分析了曲宗-查齐时空（Curzon-Chazy spacetime, CCS）的带电、磁化及旋转推广，系统地揭示了电荷、磁荷及引力磁荷（gravitomagnetic charge）如何从CCS中产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于构造并分析轴对称指数度量（即曲宗-查齐时空）在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦框架下的带电和磁化推广，以探索通过精确解生成技术如何系统地引入电、磁和引力磁荷。

Method: 首先通过直接求解耦合场方程，得到由双磁单极子（dyonic monopole）构型驱动的精确带电轴对称指数解；然后利用厄恩斯特形式体系（Ernst formalism）中的哈瑞森变换重新导出同一带电几何结构；随后应用磁哈瑞森变换获得梅尔文型（Melvin-type）磁化变形时空；最后通过埃勒斯变换（Ehlers transformation）生成带有非零NUT荷（NUT charge）的稳态无旋涡旋几何结构，并进一步通过磁哈瑞森变换得到磁化涡旋时空。

Result: 导出的带电解在无荷极限下平滑退化为真空CCS，在特殊参数条件下退化为极端雷斯纳-诺德斯特伦时空（extremal Reissner-Nordström spacetime）；直接求解法与哈瑞森变换法得到的带电几何结构等价；通过后续变换成功生成了磁化、涡旋及含NUT荷的推广时空。

Conclusion: 该结果展示了电荷、磁荷和引力磁荷如何通过精确解生成技术从CCS中系统地产生，拓展了对维耳类（Weyl class）时空及其物理内涵的理解。

Abstract: We construct and analyze charged and magnetized extensions of the axially symmetric exponential metric, that is known as the Curzon-Chazy spacetime (CCS) within the Weyl class. Working within the Einstein-Maxwell framework, we first derive an exact charged axially symmetric exponential metric by directly solving the coupled field equations for a dyonic monopole configuration. The solution is shown to reduce smoothly to the vacuum CCS in the neutral limit and to the extremal Reissner-Nordström spacetime in a special parameter regime. We then rederive the same charged geometry using the Harrison transformation in the Ernst formalism, establishing the equivalence between the direct and solution-generating approaches. Subsequently, we apply the magnetic Harrison transformation to obtain a Melvin-type magnetized deformation of the spacetime. Finally, by implementing the Ehlers transformation, we generate a stationary but nonrotating swirling geometry endowed with a nonvanishing NUT charge, which we identify invariantly via the Komar dual mass. A further magnetic Harrison transformation yields a magnetized swirling (NUT-type) spacetime. These results demonstrate how electric, magnetic, and gravitomagnetic charges arise systematically from the CCS through exact solution-generating techniques.

</details>


### [6] [Images of Braneworld black holes with radiatively inefficient accretion flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26166)
*Chengjia Chen,Yin Hao,Zelin Zhang,Qiyuan Pan,Jiliang Jing*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 通过广义相对论辐射传输模拟生成与事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope, EHT）观测一致的M87*合成图像，发现CFM膜世界黑洞的潮汐参数对图像形态产生非单调影响，且图像差异度量高达10^3量级，表明即使借助未来ngEHT和BHEX观测，通过黑洞图像识别膜世界黑洞仍具有挑战性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视界尺度成像为强场区引力理论检验提供了变革性工具。CFM膜世界黑洞包含一个表征体几何（bulk geometry）潮汐效应的额外参数，对探测时空几何具有重要价值。

Method: 采用广义相对论辐射传输（general relativistic radiative transfer, GRRT）模拟，生成与M87* EHT观测一致的合成图像。利用归一化互相关系数（normalized cross-correlation coefficient）和DSSIM指数（DSSIM index）进行图像比较度量分析。

Result: 潮汐参数对图像形态产生非单调影响，揭示了时空几何与吸积等离子体可观测辐射之间的复杂耦合。图像差异度量的量级约为10^3，表明识别膜世界黑洞存在较大困难。

Conclusion: 即使借助未来ngEHT和BHEX等更高分辨率的观测设备，通过黑洞图像区分膜世界黑洞与标准广义相对论预言的黑洞仍然挑战重重。

Abstract: Horizon-scale imaging acts as a transformative tool for probing spacetime geometry, enabling stringent tests of gravitational theories in the strong-field regime. The Casadio-Fabbri-Mazzacurati(CFM) black hole in braneworld contains an extra parameter that characterizes the tidal effects from the bulk geometry, making it highly valuable for this task. We perform general relativistic radiative transfer (GRRT) simulations and generate synthetic images consistent with Event Horizon Telescope observations of M87*. We find that the tidal parameter imprints nonmonotonic changes on the image morphology, underscoring the intricate coupling between spacetime geometry and the observable radiation from the accreting plasma. We also analyze the image-comparison metric using normalized cross-correlation coefficients and the DSSIM index and find that the magnitudes of these mismatches are on the order of 10^3, which implies that identifying braneworld black holes through black hole images remains challenging even with future ngEHT and BHEX observations.

</details>


### [7] [Electrically Charged Distorted Black Holes: Thermodynamics, Particle Dynamics, and Quasinormal Signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26174)
*Gamal G. L. Nashed,Salvatore Capozziello*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过Harrison变换构建了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中带电扭曲黑洞的精确解，系统分析了其热力学性质、带电粒子运动、黑洞阴影以及标量扰动行为，发现电荷不改变视界结构但扩展了热力学相空间，而扭曲参数显著影响光学和扰动可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究带电扭曲黑洞（charged distorted black hole）的精确解及其物理性质，特别是在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦（Einstein-Maxwell）理论框架下，探索电磁场引入非线性变换对黑洞几何和热力学的影响。

Method: 采用Harrison变换（Harrison transformation）构建带电扭曲黑洞的精确解；利用有效势形式论（effective potential formalism）分析带电试验粒子运动；通过几何光学方法研究黑洞阴影；采用WKB方法（WKB method）估计准正则模（quasinormal mode）频谱。

Result: 电荷不改变Killing视界位置，视界面积、熵和温度由几何扇区决定；扭曲参数改变圆形轨道并移位最内稳定圆轨道；扭曲参数将光子球面向外推移，增大阴影表观尺寸；光子轨道与领先eikonal准正则模频率之间存在几何对应关系；零视界电势阻止带电超辐射放大（superradiant amplification）。

Conclusion: 荷电通过电磁势扩展热力学相空间；电磁相互作用通过规范不变组合(ω - q_s ξ_t)进入弱耦合准正则模谱，并偏移扰动振荡频率；光学与扰动可观测量通过光子轨道建立几何联系。

Abstract: We construct an exact solution for the electrically charged extension of a distorted black hole spacetime within Einstein-Maxwell theory using the Harrison transformation. The resulting solution represents a charged deformation of a static distorted vacuum geometry in which the electromagnetic field is introduced through a nonlinear transformation preserving the radial structure of the seed spacetime. Consequently, the Killing horizon remains determined solely by the seed metric and it is not shifted by the electric charge. We analyze the thermodynamic properties of the solution and show that the horizon area, entropy, and temperature are governed by the geometric sector, while the electric charge enlarges the thermodynamic phase space through the electromagnetic potential. The motion of charged test particles is studied using the effective potential formalism, where the distortion parameter modifies circular orbits and shifts the location of the innermost stable circular orbit. We also investigate the black hole shadow for a static observer at finite distance and show that the distortion parameter displaces the photon sphere outward, increasing the apparent shadow size. A geometric correspondence between the photon orbit, determining the shadow and the leading eikonal quasinormal-mode frequency, is discussed, linking optical and perturbative observables. Finally, we study charged scalar perturbations and show that the vanishing horizon electric potential prevents a charged superradiant amplification. In the weak-coupling regime, the quasinormal-mode spectrum is estimated using the WKB method, where the electromagnetic interaction enters through the gauge-invariant combination $(ω- q_s ξ_t)$ and shifts the oscillation frequencies of the perturbations.

### [8] [Gravitational Wave Signatures from Periodic Orbits around a Non--commutative Schwarzschild Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26182)
*N. Heidari,A. A. Araújo Filho,I. P. Lobo,V. B. Bezerra*

TL;DR: 本文研究非对易施瓦西黑洞（non-commutative Schwarzschild black hole）周围大质量粒子的周期运动及其产生的引力波发射，发现非对易修正使特征轨道半径和角动量减小，并基于S2星近日点进动给出参数约束Θ/M²<0.014，同时计算了引力波极化并观察到相位偏移和振幅增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非对易几何修正对黑洞周围粒子运动及其引力波信号的影响，以期通过天文观测约束非对易参数。

Method: 分析非对易施瓦西黑洞的有效势（effective potential）、边缘束缚轨道（marginally bound orbit）和最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）；通过有理参数q分类周期轨道；利用绝热近似（adiabatic approximation）和数值kludge近似（numerical kludge approximation）计算引力波极化。

Result: 非对易修正使特征轨道向更小半径移动、角动量降低；(E, L)平面允许区域下移；增大非对易参数降低周期轨道所需能量并使轨道更紧凑；基于S2星近日点进动得到约束Θ/M²<0.014；引力波极化出现相位偏移和整体振幅增强。

Conclusion: 非对易效应显著影响黑洞周围粒子动力学和引力波波形，为通过天文观测检验非对易几何提供了潜在途径。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate massive particle motion and the gravitational wave emission generated by periodic trajectories around a non--commutative \textit{Schwarzschild} black hole sourced by a Lorentzian matter distribution. We analyze the effective potential, the marginally bound orbit, and the innermost stable circular orbit, showing that non--commutative corrections shift these characteristic orbits toward smaller radii and reduce their corresponding angular momenta. The allowed region in the $(E, L)$ plane is also displaced toward lower values, favoring more tightly bound configurations. Periodic trajectories are classified through the rational parameter $q$, which relates the radial and azimuthal frequencies. For a fixed orbital topology, increasing the non--commutative parameter lowers the energy required to produce the orbit and results in more compact zoom--whirl configurations. Small deviations from the periodic energies are also shown to generate precessional drift. From the periastron advance of the S2 star around Sgr~A$^*$, we obtain the preliminary bound $Θ/M^{2}<0.014$. Finally, using the adiabatic and numerical kludge approximations, we compute the gravitational wave polarizations and find phase shifts and an overall enhancement of the amplitude.

### [9] [Extended Thermodynamics and Throttling Process of Charged AdS Black Holes in ModMax-dRGT Massive Gravity with Sharma-Mittal Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26210)
*Naba Jyoti Gogoi,Hassan Hassanabadi,Himasri Pinapothu,Dhruba Jyoti Gogoi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了四维带电反德西特黑洞在ModMax非线性电动力学与dRGT-like有质量引力框架下的扩展热力学，包括焦耳-汤姆孙膨胀和P-V临界性。采用广义Sharma-Mittal熵考虑非广延统计关联，推导了修正的霍金温度、比热、焦耳-汤姆孙系数等解析表达式。结果表明：ModMax场共形非线性扩大了冷却域；Sharma-Mittal参数控制局部热力学稳定性；而全局反演相边界由有质量引力子背景主导。吉布斯自由能分析揭示了类范德瓦耳斯一级相变，各修正机制在临界区域呈现清晰的物理退耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的黑洞热力学中，熵通常遵循面积律（Bekenstein-Hawking熵），但在考虑了非线性电动力学（如ModMax理论）或有质量引力（如dRGT理论）等修正时，黑度系统的统计行为可能偏离广延性。本文旨在将三者（ModMax电动力学、dRGT有质量引力、Sharma-Mittal非广延熵）统一到一个自洽框架中，系统研究这些修正对四维带电AdS黑洞热力学相行为的影响。

Method: 在扩展相空间中，采用广义Sharma-Mittal熵来处理非广延统计关联，结合ModMax非线性电动力学和dRGT-like有质量引力的组合框架。通过解析推导，得到修正的霍金温度（Hawking temperature）、比热（specific heat）、焦耳-汤姆孙系数（Joule-Thomson coefficient）和状态方程（equation of state），并分析吉布斯自由能（Gibbs free energy）的相变结构。

Result: (1) ModMax场的共形非线性参数γ通过将反演转变（inversion transition）推向更小的视界半径，扩大了物理可及的冷却域；(2) Sharma-Mittal参数δ和R关键地控制着局部热力学稳定性和反演半径；(3) 全局反演相边界由有质量引力子（massive graviton）背景决定；(4) 吉布斯自由能呈现出类范德瓦耳斯（van der Waals-like）一级相变，具有清晰的燕尾结构（swallow-tail structure）；(5) 在临界区域各修正机制表现出物理退耦：ModMax非线性抑制电磁相互作用而改变临界相边界，Sharma-Mittal参数决定竞争相的相对热稳定性，有质量引力主导宏观相图。

Conclusion: 非线性效应（ModMax电动力学）与非广延效应（Sharma-Mittal熵）对黑洞热力学相行为的影响在临界区域呈现清晰的物理退耦，表明热力学相现象可以作为一种区分非线性与非广延修正的鲁棒诊断工具。这些结果为深入理解修正引力理论下黑洞的热力学性质提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We investigate the extended thermodynamics, including the Joule-Thomson expansion and $P-V$ criticality, of a four-dimensional charged anti-de Sitter (AdS) black hole within the combined framework of ModMax nonlinear electrodynamics and dRGT-like massive gravity. Operating in the extended phase space and employing the generalised Sharma-Mittal entropy to account for non-extensive statistical correlations, we derive exact analytical expressions for the modified Hawking temperature, specific heat, Joule-Thomson coefficient, and the equation of state. Our analysis of the throttling process reveals that the conformal nonlinearities of the ModMax field ($γ$) expand the physically accessible cooling domain by shifting the inversion transition to smaller horizon radii. While the Sharma-Mittal parameters ($δ$, $R$) critically govern local thermodynamic stability and the inversion radius, the global inversion phase boundary remains fundamentally dictated by the massive graviton background. Furthermore, an analysis of the Gibbs free energy uncovers a van der Waals-like first-order phase transition characterized by a distinct swallow-tail structure. We observe a clear physical decoupling in the critical regime: ModMax nonlinearities modify the critical phase boundary by suppressing electromagnetic interactions, Sharma-Mittal parameters dictate the relative thermal stability of competing phases, and massive gravity governs the overarching macroscopic phase landscape. These results highlight the sensitivity of thermodynamic phase phenomena as robust diagnostic tools for distinguishing nonlinear and non-extensive modifications to black hole physics.

### [10] [Time-domain framework for the Teukolsky equation with a particle source using comoving hyperboloidal coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26339)
*Aditya Vaswani,Leor Barack,Oliver Long,Rodrigo Panosso Macedo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于共动、空间紧致超双曲坐标的1+1维Teukolsky方程时域积分方案，有效消除了非物理增长模式问题，并在Schwarzschild背景下的标量场和s=-2 Teukolsky方程测试中验证了长期稳定性，为极端质量比散射中的完整自引力计算铺平了道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克服现有数值演化方案中由于未引入紧致化（compactification）而出现的非物理增长模式（nonphysical growing modes）问题，并简化粒子世界线上跳跃条件（jump conditions）的应用，从而为极端质量比散射（extreme-mass-ratio scattering）中的完整引力自力（gravitational self-force）计算奠定基础。

Method: 采用共动、空间紧致超双曲坐标（comoving, spatially compactified hyperboloidal coordinates），在1+1维框架下对含点粒子源（point-particle source）的Teukolsky方程进行时域积分，并基于Schwarzschild背景对标量场和s=-2自旋权重Teukolsky方程实施测试。

Result: 在标量场情形下，针对圆型测地线轨道（circular geodesic orbit）和散射测地线轨道（scattering geodesic orbit）两种源均验证了方案的有效性；在s=-2 Teukolsky方程测试中，通过与未紧致化特征坐标（characteristic coordinates）方法的对比，展示了方案的长期稳定性（long-term stability）及无增长模式行为。

Conclusion: 该方案有效避免了非物理增长模式，简化了跳跃条件处理，并展现出良好的长期稳定性，为极端质量比系统中的完整引力自力计算提供了可行路径。

Abstract: We present a scheme and implementation code for time-domain integration of the Teukolsky equation in 1+1 dimensions with a point-particle source, based on comoving, spatially compactified hyperboloidal coordinates. We demonstrate that the scheme evades the problem of nonphysical growing modes that plague some numerical evolution schemes without compactification. Our use of comoving coordinates greatly simplifies the application of jump conditions on the particle's worldline. We develop our method and test its performance for a scalar field on a Schwarzschild background, first for a circular geodesic orbit source and then for a scattering geodesic orbit. We then present a test implementation of the method for the $s = -2$ Teukolsky equation, illustrating its long-term stability and absence of growing-mode behavior through comparison with similar results using noncompactified characteristic coordinates. Our method paves the way to calculations of the full gravitational self-force in extreme-mass-ratio scattering.

### [11] [Thermodynamics of thin-shell wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26370)
*Francisco S. N. Lobo,Manuel E. Rodrigues*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了动态薄壳虫洞（dynamic thin-shell wormholes）的统一热力学描述，从透明真空背景推广至含体物质穿过喉部的情形。研究表明孤立壳层在透明演化下熵守恒（$TdS=0$）；存在体物质时，广义第一定律为$T\dot{S}=A\Phi$，熵随物质流入（出）而增加（减少）。文章给出了零尘埃和无质量标量场的通量表达式，并讨论了量子对产生（霍金式辐射）及广义第二定律。作为天体物理应用，研究了零尘埃吸积的临界速率与时空几何及物态方程的敏感依赖关系。涨落诱导的随机力导致朗之万描述及相应的涨落-耗散关系，产生喉径扩散与额外熵产生。该框架普遍适用于广义相对论中的球对称薄壳构造，为薄壳虫洞的一致热力学描述、吸积过程的敏感性及通过未来引力波观测探测奇异致密天体提供了证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献对薄壳虫洞（thin-shell wormholes）的动力学研究较多，但其热力学性质缺乏统一的理论框架。本文旨在发展一个涵盖透明真空背景与包含体物质穿过喉部的一般情形的热力学描述，并探讨其天体物理应用与可观测后果。

Method: 从透明真空背景（transparent vacuum bulk）情形出发，逐步放松透明性条件（transparency condition），允许体物质（bulk matter）穿过虫洞喉部。基于薄壳形式论（thin-shell formalism）推导出广义第一定律$T\dot{S}=A\Phi$，并给出零尘埃（null dust）和无质量标量场（massless scalar field）的通量表达式。引入广义第二定律（generalised second law），并通过能量通量涨落诱导的随机力建立朗之万描述（Langevin description）与涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relation）。

Result: 孤立薄壳在透明演化下熵守恒，$TdS=0$；体物质存在时，广义第一定律为$T\dot{S}=A\Phi$。零尘埃吸积的临界速率对时空几何和壳层物态方程敏感。涨落导致喉径扩散与额外熵产生。广义第二定律在热从高温区流向低温区时与标准热力学预期一致。

Conclusion: 薄壳虫洞在广义相对论的球对称框架下具备一致的热力学描述，其动力学行为对吸积过程敏感，可通过未来引力波观测（gravitational wave observations）为探测奇异致密天体（exotic compact objects）提供新途径。

Abstract: We develop a unified thermodynamic description of dynamic thin-shell wormholes, starting from the transparent (vacuum bulk) case and then relaxing the transparency condition to include bulk matter crossing the throat. For isolated shells, we show that the entropy is conserved under transparent evolution, $TdS=0$, which holds for arbitrary dynamical motion of the throat within the assumptions of the thin-shell formalism. When bulk matter is present, the generalised first law becomes $T\dot{S}=AΦ$, where $Φ$ is the net energy flux; entropy increases (decreases) when matter flows into (out of) the shell. Explicit expressions for the flux are provided for null dust and massless scalar fields, and quantum pair production (Hawking-like emission) is also discussed. A formulation of the generalised second law is presented, and it is consistent with standard thermodynamic expectations under conditions where heat flows from hotter to colder regions. As a concrete astrophysical application, we study accretion of null dust: the critical accretion rate above which the throat becomes dynamically unstable depends sensitively on the spacetime geometry and the shell equation of state, highlighting the environmental dependence of these configurations. Fluctuations in the energy flux induce a stochastic force on the throat dynamics, leading to a Langevin description with an associated fluctuation-dissipation relation. This results in diffusion of the throat radius and additional entropy production. The framework applies to a broad class of spherically symmetric thin-shell constructions within general relativity. Our results provide evidence that thin-shell wormholes admit a consistent thermodynamic description, quantify their sensitivity to accretion processes, and suggest possible avenues for probing exotic compact objects with future gravitational wave observations.

</details>


### [12] [Effect of the magnetic monopole charge on Dirac entanglement and Bell non-locality in Hayward spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26372)
*Abdessamie Chhieb,Mohamed Ouchrif*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了Hayward正则黑洞时空中Dirac场的二分量子关联，发现费米子关联在无限高温极限下因泡利不相容原理（Pauli exclusion principle）仍保持非零，而霍金温度随正则参数$g$增大而降低有助于量子信息保持，表明奇点消解与费米子量子关联鲁棒性之间存在密切联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Hayward正则黑洞（Hayward regular black hole）时空中Dirac场的二分量子关联行为，特别是霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）对纠缠态的影响，以及正则参数$g$在其中的作用。

Method: 采用Wootters concurrence和CHSH Bell参数（CHSH Bell parameter）两类度量，分析一个惯性观测者与一个近地平线观测者共享的纠缠态在霍金辐射影响下的演化。

Result: 费米子关联在无限高温极限下仍非零，与玻色子情形不同，原因在于泡利不相容原理阻止全同费米子占据同一量子态；部分纠缠被重新分配到视界内不可达模式中；可达模式在所有有限霍金温度下均呈现Bell非定域性（Bell nonlocality），而内部模式从未违反Bell不等式；正则参数$g$仅通过霍金温度影响关联，$g$增大使霍金温度降低，从而增强量子信息保持。

Conclusion: 奇点消解（singularity resolution）与费米子量子关联在正则黑洞时空中的鲁棒性之间存在紧密联系。

Abstract: We investigate bipartite quantum correlations of Dirac fields in the spacetime of a Hayward regular black hole. Using the Wootters concurrence and the CHSH Bell parameter, we analyze the influence of Hawking radiation on an entangled state shared by an inertial observer and a near-horizon observer. We show that, unlike the bosonic case, fermionic correlations remain nonzero even in the infinite-temperature limit owing to the Pauli exclusion principle, while part of the entanglement is redistributed to inaccessible modes inside the horizon. The accessible modes exhibit Bell nonlocality for all finite Hawking temperatures, whereas the interior modes never violate Bell's inequality. The Hayward regularity parameter $g$ affects the correlations only through the Hawking temperature, whose decrease with increasing $g$ enhances the preservation of quantum information. These results suggest a close connection between singularity resolution and the robustness of fermionic quantum correlations in regular black-hole spacetimes.

### [13] [Stueckelberg Gauge Invariant Formulation of MOG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26427)
*John W. Moffat*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种修正引力（MOG）的Stueckelberg规范不变形式化方法，通过引入补偿标量场使有质量矢量场具有规范不变性，无需希格斯场或自发对称性破缺，从而将有效牛顿引力耦合与宇宙学演化分离，为MOG的宇宙学检验提供了规范不变框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有修正引力（MOG）理论中，有质量矢量场的规范不变性尚未得到明确处理，且有效牛顿引力耦合通常依赖于对称性破缺真空（symmetry-breaking vacuum）。需要一种形式化方法，使得矢量质量与引力耦合的宇宙学演化相互独立，从而为早期宇宙约束和晚期大尺度引力现象提供一致的检验基础。

Method: 采用Stueckelberg机制（Stueckelberg mechanism），通过引入一个补偿标量场（compensating scalar field）使有质量矢量场（massive vector field）获得规范不变性。该构造不依赖希格斯场（Higgs field）、自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）或真空期望值（vacuum expectation value），将有效牛顿引力耦合（effective Newtonian gravitational coupling）的处理与矢量质量的起源分离开来。

Result: 所提形式化方法保留了MOG的有限程矢量相互作用（finite-range vector interaction），同时允许有效引力耦合被当作独立的标量量或尺度相关量（scale-dependent quantity）处理。这为将MOG与核合成（nucleosynthesis）、宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background）、大尺度结构（large-scale structure）、引力透镜（lensing）及距离数据（distance data）进行对比提供了规范不变框架。

Conclusion: Stueckelberg形式化方案为MOG的宇宙学检验建立了理论框架。由于早期宇宙约束与晚期大尺度引力现象不再必须与对称性破缺真空相关联，该框架在宇宙学测试中具有重要区分意义。

Abstract: We develop a Stueckelberg gauge-invariant formulation of modified gravity (MOG). The massive vector field is made gauge-invariant by introducing a compensating scalar field, without requiring a Higgs field, spontaneous symmetry breaking, or a vacuum expectation value to fix the effective Newtonian gravitational coupling. This separates the gauge-invariant origin of the vector mass from the cosmological evolution of the gravitational coupling. The formulation preserves the finite-range vector interaction of MOG, while allowing the effective gravitational coupling to be treated as an independent scalar or scale-dependent quantity. This distinction is important for cosmological tests, since early-universe constraints and late-time large-scale gravitational phenomena need not be tied to a symmetry-breaking vacuum. The Stueckelberg formulation provides a gauge-invariant framework for comparing MOG with nucleosynthesis, cosmic microwave background, large-scale structure, lensing, and distance data.

### [14] [Massive boson stars: Waveform-based branch diagnosis with neural reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26436)
*Bo-Xuan Ge*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于分支条件神经重建模型的分支条件重建方法，通过比较候选波形假设的重建质量，从引力波波形中诊断大质量玻色子星并合的结果，并证明并合结果编码于波形形态学中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究能否利用大质量玻色子星（massive boson star）并合产生的引力波波形（gravitational waveform）来诊断并合的最终结果（merger outcome），而非仅依靠初始参数空间（initial parameter space）的直接分类。

Method: 利用已有的数值相对论（numerical relativity）目录，构建一个分支条件神经重建模型（branch-conditioned neural reconstruction model），通过比较候选波形假设的重建质量来推断并合结果，使诊断基于波形本身；同时比较监督基线模型（supervised baseline model）与知识蒸馏学生模型（distilled student model）。

Result: 研究发现并合结果编码在波形形态学（waveform morphology）中，可通过分支条件重建方法恢复；蒸馏学生模型在性能上与监督基线模型可比。

Conclusion: 该工作为基于波形分类的、具有多种可能终态的奇异致密天体并合（exotic compact-object mergers）的诊断提供了初步步骤。

Abstract: We investigate whether gravitational waveforms from massive boson-star mergers can be used to diagnose the underlying merger outcome. Using an existing numerical-relativity catalogue, we construct a branch-conditioned neural reconstruction model and infer the outcome by comparing the reconstruction quality of candidate waveform hypotheses. This makes the diagnosis waveform-based rather than a direct classification in the initial parameter space. We compare a supervised baseline model with a distilled student model and find that the merger outcome is encoded in the waveform morphology and can be recovered through branch-conditioned reconstruction. Our results provide a first step toward waveform-based classification of exotic compact-object mergers with multiple possible final states.

</details>


### [15] [Primordial black hole formation in bulk-viscous cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26532)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究体粘滞（bulk viscosity）作为一种耗散效应，是否以及如何影响原初黑洞（PBH）在早期宇宙中的形成阈值和质量分布。

Method: 采用数值模拟（numerical simulations）确定坍缩阈值和PBH质量；对近阈值坍缩拟合标准临界标度律（critical-scaling law）。

Result: 临界阈值$μ_c$对状态方程参数$w$的依赖关系与无粘情况类似，但阈值整体提升了与体粘滞强度$ε$相当的量；在固定$w$下，$μ_c$的增加近似线性于$ε$；体粘滞导致PBH质量增强。

Conclusion: 体粘滞能够系统性地修改PBH的坍缩阈值和质量标度律，是理解早期宇宙PBH形成的重要耗散机制。

Abstract: We investigate primordial black hole (PBH) formation in a cosmological background with bulk viscosity. Using numerical simulations, we determine the collapse threshold and the resulting PBH mass. We find that the critical threshold $μ_c$ retains a dependence on the equation-of-state parameter $w$ similar to that in the inviscid case, but is enhanced by an amount comparable to the bulk-viscosity strength $ε$. For fixed $w$, the increase in $μ_c$ is approximately linear in $ε$. By fitting the standard critical-scaling law for near-threshold collapse, we find that the bulk viscosity leads to an enhancement in the resulting PBH mass. These results indicate that bulk viscosity can systematically modify both the PBH threshold and PBH mass scaling law in the early universe.

### [16] [Accretion Flow onto Ellis-Bronnikov Wormhole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26628)
*R. M. Yusupova,R. Kh. Karimov,R. N. Izmailov,K. K. Nandi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用重子流体模型描述宇宙暗能量，考虑幻影（phantom）、精质（quintessence）、尘埃（dust）和刚性物质（stiff matter）四种流体类型；利用复杂Wick旋转（Wick rotation）揭示EBWH与Schwarzschild黑洞之间的数学联系，并分析流体径向速度、密度及EBWH质量变化率的剖面。

Result: 幻影和非幻影吸积下Schwarzschild黑洞的质量均增加，而EBWH的质量则减少；零ADM质量EBWH（即非零Wheelerian质量）的吸积行为与有质量EBWH一致，无法通过吸积流区分两者。

Abstract: Study of accretion onto wormholes is rather rare compared to that onto black holes. The accreting fluid is assumed to be phantom, quintessence, dust and stiff matter. We begin by first pointing out a mathematical novelty showing how the EBWH can lead to the Schwarzschild black hole under a complex Wick rotation. Then, we analyze the profiles of fluid radial velocity, density and the rate of mass variation of the EBWH due to accretion and compare the profiles with those of the Schwarzschild black hole. We also analyze accretion to the massless EBWH that has zero ADM mass but has what we call nonzero Wheelerian mass (``mass without mass''), composed of the non-trivial scalar field, that shows gravitational effects. Our conclusion is that the mass of SBH due to phantom and non-phantom accretion increases consistently with known results, while, in contrast, the mass of EBWH decreases. Accretion to massless EBWH (i.e., to nonzero Wheelerian mass) shares the same patterns as those of the massive EBWH; hence there is no way to distinguish massive and massless cases by means of accretion flow. The contrasting mass variations due to phantom accretion could be a reflection of the distinct topology of the central objects.

Method: 采用哈密顿分析（Hamiltonian analysis）方法，借助 Cartan 几何（Cartan geometry）工具，从最一般的 Carroll 不变拉格朗日量出发，系统推导约束结构（constraint structure）、规范对称性（gauge symmetries）和哈密顿向量场（Hamiltonian vector fields），并在磁 Carroll 体系（magnetic Carrollian regime）中引入类似 Ashtekar 变量（Ashtekar-like variables）的表达。

Conclusion: 该工作为 Carroll 引力体系的哈密顿形式化建立了完整框架，为后续在量子引力和凝聚态物理中的应用提供了基础。

Abstract: The Carrollian regime of gravity provides a useful ultrarelativistic framework for studying asymptotically flat spacetimes, horizon dynamics, and condensed matter systems. In this paper, we present a comprehensive Hamiltonian analysis of the most general Carroll-invariant Lagrangian that can be derived from the Holst action. To guide the analysis, Cartan geometry tools are used. We identify the full constraint structure of the theory, characterize its gauge symmetries, obtain the explicit form of the Hamiltonian vector fields and introduce Ashtekar-like variables for the magnetic Carrollian regime. We also discuss in detail an analog of the time gauge employed in the Hamiltonian analysis of the Holst action for general relativity.

### [18] [Conservation law of super-Lorentz charges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26848)
*Geoffrey Compère,Sébastien Robert*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义引力散射假设下，系统给出了空间无穷远处真空相对论引力场的领头阶与次领头阶完整描述。作者利用渐近Bondi-Sachs场和Beig-Schmidt场，分别提出了超平移不变和超平移-对数平移不变的荷定义，并推导了超洛伦兹荷在未来与过去空间无穷远之间的守恒律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义引力散射条件下，真空相对论引力场在空间无穷远处的大半径展开中，其领头阶由超动量（supermomentum）、对偶超动量（dual supermomentum）和全局超平移标架（global supertranslation frame）决定。然而，次领头阶的完整描述需要引入超洛伦兹荷（super-Lorentz charges）、领头尾荷（leading tail charges）和首阶破缺剥离荷（leading peeling-breaking charges）这三组额外荷。这些荷的超平移不变定义及守恒律尚不明确，构成了本研究的主要动机。

Method: 本研究采用渐近分析方法，首先在Bondi-Sachs形式体系中给出这些荷的超平移不变定义，然后在Beig-Schmidt形式体系中给出它们的超平移不变且对数平移不变（logarithmic translation invariant）定义。利用空间无穷远处边界de Sitter时空上相关波动方程的齐次与非齐次解性质，推导了超洛伦兹荷的守恒律。

Result: 研究得到：超洛伦兹荷在未来与过去空间无穷远之间遵循守恒律；超洛伦兹aspects（super-Lorentz aspects）由Bondi-Sachs场非局域地定义。

Conclusion: 本文在广义引力散射假设下，建立了空间无穷远处引力场次领头阶荷的完整理论框架，给出了超洛伦兹荷的超平移不变定义并证明了其守恒性，深化了对渐近时空对称性与引力辐射之间关系的理解。

Abstract: Under assumptions compatible with generic gravitational scattering, the vacuum relativistic gravitational field is entirely determined at leading order in the large radius expansion at spatial infinity by its supermomentum, its dual supermomentum and its global supertranslation frame. At subleading order, the gravitational field is determined by three additional sets of charges: the super-Lorentz charges, the leading tail charges and the leading peeling-breaking charges. In this work we provide a supertranslation-invariant definition of these charges in terms of asymptotic Bondi-Sachs fields as well as a corresponding supertranslation and logarithmic translation invariant definition of these charges in terms of Beig-Schmidt fields. Using the properties of homogeneous and inhomogeneous solutions to relevant wave equations over the boundary de Sitter spacetime at spatial infinity, we derive the conservation law of super-Lorentz charges between the future and past of spatial infinity. We obtain that the super-Lorentz aspects are non-locally defined from the Bondi-Sachs fields.

### [19] [Bipartite entanglement of the primordial Majorana during inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26869)
*Ai-chen Li,Han-Qing Shi,Keyun Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究早期宇宙暴涨（inflation）期间，利用原初马约拉纳场（Majorana field）作为费米子探针来探测量子关联。在无挠率FLRW时空和轴子-暴涨背景下，推导了双分量马约拉纳模式方程和配对动量基下的二次哈密顿量（quadratic Hamiltonian），并证明哈密顿量对角化与费米子压缩形式化（fermionic squeezing formalism）给出相同的Bogoliubov变换。由于费米统计限制每个螺旋度扇区（helicity sector）只有真空和单对态，希尔伯特空间有限，可显式计算二分量子信息度量。结果表明，足够轻的马约拉纳模式在超视界尺度上仍能保持增强的二分量子性（bipartite quantumness），对数负性（logarithmic negativity）尤其明确地揭示了残留的不可分离性。该结果本身并非观测性Bell检验或完整的退相干分析，而是识别了一个受泡利统计限制的物质扇区，在该扇区中仅靠视界逃逸不足以抹除双模态中的量子特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找暴涨期间量子关联的费米子探针，并检验视界逃逸是否足以抹除费米子系统中的量子特征；已有的研究多集中在玻色子系统，费米子探针因泡利不相容原理（Pauli exclusion principle）导致的有限希尔伯特空间特性尚未被充分探索。

Method: 在无挠率FLRW时空和轴子-暴涨（axion-inflation）背景下，推导双分量马约拉纳模式方程，构建配对动量基下的二次哈密顿量；通过哈密顿量对角化与费米子压缩形式化得到Bogoliubov变换，将模式函数映射到瞬时占据数和每个(𝒌,−𝒌)配对的双模态（two-mode state）；利用有限希尔伯特空间直接计算约化模的von Neumann熵和马约拉纳配对的对数负性。

Result: 对于足够轻的马约拉纳模式，超视界尺度下二分量子性得到增强；对数负性明确揭示了双模态间残留的不可分离性（inseparability）；仅靠视界逃逸（horizon exit）并不足以完全抹除双模态中的量子特征。

Conclusion: 识别了一个受泡利统计限制的物质扇区（Pauli-bounded matter sector），在该扇区中视界逃逸本身不足以消除量子特征；未来需进一步开展开放量子系统研究，考察再加热（reheating）和暴胀子诱导相互作用如何使原初费米子探针经典化（classicalize）。

Abstract: We use a primordial Majorana field as a fermionic probe of quantum correlations during inflation. Working in a torsion-free FLRW spacetime, we derive the two-component Majorana mode equations in an axion-inflation background and construct the corresponding quadratic Hamiltonian in the paired momentum basis. Hamiltonian diagonalization and the fermionic squeezing formalism are shown to give the same Bogoliubov transformation, providing a direct map from the Majorana mode functions to the instantaneous occupation number and to the two-mode state of each $(\boldsymbol{k},-\boldsymbol{k})$ pair. Because Fermi statistics restricts each helicity sector to the vacuum and one-pair states, the resulting Hilbert space is finite and the bipartite quantum-information measures can be evaluated explicitly. We compute the von Neumann entropy of the reduced mode and the logarithmic negativity of the Majorana pair. Both diagnostics indicate that sufficiently light Majorana modes can retain enhanced super-horizon bipartite quantumness, with the logarithmic negativity making the residual inseparability especially explicit. Our result does not by itself constitute an observational Bell test or a complete decoherence analysis; rather, it identifies a Pauli-bounded matter sector in which horizon exit alone is not sufficient to erase the quantum signature encoded in the two-mode state, thereby motivating an open-system study of how reheating and inflaton-induced interactions classicalize primordial fermionic probes.

### [20] [A geometric multimessenger consistency test of radiative and near-zone gravity with LISA and SKA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26945)
*Bhooshan Gadre*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于轨道倾角（orbital inclination）的多信使自洽性检验方法，通过比较致密双星脉冲星（compact binary pulsar）在射电计时（radio timing）中夏皮罗延迟形状参数（Shapiro-delay shape parameter）与低频引力波（gravitational wave）中张量极化振幅比（tensor polarization amplitude ratio）对倾角的测量结果，检验广义相对论预言。利用LISA–SKA代表性源进行精度估计，发现对于双中子星系统精度约为$4\times10^{-3}$，对于脉冲星–黑洞系统精度可达$9\times10^{-4}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前已有通过射电精密计时和低频引力波两种独立信使观测到的致密双星脉冲星，但尚缺乏一种基于相同双星几何结构的直接自洽性检验方法。利用这两种信使均可独立测量轨道倾角这一共同几何量，为检验广义相对论（general relativity）和探测可能的系统误差提供了新途径。

Method: 定义共同历元残差$\eps(t_0)=s_{\rm Shapiro}(t_0)-s_{\rm GW}(t_0)$，其中$s_{\rm Shapiro}$来自射电计时中夏皮罗延迟形状参数对倾角的测量，$s_{\rm GW}$来自引力波信号中张量极化振幅比对倾角的测量。采用七参数计时费舍尔矩阵（Fisher matrix）和包含银河系前景的平均天空LISA灵敏度曲线进行精度估计。射电基线采用保守参数：$σ_{\rm TOA}=1\,μ{\rm s}$、$N_{\rm eff}=10^4$，以综合射电噪声、抖动、残余色散与散射效应、轮廓演化和观测间隔损失。

Result: 对于距离$d=5\,{\rm kpc}$、观测四年的系统，双中子星系统的$\eps$测量精度$σ_\eps\simeq4\times10^{-3}$，而假想的脉冲星–黑洞系统可达$σ_\eps\simeq9\times10^{-4}$。前者是更可靠的实测天体物理基准，后者展示了若发现此类高信噪比（high-SNR）啁啾源时的潜力。

Conclusion: 广义相对论预言$\eps=0$，非零值则暗示存在未建模的系统误差或广义相对论近区与辐射区引力描述的不匹配。有用案例主要受限于引力波极化测量能力，而射电计时提供了近区倾角参考测量。该结果为未来对射电和引力波联合观测的致密双星脉冲星进行联合贝叶斯分析（joint Bayesian analysis）设定了定量目标。

Abstract: Compact binary pulsars observed both through precision radio timing and low-frequency gravitational waves offer a direct way to compare the same binary geometry with two independent messengers. We propose a multimessenger consistency test based on the orbital inclination, measured from the Shapiro-delay shape parameter in radio timing and from the tensor polarization amplitude ratio in the gravitational-wave signal. Defining the common-epoch residual $\eps(t_0)=s_{\rm Shapiro}(t_0)-s_{\rm GW}(t_0)$, general relativity predicts $\eps=0$, while a nonzero value would indicate either an unmodeled systematic or a mismatch between the near-zone and radiative descriptions of gravity. We estimate the attainable precision on this quantity for representative LISA--SKA compact binary pulsars using a seven-parameter timing Fisher matrix and a sky-averaged LISA sensitivity curve including the Galactic foreground. We adopt a conservative radio baseline, $σ_{\rm TOA}=1\,μ{\rm s}$ and $N_{\rm eff}=10^4$, intended to summarize radiometer noise, jitter, residual dispersion-measure and scattering effects, profile evolution, and cadence losses after wideband timing. For systems at $d=5\,{\rm kpc}$ observed for four years, we find $σ_\eps\simeq4\times10^{-3}$ for a favorable double neutron star and $σ_\eps\simeq9\times10^{-4}$ for a hypothetical pulsar--black-hole system. The former is the more robust astrophysical benchmark; the latter illustrates the reach if such a high-SNR chirping source is discovered. The useful cases remain limited mainly by gravitational-wave polarimetry, while radio timing supplies the near-zone reference measurement of the inclination. These results define a quantitative target for future joint Bayesian analyses of compact binary pulsars observed in both radio and gravitational waves.

</details>


### [21] [Time-domain evolution of Lorenz-gauge metric perturbations: taming the $\ell=m=1$ gauge instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27016)
*Jonathan Thornburg*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对极端质量比旋近（extreme-mass-ratio inspiral）系统中由小质量粒子在Schwarzschild/Kerr背景下引发的度规扰动（metric perturbation, MP）问题，提出了一种在时域中计算Lorenz规范（Lorenz gauge）下O(μ)级MP的方法。该方法通过对有源MP与同质MP进行线性组合并周期性正交化，有效抑制了不稳定的规范模式（unstable gauge mode），使得计算得到的“正交化”MP在Schwarzschild圆轨道测试案例中保持有界且满足Einstein方程与Lorenz规范条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算小质量粒子在Schwarzschild或Kerr背景黑洞时空中引发的时空度规扰动是广义相对论领域的长期研究课题，且对极端质量比旋近（extreme-mass-ratio inspiral）系统引力波的计算具有重要的天体物理动机。此前Dolan与Barack的工作发现，m=1模态下的Lorenz规范时域度规扰动普遍包含一种随时间线性增长的不稳定规范模式（unstable gauge mode），需要加以解决。

Method: 将Schwarzschild背景下的度规扰动（MP）分解为e^{imφ}模态；计算“正交化”MP h_{ab}^\text{ortho}，将其表达为有源MP h_{ab}^\text{source}与同质MP h_{ab}^\text{hom}（后者与时域有源MP并行演化）的线性组合；根据选定的内积（inner product）周期性地更新线性组合系数，使h_{ab}^\text{ortho}与h_{ab}^\text{hom}正交；粒子模型分别采用MP跃变条件（jump conditions）与有效源（effective source）两种方式。

Result: 在Schwarzschild圆轨道测试案例中，正交化MP h_{ab}^\text{ortho}满足O(μ)级Einstein方程与Lorenz规范条件，在t→∞时保持有界，且在有限后期时间中仅包含极少量不稳定规范模式成分。无论采用MP跃变条件还是有效源模型，结果均成立。随文附有数值代码。

Conclusion: 本文提出的正交化方法可有效抑制Lorenz规范时域度规扰动中的不稳定规范模式，为极端质量比旋近系统的引力波计算提供了可行的时域数值方案；代码已开源并存放于Black Hole Perturbation Toolkit中。

Abstract: Calculating the spacetime metric perturbation (MP) sourced by a small "particle" of mass $μM$ (with $0 < μ\ll 1$) moving in a Schwarzschild or Kerr "background" black hole spacetime of mass $M$ is a longstanding research area in general relativity. This calculation also has an important astrophysical motivation as a major step in calculating the gravitational waves emitted by an extreme-mass-ratio inspiral system. Here I consider the specific problem of the time-domain calculation of the $\mathcal{O}(μ)$ Lorenz-gauge MP $h_{ab}$ sourced by the particle. Decomposing the Schwarzschild-background MP into $e^{imφ}$ modes, Dolan and Barack [Phys. Rev. D 87, 084066 (2013), arXiv:1211.4586] found that the $m=1$ time-domain Lorenz-gauge MP generically contains an \emph{unstable gauge mode} which grows linearly with time. Here I demonstrate a method for computing a Lorenz-gauge time-domain evolution which is mostly free of this gauge mode. This method computes an "orthogonalized" MP $h_{ab}^\text{ortho}$ as a linear combination of the sourced MP and a homogeneous MP $h_{ab}^\text{hom}$ (evolved in parallel with the sourced MP). The linear combination is updated "occasionally" to make $h_{ab}^\text{ortho}$ orthogonal to $h_{ab}^\text{hom}$ with respect to a chosen inner product on MPs. I show that, for a Schwarzschild-circular-orbit test case, the resulting $h_{ab}^\text{ortho}$ satisfies the $\mathcal{O}(μ)$ Einstein equations and Lorenz gauge conditions, remains bounded as $t \to \infty$, and at late (finite) times contains only a small component of the unstable gauge mode. These results hold both with the particle modelled via MP jump conditions and with particle modelled by a "effective source". My numerical code for obtaining all of these results is included with this paper, and will be deposited in the Black Hole Perturbation Toolkit.

</details>


### [22] [Terrestrial Sagnac delay in scalar-tensor-vector-gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27033)
*R. Kh. Karimov,R. N. Izmailov,K. K. Nandi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过分析GPS Sagnac延迟的地面实验，将标量-张量-矢量引力理论（STVG）的无量纲参数α的取值范围从现有文献的0.03<α<2.47大幅压缩至0<α<10^{-5}，从而对该修正引力理论施加了强烈的实验约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: STVG（标量-张量-矢量引力）作为一种修正引力理论原型，能够在不引入暗物质的情况下解释星系旋转曲线、星系团动力学、子弹星系团现象及宇宙学数据，且与中子星质量观测更为吻合，但该理论中无量纲参数α的合理取值范围尚未明确，已有文献给出了0.03<α<2.47的较宽范围，需要进一步约束。

Method: 利用最新GPS（全球定位系统）波动数据不超出α相关修正项导致的陆地Sagnac延迟（Sagnac delay）变化这一约束条件，对STVG理论中的无量纲参数α进行重新限定。

Result: 在假设更新后的GPS波动不超过α依赖修正对地面Sagnac延迟的影响条件下，α的取值范围被显著压缩至0<α<10^{-5}，远窄于此前的0.03<α<2.47。

Conclusion: 该结果表明，STVG理论中的参数α受到来自GPS实验数据的极强约束，若将α限制在10^{-5}以下，则STVG作为一种修正引力理论的可行性将面临更严格的检验。

Abstract: The scalar-tensor-vector-gravity (STVG), a prototype of modified gravity developed by Moffat, can correctly explain galaxy rotation curves, cluster dynamics, Bullet Cluster phenomena and cosmological data without invoking the observationally elusive general relativistic (GR) dark matter. Further, recent observations of neutron star masses are shown to defy some GR predictions, whereas STVG turns out to be more consistent with those observations. These successes indicate that STVG could be a potential candidate for a new theory of gravity. However, an important question concerns the possible range of values of the STVG dimensionless parameter $α$ imposed by various physical scenarios. In the literature, the range $0.03<α<2.47$ corresponding to different central source masses has been suggested. We show here that the $α$ can be considerably constrained into the range $0<α<10^{-5}$ assuming that the updated GPS fluctuation does not exceed the $α$-dependent correction to the terrestrial Sagnac delay.

### [23] [A Shortest-Path Anisotropy Diagnostic for Black-Hole Graph Geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27248)
*Ariadna Uxue Palomino Ylla*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于最短路径多重性各向异性（shortest-path multiplicity anisotropy）的壳层统计量，用于分析黑洞内嵌几何（black-hole embedding geometries）的图离散化（graph discretization）结构。该统计量在多种球对称黑洞模型（Schwarzschild/Flamm、Reissner–Nordström、Bardeen、Hayward）中表现出与对数Kretschmann轮廓（logarithmic Kretschmann profile）强相关的稳定径向组织，而在平直对照几何中不重现该趋势。结果表明该统计量是一种曲率敏感的图诊断工具，可用于探测黑洞内嵌几何图中的曲率组织化结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于图的弯曲空间表示（graph-based representations of curved spaces）提供了一种探索几何信息如何编码在最短路径结构中的途径。本文旨在引入一种新的统计量，用于定量刻画黑洞几何图离散化中的曲率相关结构特征。

Method: 提出了一种基于壳层的最短路径各向异性统计量（shell-based shortest-path anisotropy statistic），其定义为从参考顶点到图距离壳层（graph-distance shell）上各顶点的最短路径数量的对数之立方平均偏差（cubic mean deviation）。将该统计量应用于静态球对称黑洞内嵌几何的图离散化，包括Schwarzschild/Flamm、Reissner–Nordström、Bardeen及Hayward背景，并采用平直对照几何进行对比验证。

Result: 该统计量在所有测试的黑洞家族中均表现出稳定的径向组织，且与对数Kretschmann轮廓（logarithmic Kretschmann profile）强相关，而平直对照几何不呈现该趋势。在Reissner–Nordström几何（M=1/2，电荷Q=0~0.4）中，种子平均后的径向与曲率轮廓相关性在十个随机种子上保持稳定；Bardeen和Hayward参数扫描也表现出类似的鲁棒性。对非黑洞基准曲面的额外测试表明该统计量并非通用的逐点曲率标量（pointwise curvature scalar）。

Conclusion: 最短路径多重性各向异性（shortest-path multiplicity anisotropy）可作为探测黑洞内嵌几何图离散化中曲率组织化结构的有用诊断工具。该统计量的解释依赖于图构造方式和对照几何选择，其本质是一种曲率敏感的图诊断（curvature-sensitive graph diagnostic）。

Abstract: Graph-based representations of curved spaces offer a way to probe how geometric information is encoded in shortest-path structure. In this work, we introduce a shell-based shortest-path anisotropy statistic for graph discretizations of embedded spatial slices of black-hole geometries. The statistic is based on the cubic mean deviation of the logarithm of the number of shortest paths from a reference vertex to vertices on a graph-distance shell. We test the diagnostic on graph discretizations of static, spherically symmetric black-hole embedding geometries, including Schwarzschild/Flamm, Reissner--Nordström, Bardeen, and Hayward backgrounds. Across these black-hole families, the statistic exhibits a stable radial organization that is strongly associated with the logarithmic Kretschmann profile, while matched-flat controls do not reproduce the same trend. For Reissner-Nordström geometries with $M=1/2$ and charges $Q=0,\ldots,0.4$, the seed-averaged radial and curvature-profile correlations remain stable over ten random seeds. Similar robustness is found for Bardeen and Hayward parameter scans. Additional tests on non-black-hole benchmark surfaces indicate that the statistic is not a universal pointwise curvature scalar; rather, it is a curvature-sensitive graph diagnostic whose interpretation depends on the graph construction and control geometry. These results suggest that shortest-path multiplicity anisotropy can provide a useful probe of curvature-organized structure in graph discretizations of black-hole embedding geometries.

### [24] [Endpoint Control of Thermodynamic Topological Classes for Fixed Charge \texorpdfstring{$d$}{d}-dimensional Reissner--Nordström Black Holes in a Cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27236)
*Rongrong Zhai*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过准局部方法研究了腔内Reissner-Nordström（RN）黑洞的热力学拓扑类，发现电荷和空腔边界而非时空维度决定了精细拓扑分类：中性黑洞属于$W^{0-}$类，带电黑洞属于$W^{1+}$类；当腔半径趋于无穷时，分类反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究黑洞热力学拓扑类（thermodynamic topological class）如何依赖于边界条件（空腔）和电荷，并检验时空维度对分类的影响。

Method: 从约化欧几里得作用量（reduced Euclidean action）出发，利用准局部能量（quasilocal energy）、熵（entropy）和壳上逆温（on-shell inverse temperature）构建离壳矢量场（off-shell vector field），通过该矢量场的拓扑性质对系统进行分类。

Result: 有限空腔下存在两类依赖电荷的拓扑类：中性黑洞为$W^{0-}$，带电黑洞为$W^{1+}$。当腔半径趋于无穷时，中性变为$W^{1-}$，带电变为$W^{0+}$。在四维和五维示例中，时空维度不改变分类结果。

Conclusion: 在RN空腔体系中，电荷和外边界是决定精细拓扑类的关键因素，而非时空维度。

Abstract: We study thermodynamic topological classes of $d$-dimensional Reissner--Nordström (RN) black holes in a cavity at fixed charge. Starting from the reduced Euclidean action, we use the quasilocal energy, entropy, and on-shell inverse temperature to construct the off-shell vector field. A finite cavity gives two charge dependent classes: neutral black holes belong to $W^{0-}$, whereas charged black holes belong to $W^{1+}$. If the cavity radius is sent to infinity at fixed physical charge, the endpoint data change, giving $W^{1-}$ for the neutral case and $W^{0+}$ for the charged case. Thus the electric charge and the outer boundary, rather than the spacetime dimension in the explicit four- and five-dimensional examples, determine the refined topological class within this RN cavity family.

### [25] [Beyond the equation of state: a second-order diagnostic for dynamical dark energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27356)
*Bob Osano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过将暗能量密度演化方程从一阶推广到二阶，显式引入状态方程参数对e-fold时间的导数（ω'_DE），构建曲率诊断量（curvature diagnostic）C=ρ_DE''/ρ_DE，从而在不依赖相互作用强度的情况下直接探测动力学暗能量（dynamical dark energy），并能有效区分相互作用强度与动力学效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一阶连续性方程（first-order continuity equations）仅依赖于暗能量状态方程参数（dark-energy equation-of-state parameter）的瞬时值，无法显式体现状态方程的演化信息。因此需要更高阶的描述来直接捕捉暗能量动力学行为。

Method: 将能量密度的一阶演化方程对e-fold时间求导，显式引入ω'_DE项，从而获得二阶描述。对于具有线性耦合Q_AB=αρ_AH的双流体相互作用暗区模型（two-fluid interacting dark-sector model），定义曲率诊断量C=ρ_DE''/ρ_DE。在宇宙学常数极限下，该诊断量的主导贡献为α²，而偏离ω_DE=-1时则通过δω=1+ω_DE和特征项-3ω'_DE产生修正。

Result: 在与DESI约束一致的CPL参数模型上应用该诊断量，可在完整红移范围内恢复ω'_DE，且无论强耦合还是弱耦合情形均有效。噪声传播分析表明，当σ_H/H≲1.5%时，诊断量的信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）超过3；当α≲0.1时，α与ω'_DE之间的简并性（degeneracy）可以忽略。

Conclusion: 二阶形式化方法提供了互补性的描述，使得状态方程的局域演化通过密度轨迹的曲率直接呈现。在非相互作用极限下，该方法自然恢复Caldwell–Linder的thawing/freezing分类，并将其推广到相互作用暗能量模型。

Abstract: The first-order continuity equations determine the evolution of the energy densities but depend only on the instantaneous value of the dark-energy equation-of-state parameter. Differentiating these equations with respect to e-fold time introduces the term $ω'_{\rm DE}$ explicitly, providing a second-order probe of dark-energy dynamics. Consequently, while information about the evolution of the equation of state is encoded in the full dynamical solution, it is not explicit in the first-order continuity equations evaluated at a given epoch. The second-order formulation, therefore, provides a complementary description in which the local evolution of the equation of state appears directly through the curvature of the density trajectory.
  For a two-fluid interacting dark-sector model with linear coupling $Q_{AB}=αρ_AH$, the resulting second-order equation defines a curvature diagnostic, $\mathcal{C}=ρ_{DE}''/ρ_{DE}$, whose leading contribution, in the cosmological-constant limit, is $α^2$, while departures from $ω_{DE}=-1$ generate corrections through both $δω=1+ω_{DE}$ and the distinctive term $-3ω_{DE}'$. Unlike first-order analyses, this contribution is independent of the interaction strength and directly identifies dynamical dark energy. Applying the diagnostic to a CPL model with parameters consistent with DESI constraints, we recover $ω_{DE}'$ across the full redshift range for both weak and strong interactions. Noise propagation shows that the diagnostic is detectable with signal-to-noise ratio exceeding three for $σ_H/H\lesssim1.5\%$, while the degeneracy between $α$ and $ω_{DE}'$ remains negligible for $α\lesssim0.1$. In the non-interacting limit, the formalism naturally recovers the Caldwell--Linder thawing/freezing classification and extends it to interacting dark-energy models.

</details>

### [26] [Defect-Width-Tunable Resonant Elastic-Wave Transmission in Micro-Pillar Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22264)
*Alok Pokharel*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过有限元模拟，数值研究了在硅基底上沉积的周期性钨微柱阵列中，通过缺陷工程（defect engineering）调控弹性波谐振透射（resonant transmission）的机制。研究发现缺陷宽度显著影响透射调制，并伴随局域谐振弹性波再分布；Floquet色散分析揭示多个近平坦谐振分支对应低群速度（low-group-velocity）的亚波长局域谐振模式。相比铜，钨由于与基底间更大的惯性对比（inertial contrast）增强了谐振约束。该缺陷工程微柱晶格为实现弹性超材料中的频率选择性弹性波控制与局域谐振波操控提供了有效途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 周期性微柱晶格集成于弹性基底上，为通过局域谐振相互作用控制弹性波传播提供了有前景的平台。本研究旨在通过缺陷工程，探索在周期性钨微柱阵列中实现弹性波谐振透射的调控机制。

Method: 采用有限元模拟（finite-element simulations）进行二维频域分析，分别评估一柱、两柱和三柱缺陷对弹性波透射特性的影响；并使用全三维模拟确认缺陷敏感的谐振局域化与弹性波传输路径的改变；通过周期性单胞的Floquet色散分析（Floquet dispersion analysis）揭示谐振分支特性。

Result: 发现缺陷宽度显著影响透射调制，并在周期性晶格内出现局域谐振弹性波再分布；Floquet色散分析显示多个近平坦谐振分支，对应低群速度的亚波长局域谐振模式；钨相较于铜具有更强的谐振约束，归因于其与基底间更大的惯性对比。

Conclusion: 所提出的缺陷工程微柱晶格为弹性超材料（elastic metamaterials）系统中的频率选择性弹性波控制与局域谐振波操控提供了有效方法。

Abstract: Periodic micro-pillar lattices integrated on elastic substrates provide a promising plat-form for controlling elastic-wave propagation through localized resonant interactions. In this work, defect-engineered resonant transmission in periodic tungsten micro-pillar arrays deposited on silicon substrates is numerically investigated using finite-element simulations. Two-dimensional frequency-domain analyses were performed to evaluate the influence of one-, two- and three-pillar defects on elastic wave transmission characteristics. The results reveal strong defect-width-dependent transmission modulation together with the localized resonant elastic-wave redistribution within the periodic lattice. Full three-dimensional simulations further confirm the presence of defect-sensitive resonant localization and modified elastic-wave transport pathways. Floquet dispersion analysis of a periodic unit cell reveals multiple nearly flat resonant branches associated with low-group-velocity elastic-wave modes, indicating predominantly subwavelength locally resonant behavior. A comparative study between tungsten and copper resonators demonstrates enhanced resonant confinement in tung-sten-based structures due to their larger inertial contrast with the supporting sub-strate. The proposed defect-engineered micro-pillar lattices provide an effective approach for frequency-selective elastic-wave control and localized resonant wave ma-nipulation in elastic metamaterial systems.

### [27] [Algebraic structures of the Lindblad equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26477)
*Leonel Bixano,Guillermo López-Alvarez,Victor Alberto Cruz-Barriguete,V. G. Ibarra-Sierra,José Luis Cardoso,Juan Carlos Sandoval-Santana,Alejandro Kunold*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了有限维开放量子系统中Lindblad方程（Lindblad equation）背后的封闭代数结构（closed algebra of Hermitian operators），该结构独立于具体物理模型，能够统一描述耗散动力学（dissipative dynamics）并显著降低Liouville超算符（Liouville superoperator）的构建计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放量子系统的耗散动力学比纯幺正演化（unitary evolution）具有更丰富的代数结构，但现有方法缺乏对此结构的统一数学刻画，且直接构建Liouville超算符的计算代价较高。

Method: 引入Liouville超算符的算符表示（operator representation），将动力学表述为依赖于厄米算符（Hermitian operators）的封闭代数；推导了适用于维数递增系统的递归关系（recursion relations）；所有模型相关信息仅通过一组系数进入框架，从而实现代数基（algebraic basis）的通用性。

Result: 该代数框架自然导出了动力学映射（dynamical map）的参数化形式及其演化的微分方程；递归关系支持高效构建高维系统代数；通过一个单量子比特（one-qubit）的Mathematica示例验证了方法的可扩展性。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架既为有限维Lindblad动力学（finite-dimensional Lindblad dynamics）提供了通用的数学描述，也为高效的解析与数值实现奠定了实用基础。

Abstract: We investigate the algebraic structure underlying the Lindblad equation for finite-dimensional open quantum systems. By introducing a suitable operator representation of the Liouville superoperator, we show that the dynamics can be formulated in terms of a closed algebra of Hermitian operators that is independent of the particular physical model. This formulation reveals that dissipative dynamics requires a substantially richer algebraic structure than purely unitary evolution, thereby providing a clear characterization of the additional complexity introduced by the Lindbladian. The resulting framework naturally leads to parametrizations of the dynamical map and to differential equations governing its evolution. We further derive recursion relations that enable the efficient construction of the algebra for systems of increasing dimension. Because the algebraic basis is universal, while all model-dependent information enters through a single set of coefficients, the proposed approach significantly reduces the computational cost of constructing the Liouville superoperator compared with direct methods. To facilitate the implementation of the method, we provide a Mathematica notebook containing a one-qubit example that can be systematically extended to an arbitrary number of qubits. The proposed framework therefore provides both a general mathematical description of finite-dimensional Lindblad dynamics and a practical foundation for efficient analytical and numerical implementations.

</details>


### [28] [A fidelity metric for quantum annealing benchmarked by extreme scaling quantum Monte-Carlo simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26233)
*Gabriel Gouraud,Miha Srdinsek,Xavier Waintal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种衡量量子退火（quantum annealing）过程质量的精度度量 ε（类似于基于门的量子计算机中的每门保真度），并通过两种模拟量子退火方法对里德伯原子（Rydberg atoms）系统进行基准计算，结果表明在高达一亿原子的规模上可达到 ε∼10⁻²–10⁻³ 的精度，远优于当前实验平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子退火器的性能评估过分依赖优化问题的求解结果和经典基准算法，这种“以结果论英雄”的方法具有脆性（brittle），缺乏对退火过程本身质量的衡量指标。

Method: 定义量子退火精度的度量 ε，作为退火器状态方程（equation of state）的精度指标；利用两种模拟量子退火技术——基于变分量子蒙特卡洛（variational quantum Monte-Carlo，受热退火启发）和基于格林函数量子蒙特卡洛（Green function quantum Monte-Carlo）——对里德伯原子系统进行基准计算。

Result: 变分量子蒙特卡洛方法在单CPU上可处理高达一亿个原子，精度达 ε∼10⁻²–10⁻³；格林函数量子蒙特卡洛方法可处理十万个原子，精度达 ε∼10⁻⁴。两种方法在精度和规模上均比当前里德伯原子量子退火实验平台高出数个数量级。

Conclusion: 所提出的精度度量 ε 为量子退火过程质量提供了独立于具体优化问题的衡量标准；基准结果表明经典模拟方法在规模和精度上远超现有实验硬件，为未来量子退火硬件的发展设定了严格约束。

Abstract: Quantum annealers are supposed to follow adiabatically the ground state of a system as its Hamiltonian slowly interpolates between a trivial phase and a non-trivial one; the non-trivial ground state being the solution to an optimization problem. Overwhelmingly, their performances are measured in terms of how well or fast the optimization problem is solved. While pragmatic, this approach is inherently brittle as it strongly depends on the problem considered and the classical algorithm used as the reference benchmark. Here, we propose a quantity that not only measures the end result but also the quality of the actual quantum annealing process itself. Our metric is the quantum annealing counterpart of the fidelity-per gate of gate-based quantum computers. It takes the form of an accuracy $ε$ for the equation of state of the annealer. We calculate benchmark values of $ε$ using two variants of the simulated quantum annealing technique for Rydberg atoms systems. Our first approach uses variational quantum Monte-Carlo with an ansatz inspired by thermal annealing. It suggests that within $ε\sim 10^{-2}-10^{-3}$, a quantum annealer is indistinguishable from its thermal classical counterpart. Critically, we could reach this precision up to $100,000,000$ atoms on a single CPU. Our second approach (based on Green function quantum Monte-Carlo) reaches accuracies around $ε\sim 10^{-4}$ and we have run it up to $100,000$ atoms. These results outperform current Rydberg atom quantum annealing experimental platforms in both precision and size by orders of magnitude and put severe constraints for future hardware.

</details>


### [29] [Measures of Chirality in Mixed-State Topological Phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26235)
*Shijun Sun,Bader Aldossari,Rasmit Devkota,Zhu-Xi Luo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出，在混合态拓扑相中，传统用于纯态拓扑相的手性诊断（如体边对应、能隙纠缠谱、模交换子及热霍尔响应）均失效；为此，作者针对已知无错父态的退相干拓扑相，提出了两种基于相对熵（relative entropy）的度量来诊断手性，并进一步通过其中一种度量提取手性中心荷（chiral central charge）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合态拓扑相是否具有手性（chirality）这一基本问题在数学上可以通过对称代数（symmetry algebra）刻画，但在物理上缺乏清晰且可靠的定义与诊断工具。

Method: 针对具有已知无错父态（error-free parent state）的退相干拓扑相，提出两种基于相对熵（relative entropy）的度量，用于诊断混合态的手性，其中一种度量可进一步提取手性中心荷（chiral central charge）。

Result: 在纯态中用于指示拓扑手性的经典诊断——体边对应（bulk-boundary correspondence）、能隙纠缠谱（gapless entanglement spectrum）、非平凡模交换子（modular commutator）以及量子化热霍尔响应（quantized thermal Hall response）——在混合态中均不再可靠。

Conclusion: 混合态拓扑学需要本质上的新诊断手段，不能仅仅依赖纯态探针的直接类比。

Abstract: What does it mean for a mixed-state topological phase to be chiral? Mathematically, chirality can be sharply characterized through the symmetry algebra of the mixed state. Physically, however, the question is far more subtle. In pure states, chirality in topological phase is tied to a web of familiar diagnostics, involving bulk-boundary correspondence, a gapless entanglement spectrum, a nontrivial modular commutator, and a quantized thermal Hall response. We show that none of these diagnostics remain reliable in mixed states. Instead, for decohered topological phases with a known error-free parent state, we propose two relative-entropy-based measures that can diagnose chirality, with one of them further extracting the chiral central charge. Our results emphasize how mixed-state topology demands intrinsically new diagnostics beyond direct analogues of pure-state probes.

### [30] [Optimal observables for quantum-enhanced sensing and applications in a Floquet time crystal sensor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26248)
*M. A. Manya,Andrei Tsypilnikov,Fernando Iemini*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了如何确定并实现可行的最优观测量，以在矩估计法（MoM）中饱和量子Fisher信息（QFI）界。研究发现，对称对数导数（SLD）算符虽能饱和QFI界，但过于复杂且非局域化，难以直接实验实现。针对Floquet时间晶体（FTC）交流场传感器这一模型，研究者展示了SLD可被简化为磁化强度或宇称观测量的近似替代。核磁共振实验模拟进一步验证了理论预测，为FTC传感器实现近最优计量学提供了一条实用路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子计量学中，饱和量子Fisher信息（QFI）界需要实现最优观测量，但理论最优的对称对数导数（SLD）算符通常过于复杂且非局域化，难以在实验中直接实现。因此，寻找可实验实现的近似替代方案是推动量子增强计量学走向实际应用的关键。

Method: 论文首先证明对称对数导数（SLD）算符在矩估计法（MoM）中可以饱和QFI界，随后以Floquet时间晶体（FTC）交流场传感器为具体模型，分析SLD的数学结构，发现其可被简化为诸如裸自旋磁化强度或宇称观测量等更简单的可观测算符。最后在核磁共振系统中采用实验参数进行模拟，验证理论预测的有效性。

Result: 研究表明，在不同初始态制备条件下，FTC传感器中原本不可实现的SLD算符可以被显著简化的观测量（如自旋磁化强度或宇称观测量）有效近似。基于实验参数的核磁共振系统模拟结果进一步支持了理论分析，表明这些简化观测量仍能保持量子增强的灵敏度。

Conclusion: 该工作为FTC传感器提供了一条实用路径：通过用更简单的可观测算符替代不可实现的SLD，同时保留量子增强灵敏度，从而实现近最优量子计量学（near-optimal metrology）。

Abstract: In this work, we discuss how to determine and implement feasible optimal observables for a metrology protocol that saturates the quantum Fisher information (QFI) bound. In particular, we focus our study on a simple protocol, namely the method of moments (MoM). We first demonstrate that the symmetric logarithmic derivative (SLD) operator, a Hermitian observable, once implemented in the MoM, saturates the QFI bound. However, the SLD is generally too complex and typically non-local, rendering its direct experimental realization unfeasible. To overcome this limitation, we explore its structure in a specific sensing model - a Floquet time crystal (FTC) acting as an ac field sensor - and show that the SLD can be approximated by substantially simpler observables, such as the bare spin magnetization or a parity observable, for different relevant initial state preparations. We further corroborate our theoretical predictions in a nuclear magnetic resonance system operating as an FTC sensor, employing experimentally motivated parameters to simulate its performance in a state-of-the-art implementation. In general, our results establish a practical route toward near-optimal metrology in FTC sensors, where the inaccessible SLD operator can be replaced by simpler observables while retaining quantum-enhanced sensitivity.

Abstract: We present a comprehensive study of quadrature squeezing in a quantum well laser based on a fully quantum Langevin approach. We further analyse the role of the linewidth enhancement factor (alpha factor) in the emergence of these features. Our results establish semiconductor lasers as a platform for the generation of non-classical light and open new perspectives for their application in quantum communication and sensing.

*Yanyan He,Tomoki Ozawa*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了非厄米布洛赫振荡的通用理论框架，推导了动量、质心及群速度的运动方程，识别了非厄米性导致的异常群速度，揭示了非互易非光滑布洛赫振荡和周期性时间古斯-汉欣位移等新现象。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现非厄米性会导致异常群速度（anomalous group velocity）的出现；在非厄米晶格中可产生非互易非光滑布洛赫振荡（nonreciprocal non-smooth Bloch oscillations），其特点是群速度出现周期性跳跃；在具有单向跃迁和开边界的体系中，进一步发现了周期性时间古斯-汉欣位移（temporal Goos–Hänchen shifts）以及沿跃迁消失方向的异常波传播（anomalous wave propagation）。

Conclusion: 非厄米性显著改变了布洛赫振荡的动力学行为，产生了一系列在厄米体系中不存在的独特现象，为理解和操控非厄米晶格中的量子输运提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We establish a general framework for non-Hermitian Bloch oscillations by investigating the wave-packet dynamics in one-dimensional non-Hermitian lattices driven by a dc force. The equations of motion for the momentum, center of mass, and group velocity of a wave packet are derived, where an anomalous group velocity due to the non-Hermiticity is identified. We show that nonreciprocal non-smooth Bloch oscillations, characterized by periodic jumps in group velocity, can emerge, and we analyze the role of finite-size effects. In non-Hermitian lattices with unidirectional hopping under open boundary conditions, we further uncover the emergence of periodic temporal Goos--Hänchen shifts together with an anomalous wave propagation along the direction of vanishing hopping.

### [33] [Dissipation-Induced Deviations from Kibble-Zurek Scaling in Non-Hermitian Quantum Annealing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26870)
*H. Najafzadeh,S. Sadeghizade,R. Jafari,A. Langari*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视非厄米横场伊辛模型中的量子退火问题，通过解析和数值方法确定了内在跃迁概率及缺陷密度。研究发现，与厄米情况不同，非厄米动力学的缺陷产生涉及广阔动量区间的显著贡献。缺陷密度随耗散强度变化，分别呈现标准的Kibble-Zurek标度律、反Kibble-Zurek行为以及比Kibble-Zurek预测更快的抑制机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子退火研究多聚焦于厄米系统（Hermitian systems），而实际物理系统中普遍存在的非厄米性（non-Hermiticity）及其对退火动力学的影响尚未被充分理解。本文旨在揭示非厄米横场伊辛模型中缺陷产生的内在机制，填补该领域理论空白。

Method: 采用解析分析与数值模拟相结合的方法，求解非厄米横场伊辛模型（non-Hermitian transverse-field Ising model）中的内在跃迁概率（intrinsic transition probabilities）并计算缺陷密度（defect density）。通过对比不同耗散强度下的标度行为，分类讨论偏离标准Kibble-Zurek标度律（Kibble-Zurek scaling）的三种情形。

Result: 缺陷密度随耗散强度的变化呈现三种特征：标准的Kibble-Zurek标度、反Kibble-Zurek行为（anti-Kibble-Zurek behavior），以及比Kibble-Zurek预测更快的抑制。非厄米系统中广阔动量区间的模式均对缺陷产生有显著贡献，而非仅限于能隙闭合点（gap-closing point）附近的模式。

Conclusion: 缺陷密度的快速衰减源于一种在广泛退火时间范围内、对所有允许模式均消失的激发概率，即使能隙闭合点处亦然；而反Kibble-Zurek行为则归因于耗散在广阔模式区间（尤其是远离能隙闭合区的模式）所导致的额外激发。这些结果拓展了对非厄米量子退火动力学的理解。

Abstract: We revisit the quantum annealing problem in the non-Hermitian transverse-field Ising model. We determine, both analytically and numerically, the intrinsic transition probabilities and the resulting defect density. Our results reveal that, unlike the Hermitian case where defect production is dominated by modes near the gap-closing point, the non-Hermitian dynamics involve significant contributions from broad momentum sectors. We find that, depending on the dissipation strength, the defect density exhibits standard Kibble-Zurek scaling, anti-Kibble-Zurek behavior, and a suppression faster than the Kibble-Zurek prediction. We demonstrate that these deviations from the standard Kibble-Zurek scaling can be understood in terms of the underlying excitation probabilities. Specifically, the fast decay of the defect density originates from a vanishing excitation probability spanning a range of annealing times across all allowed modes, even at the gap-closing points. In contrast, the anti-Kibble-Zurek behavior arises from supplementary excitations facilitated by dissipation over a broad range of allowed modes, particularly those situated away from the gap-closing region.

### [34] [From Approximate Floquet Engineering to Full Floquet Theory: Coherent Control of Chiral Spin Systems in Spintronics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27183)
*Andrea Simion,Claudiu Filip,Coriolan Tiusan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文展示了从核磁共振（NMR）方法改编的全 Floquet 空间形式体系，用于在静态磁场 B0 和横向振荡场 B1 下建模驱动耦合电子自旋的动力学，系统验证了该框架在包含同位旋交换耦合（exchange coupling）J 和手性 Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya 反对称交换相互作用（DMI）情况下的数值收敛性与预测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在时间周期驱动下对相互作用自旋系统进行相干控制，是基于自旋的量子技术中的核心挑战；现有方法在超越简单相干旋转区域时的建模能力有限，亟需一种稳健且预测性的理论框架。

Method: 采用全 Floquet 空间形式体系（full Floquet-space formalism），该体系改编自核磁共振（Nuclear Magnetic Resonance, NMR）方法；显式包含各向同性交换耦合（isotropic exchange coupling）J 和手性 Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya 反对称交换相互作用（DMI）；系统验证了傅里叶空间截断（Fourier-space truncation）下的数值收敛性。

Result: 在非相互作用极限下，恢复由 B1 决定周期性的预期驱动自旋动力学；仅交换耦合不改变集体自旋期望值；DMI 增大产生非零 Sy 期望值、抑制 Sz 期望值，并产生倾斜椭圆 Bloch 球轨迹；开放边界条件下效果显著，周期边界条件下可忽略；当交换耦合与 DMI 共存时，动力学出现强扰动和多频特征。

Conclusion: 全 Floquet 空间建模为分析和工程化驱动相互作用自旋系统中的相干动力学提供了一个稳健且预测性的框架，可超越简单的相干旋转区域（coherent-rotation regimes）。

Abstract: Coherent control of interacting spin systems under time-periodic driving is a central challenge in spin-based quantum technologies. Here we demonstrate the applicability of a full Floquet-space formalism, adapted from Nuclear Magnetic Resonance (NMR) methodologies, to model the dynamics of driven coupled electron spins in the presence of a static magnetic field B0 and a transverse oscillating field B1. The framework explicitly includes isotropic exchange coupling J and the chiral Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya antisymmetric exchange interaction (DMI), and its numerical convergence is systematically validated with respect to Fourier-space truncation. In the non-interacting limit, the expected driven-spin dynamics is recovered, with the oscillation periodicity governed by B1. Exchange coupling alone does not modify the collective spin expectation values under the chosen initial condition, consistent with symmetry considerations. In contrast, increasing DMI generates a finite expectation value of Sy, suppresses the expectation value of Sz, and produces tilted, elliptical Bloch-sphere trajectories, reflecting the emergence of chiral spin-spin correlations. These effects are pronounced for open boundary conditions, while remaining nearly negligible in the periodic boundary case. When exchange coupling and DMI coexist, the dynamics becomes strongly perturbed and multi-frequency in nature. Together, these results demonstrate that full Floquet-space modeling provides a robust and predictive framework for analyzing and engineering coherent dynamics in driven interacting spin systems beyond simple coherent-rotation regimes.

### [35] [Quantum computer architecture with ions in tweezer arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27249)
*Benjamin F. Schiffer,Christopher Monroe,Peter Zoller,J. Ignacio Cirac*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于光镊阵列（optical tweezer arrays）中束缚离子的量子计算机架构，通过将离子输运至局部相互作用区并激发至辅助态以产生有效电偶极矩（effective electric dipole），利用库仑相互作用实现纠缠门（entangling gate）。该机制可实现质心与相对运动轨迹的精确、温度鲁棒性闭合，消除量子比特与运动之间的残余纠缠。基于钡离子（barium ions）给出了具体实现方案，并分析了并行门操作中的串扰抑制，为可扩展离子-光镊量子处理器提供了现实路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有离子阱（trapped-ion）量子计算平台虽具有长相干时间（coherence time），但在可重构性与并行操作方面受限。光镊阵列（optical tweezer arrays）提供了可重构性与并行操作能力，但尚未充分结合离子阱的长相干时间优势。本文旨在将两者结合，提出一种可扩展且温度鲁棒的量子计算架构。

Method: 离子被束缚在光镊阵列中，可被输运至局部相互作用区（interaction zone）；通过激发至与位移光学势（displaced optical potential）相对应的辅助态，产生可控有效电偶极矩。利用这些有效偶极子之间的库仑相互作用（Coulomb interaction）实现纠缠门机制，并对质心运动与相对运动轨迹进行精确控制。

Result: 该纠缠门机制能够实现质心与相对运动轨迹的精确、温度鲁棒性（temperature-robust）闭合，消除量子比特与运动模式之间的残余纠缠。基于钡离子的态选择性极化率（state-selective polarizability）给出了具体实现方案，并研究了并行门执行中串扰（cross-talk）的抑制方法，对量子纠错中的横向门（transversal gates）具有相关性。

Conclusion: 该研究为构建可扩展的离子-光镊量子处理器（ion-tweezer quantum processors）提供了现实可行的技术路线。

Abstract: We propose a quantum computer architecture based on ions confined in optical tweezer arrays, combining the long coherence times of trapped-ion qubits with the reconfigurability and parallel operation enabled by tweezer platforms. Selected ions are transported to local interaction zones, where excitation to an auxiliary state with a displaced optical potential generates a controllable effective electric dipole. We develop and analyze entangling-gate mechanisms mediated by the Coulomb interaction between such effective dipoles, and show that they enable precise, temperature-robust closure of the center-of-mass and relative motional trajectories, leaving no residual entanglement between the qubits and the motion. We further outline a concrete implementation with barium ions based on state-selective polarizability, and study the suppression of cross-talk during parallel gate execution, with relevance to transversal gates in quantum error correction. Our results thereby establish a realistic route toward scalable ion-tweezer quantum processors.

### [36] [Exploring dynamics of individual vortices in a superconductor via a levitated magnetic transducer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27297)
