TL;DR: 本文利用微米级悬浮磁性粒子的机械运动探测超导体中单个涡旋（vortex）的动力学，观测到随机电报信号（random telegraph signals）和非指数衰减（non-exponential decay），揭示了涡旋-缺陷相互作用的复杂势能景观（potential landscape），为理解超导悬浮系统中的耗散机制提供了新见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 束缚涡旋（trapped vortices）决定了超导体的基本性质，并在磁悬浮等实际应用中发挥重要作用，但其复杂的动力学机制仍未被充分理解。

Method: 利用微米级悬浮磁性粒子的机械运动作为探针，测量YBCO超导薄膜中单个涡旋的动力学行为，分析机械频率、耗散率（dissipation rate）和能量中的随机电报信号，并通过ringdown测量（ringdown measurement）研究非线性衰减特征。

Result: 观测到悬浮粒子的机械频率、耗散率和能量中呈现随机电报信号，归因于单个涡旋的随机隧穿（random tunneling）；ringdown测量中观察到非指数衰减，表明涡旋-缺陷相互作用具有非线性特征，揭示了复杂的底层势能景观。

Conclusion: 研究结果为超导悬浮系统中难以捉摸的耗散机制提供了新见解，开辟了利用悬浮磁体作为灵敏探针研究超导体中单个涡旋的静态与动态性质及其与材料无序相互作用的新途径，并指向利用磁性粒子作为高相干机械换能器（mechanical transducer）的新方向。

Abstract: Trapped vortices determine fundamental properties of superconductors and play an important role in many practical applications such as magnetic levitation, however their complex dynamics remain poorly understood. Here, we use the mechanical motion of micron-scale levitated magnetic particles to probe the dynamics of individual vortices. Specifically, we show that the dynamics of levitated magnets are strongly influenced by vortices trapped in the YBCO superconducting film. We observe random telegraph signals in the mechanical frequency, dissipation rate, and energy of levitated particles, which we attribute to random tunneling of individual vortices. The nonlinearity of vortex-defect interaction manifests as non-exponential decay in ringdown measurements, revealing a complex underlying potential landscape. Our results provide insights into elusive dissipation mechanisms in superconducting levitated systems, open new avenues for using levitated magnets as sensitive probes of static and dynamic properties of individual vortices in superconductors and their interactions with material disorder, and point toward novel routes for using magnetic particles as highly coherent mechanical transducers.

</details>

### [38] [HALO II: Constraining Hubble constant $H_{0}$ through continuum delay fitting of Fairall 9](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27195)
*Amit Kumar Mandal,Francisco Pozo Nuñez,Vikram Kumar Jaiswal,Mohammad Hassan Naddaf,Bożena Czerny,Swayamtrupta Panda,Paulina Karczmarek,Grzegorz Pietrzyński,Shivangi Pandey,R. Edelson,B. M. Peterson,Michal Zajaček,Alberto Floris,Mary Loli Martínez-Aldama,Michal Dovčiak,Vladimir Karas,Weronika Narloch,Mirosław Kicia,Marek Górski,Mikołaj Kałuszyński,Gergely Hajdu,Piotr Wielgórski,Bartłomiej Zgirski,Cezary Gałan,Wojciech Pych,Radosław Smolec,Ricardo Salinas,Henryka Netzel-Iłkiewicz,Karolina Bąkowska,Wolfgang Gieren,Pierre Kervella*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 摘要提出一种基于活动星系核（AGN）连续谱时延与能谱分布（SED）建模的全新独立方法测定哈勃常数$H_0$。通过对Seyfert星系Fairall 9的监测与{\tt H0RIZON-AGN}模型分析，获得$H_0=72.4_{-3.7}^{+3.4} \, \rm km \, s^{-1} \, Mpc^{-1}$，精度约5%。该方法完全独立于宇宙距离阶梯，有望在未来将误差降至1%以下，为解决哈勃张力（Hubble tension）提供独立探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 哈勃张力（Hubble tension）是现代宇宙学中最显著且尚未解决的关键问题之一。一个重要疑问是它是否源于不同测量技术中被低估的系统不确定性（systematic uncertainties），因此亟需发展全新的独立测定方法。

Method: 该方法基于活动星系核（active galactic nuclei, AGN）的连续谱时延（continuum time delay）与能谱分布（spectral energy distribution, SED）建模，完全独立于宇宙距离阶梯（cosmic distance ladder），无需与其他距离指示器进行交叉校准。研究团队对Seyfert星系Fairall 9开展了专项监测，并进一步开发了{\tt H0RIZON-AGN}模型，该模型考虑了周围冷吸积盘（cold accretion disk）中辐射再处理（radiation reprocessing）效应，对观测到的连续谱延迟进行更真实的描述。

Result: 通过对Fairall 9的连续谱滞后谱（lag-spectrum）与宽带SED的联合建模，测得哈勃常数$H_{0}=72.4_{-3.7}^{+3.4} \, \rm km \, s^{-1} \, Mpc^{-1}$，测量精度约5%。该结果在当前不确定性范围内与早期宇宙和晚期宇宙的测量值基本一致。

Conclusion: 仅凭单一源即实现约5%的测量精度，表明该方法在独立测定哈勃常数方面具有显著潜力。未来将该方法应用于更大规模数据集（特别是Vera Rubin天文台提供的观测数据），有望将不确定性降至1%以下，从而将这一方法确立为解决哈勃张力的强有力独立探针。

Abstract: The Hubble tension remains one of the most significant unresolved problems in modern cosmology. A key question is whether it may arise from underestimated systematic uncertainties in the different measurement techniques. In this context, new independent methods are of exceptional importance. We therefore pursue a novel approach to determining the Hubble constant, $H_{0}$ based on continuum time delay and spectral energy distribution (SED) modeling in active galactic nuclei (AGNs). Unlike conventional techniques, this method is entirely independent of the cosmic distance ladder and does not require cross-calibration against other distance indicators. As a result, it enables a direct determination of $H_{0}$, free from the arbitrary normalizations that often affect indirect measurements. We conducted a dedicated monitoring campaign of the Seyfert galaxy Fairall 9 and further developed the {\tt H0RIZON-AGN} model to interpret the resulting observations. The model incorporates the effects of radiation reprocessing in the surrounding cold accretion disk, enabling a more realistic description of the observed continuum delays. Through the simultaneous modeling of the continuum lag-spectrum and the broadband SED of Fairall 9, we derived a Hubble constant of $H_{0}=72.4_{-3.7}^{+3.4} \, \rm km \, s^{-1} \, Mpc^{-1}$. Achieving a measurement precision of approximately 5% from a single source demonstrates the considerable potential of this method for independent determinations of the Hubble constant. Our determination of $H_{0}$ is broadly consistent, within the current uncertainties, with both early- and late-Universe measurements. Future applications of the method to larger datasets, particularly those provided by the Vera Rubin Observatory, are expected to reduce the uncertainty to below 1%, thereby establishing this approach as a powerful independent probe of the Hubble tension.

Conclusion: 当前观测能力尚不足以探测SGWB运动学偶极子，因此需要发展新的观测和分析策略以充分利用该信号。

Abstract: Pulsar Timing Arrays (PTAs) and astrometric surveys provide complementary probes of the nanohertz stochastic gravitational-wave background (SGWB). A primary target is the kinematic dipole induced by the Solar System's motion, whose detection would confirm the SGWB's cosmological origin. We forecast the sensitivity of the Square Kilometre Array Observatory (SKAO) using optimal estimators and Fisher techniques, considering both the baseline AA4 configuration and an optimistic 1000 pulsar scenario, including the potential gain from combining with Gaia-like astrometry. While SKAO will substantially improve constraints on SGWB anisotropies, even joint analyses remain below the sensitivity required to detect the kinematic dipole, motivating new observational and analysis strategies to fully exploit this signal.

### [40] [Lyman-Alpha Forest and its Cross-Correlation with High-Redshift Galaxies in Effective Field Theory at the Field Level](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26234)
*Roger de Belsunce,Mikhail M. Ivanov,James M. Sullivan,Shi-Fan Chen,Kazuyuki Akitsu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于场级微扰理论的莱曼α森林流量衰减前向模型，在多种模拟数据上验证了其高精度，并利用宇宙方差抵消（cosmic variance cancellation）实现了对莱曼α森林偏置参数和二次视线方向偏置算子的精确测量，还为DESI和DESI-II提供了大规模结构模拟样本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莱曼α森林（Lyman-alpha forest）作为宇宙大尺度结构的重要探针，其精确建模对于从DESI、DESI-II等巡天数据中提取宇宙学信息至关重要。现有现象学模型在场级（field-level）存在精度不足的问题，亟需发展基于第一性原理的微扰前向模型。

Method: 提出了一种场级微扰前向模型（field-level perturbative forward model），在AbacusSummit N体模拟（利用暗物质场绘制莱曼α森林）和Sherwood流体动力学模拟两套模拟数据上进行验证，覆盖红移范围z=2.0–3.2。

Result: 三维和一维功率谱在k ≤ 0.3 h/Mpc（1.0 h/Mpc）范围内与模拟莱曼α场的一致程度达到1%（5%），与暗物质晕的交叉相关性能类似；计数统计（counts-in-cells）在2 Mpc/h的网格半径下吻合极佳。模型成功检测到完整的二次视线方向（line-of-sight）偏置算子集合，符合有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）的自然性（naturalness）概念，并发现莱曼α森林的大尺度随机性（stochasticity）是白噪声形式（白谱，scale- and orientation-independent）。

Conclusion: 该模型为DESI的莱曼α森林聚类模拟提供了高精度的大规模结构模拟样本，可用于验证宇宙学参数推断流程；同时为DESI-II生成校准于Astrid流体动力学模拟且与z=3观测数据匹配的莱曼断裂星系（Lyman-break galaxies, LBGs）和莱曼α发射体（Lya emitters, LAEs）大体积模拟样本，支撑莱曼α森林与高红移星系的联合分析。

Abstract: We present a field-level perturbative forward model for the Lyman-alpha (Lya) forest flux decrement. We validate it on two simulation suites: large-volume AbacusSummit N-body simulations with the Lya forest painted onto the dark matter field, and the Sherwood hydrodynamic simulations. Across the redshift range of the simulations (z=2.0-3.2), the 3D and 1D power spectra of the model match the simulated Lya fields at the 1% (5%) level up to k <= 0.3 (1.0) h/Mpc, with similar performance for the cross-correlation with massive dark matter halos. The counts-in-cells statistic shows excellent agreement down to cell radii of 2 Mpc/h. Leveraging cosmic variance cancellation, the model enables precision measurements of Lya bias parameters and robustly detects the full set of quadratic line-of-sight bias operators, consistent with the notion of naturalness in effective field theory (EFT). We quantify the stochasticity of the Lya forest (the analog to the one-halo term), and find it to be white (scale- and orientation-independent) on large scales, matching EFT predictions. We further find that phenomenological flux power spectrum models, based on modulations of the linear-theory power spectrum, fail at the field level even on quasi-linear scales. For the currently observing Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI), we generate large-scale clustering mocks of the Lya forest to validate cosmological parameter inference pipelines. Looking ahead to its successor, DESI-II, we produce large-volume mocks of representative samples of Lyman-break galaxies (LBGs) and Lya emitters (LAEs), calibrated on Astrid hydrodynamic simulations and matched to observations at z=3, enabling joint analyses of Lya forest and high-redshift galaxy data.

### [41] [A solid unification of the dark sector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27290)
*Jose Beltrán Jiménez,María Pérez Garrote,Florencia A. Teppa Pannia,Shinji Tsujikawa*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种单一暗组分（dark component）的统一描述，该组分在早期宇宙中表现为无压流体，后期发生固相（solid phase）转变以支持加速膨胀，从而统一暗物质（dark matter）与暗能量（dark energy）。广义Chaplygin型固体（generalized Chaplygin-type solid）实现了这一场景，避免了完美流体统一方案中的不稳定性与声学振荡（acoustic oscillations），并在宇宙学扰动（cosmological perturbations）中产生可检验的特征信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有暗物质与暗能量统一模型（如完美流体方案）存在本质不稳定性（instabilities）和强声学振荡问题，难以与观测一致。本文旨在构建一种基于固体介质的统一暗组分模型，以克服上述缺陷，同时维持从暗物质到暗能量的背景演化。

Method: 采用广义Chaplygin型固体作为暗介质的本构模型，通过固相（solid phase）的弹性响应（elastic response）来避免完美流体的不稳定性。利用宇宙学扰动理论分析该模型的标量、矢量和张量扰动（scalar, vector, and tensor perturbations），并与标准ΛCDM模型对比。

Result: 该固体统一模型不会产生完美流体方案中典型的不稳定性与强声学振荡。在扰动层面出现三个特征信号：结构增长（structure growth）受到抑制、非平凡引力滑移（gravitational slip）以及引力波（gravitational waves）获得有效质量。这些效应起源于固相，因此仅在低红移（low redshifts）下显现，高红移宇宙学几乎不受影响。

Conclusion: 固体统一暗组分（solid unified dark sector）能够再现从暗物质到暗能量的预期背景转变，同时在宇宙学扰动中产生可检验的印记，为暗物质与暗能量的统一描述提供了一条无扰动不稳定性且具预测性的途径。

Abstract: We construct a unified description of dark matter and dark energy in terms of a single dark component that behaves as a pressureless fluid in the early Universe and undergoes a transition to a solid phase at late times that can support accelerated expansion. A generalized Chaplygin-type solid provides a simple realization of this scenario. The solid nature of the dark medium prevents the instabilities and strong acoustic oscillations that typically arise in perfect-fluid unifications. It also gives rise to distinctive signatures in cosmological perturbations, such as a suppression of structure growth, a nontrivial gravitational slip, and an effective mass for gravitational waves. Since these effects share a common origin in the solid phase, they become relevant only at low redshifts, leaving the high-redshift cosmology essentially unmodified. This demonstrates that a solidly unified dark sector can reproduce the desired background transition from dark matter to dark energy while yielding testable imprints in cosmological perturbations.

</details>

# physics.flu-dyn [[Back]](#toc)

### [42] [Droplet Fusion as a Relaxation Process: Comparison with Shape Recovery of Newtonian and Viscoelastic Droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26272)
*Mohammad Moein Naderi,Zhangli Peng,Huan-Xiang Zhou*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过理论分析与有限元模拟，系统研究了由相分离形成的生物分子凝聚体（biomolecular condensates）的粘弹性（viscoelasticity）如何调控形状恢复与液滴融合这两个动力学过程。研究表明，两个过程虽均由毛细力驱动，但物理机制根本不同：形状恢复受单一界面的全局粘毛细松弛控制，而融合则是一个多阶段过程。粘弹性引入的额外内禀时间尺度（以Deborah数表征）会显著改变融合动力学，且外部流体的存在会通过流体动力学耗散进一步减慢融合。纯粘性模型不足以描述粘弹性体系中的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由相分离形成的生物分子凝聚体通常表现出粘弹性行为，但现有研究往往使用纯粘性模型（purely viscous models）解释其形状恢复与融合动力学，缺乏对粘弹性作用的系统量化理解。本文旨在建立一个统一的理论与计算框架，定量揭示粘弹性如何支配这两个过程。

Method: 结合小变形形状恢复的解析理论（analytical theory）和基于Oldroyd-B本构模型（constitutive model）的轴对称有限元模拟（axisymmetric finite-element simulations），在可比较条件下系统研究形状恢复与液滴融合。采用Deborah数表征粘弹性带来的时间尺度竞争。

Result: 形状恢复由单一连接界面的全局粘毛细松弛主导，按单指数或多指数衰减取决于粘毛细时间尺度与应力松弛时间的相对大小；液滴融合则是一个多阶段过程，涉及局部曲率驱动的颈部形成、快速桥接扩展以及向全局松弛的转变。粘弹性引入的额外时间尺度（Deborah数）调控毛细驱动与应力松弛的竞争，增强了融合中间阶段的动力学并改变了松弛行为。外部流体的存在通过增加流体动力学耗散显著减慢融合过程。粘弹性体系与拉伸指数经验公式的偏差揭示了纯粘性模型的局限性。

Conclusion: 形状恢复与液滴融合虽均由毛细力驱动，但物理机制本质不同，粘弹性效应不可忽略。纯粘性模型不足以准确描述生物分子凝聚体的动力学行为，需引入考虑应力松弛的模型。该工作为理解和预测生物分子凝聚体的粘弹性动力学提供了统一的理论基础。

Abstract: Biomolecular condensates formed by phase separation often exhibit viscoelastic behavior, yet their shape recovery and fusion dynamics are frequently interpreted using purely viscous models. Here, we develop a unified theoretical and computational framework to quantify how viscoelasticity governs these two processes. We combine analytical theory for small-deformation shape recovery with axisymmetric finite-element simulations based on the Oldroyd-B constitutive model to systematically investigate both shape recovery and droplet fusion under comparable conditions. Our results show that, although both processes are driven by capillary forces, they are fundamentally distinct in their underlying physics. Shape recovery is governed by global viscocapillary relaxation of a single connected interface and follows single- or multi-exponential decay depending on the relative magnitude of the viscocapillary timescale and the stress relaxation time. In contrast, droplet fusion is intrinsically a multistage process involving localized curvature-driven neck formation, rapid bridge expansion, and a transition to global relaxation. We demonstrate that viscoelasticity introduces an additional intrinsic timescale that governs the competition between capillary driving and stress relaxation, characterized by the Deborah number. This leads to enhanced intermediate-stage fusion dynamics and modified relaxation behavior compared to Newtonian droplets. Furthermore, we show that the presence of an exterior fluid introduces additional hydrodynamic dissipation, significantly slowing the fusion process. Finally, we compare the computationally predicted droplet fusion in the Newtonian and viscoelastic cases with a stretched-exponential empirical formula. Deviations observed in viscoelastic regimes highlight the limitations of purely viscous descriptions and the need for models incorporating stress relaxation.

</details>

# cs.IT [[Back]](#toc)

### [43] [Grouped Reverse Importance Sampling for the Partition Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26748)
*Neri Merhav*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出并分析了几种分组逆重要性采样（grouped RIS, GRIS）方法，用于从玻尔兹曼分布样本估计配分函数。研究发现，任何能改善普通RIS的权重函数都必须耦合组内分量，且在不失最优性的前提下，权重函数可仅依赖于组总能量。对于k=2和k=3，非重叠分组（NOL）的均方误差（MSE）在三个示例中降低了20%–65%。进一步提出的滑动窗口变体（FSW和VSW）在数值上表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在统计力学（statistical mechanics）中，从玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann distribution）的样本估计配分函数（partition function）是一个核心问题。普通逆重要性采样（RIS）逐样本加权，存在均方误差（MSE）较大的局限。本文旨在通过引入分组策略，寻找可处理（tractable）且能最小化MSE的权重函数，从而提升配分函数估计的精度。

Method: 本文提出分组逆重要性采样（grouped RIS, GRIS）方法，将样本分为大小为k≥2的组（groups/batches），对每组施加联合权重函数（joint weight function）。理论分析基于将归一化MSE与卡方散度（chi-squared divergence）关联的恒等式，证明改进型权重必须耦合（couple）组内分量，且可简化为仅依赖组总能量（group-energy weight functions）的形式。此外，还提出了两种滑动窗口（sliding-window）变体：固定权重滑动窗口（FSW）和变权重滑动窗口（VSW）。

Result: 对于k=2和k=3，非重叠分组（NOL）在三个数值示例中使MSE降低了20%–65%。滑动窗口变体中，FSW优于NOL，VSW进一步优于FSW。但滑动窗口变体下，关于权重函数可简化为仅依赖组总能量的结论是否成立尚待进一步研究。

Conclusion: 分组逆重要性采样（GRIS）通过组级联合加权有效降低了配分函数估计的MSE。核心理论贡献在于：权重函数必须耦合组内分量，且可无损失地简化为仅依赖组总能量的形式。滑动窗口变体提供了进一步的性能提升空间，但其理论分析仍不完整。

Abstract: We introduce and analyze several grouped variants of the method of reverse importance sampling (RIS) for estimating a partition function from samples of the Boltzmann distribution $p(x)=e^{ \betaU(x)}/Z(β)$. Ordinary RIS weighs each sample separately. By contrast, our proposed grouped RIS (GRIS) methods are based on assigning the samples into groups (or batches) of size $k\ge 2$ and applying a joint weight function to each group. The focal point of the research is the quest for a tractable weight function that would yield the smallest possible mean squared error (MSE). A simple identity relates the normalized MSE to the chi-squared divergence between the joint-weight distribution and the distribution of the $k$-fold sum of independent energies. Our first theoretical finding is that any weight that improves on ordinary RIS ($k=1$) must couple the group components. In other words, it must not be a product-form function across those components, as product-form weight functions always worsen the MSE. Our second, and more important, finding is that, without loss of optimality, it is sufficient to seek weight functions that depend only on the total energy, $\sum_iU(x_i)$, of the group (group-energy weight functions); for the sliding-window variants, the analogous result is open. This finding simplifies both the theoretical analysis and the application of the method substantially. For $k=2$ and $k=3$, the MSE associated with non-overlapping (NOL) groups is reduced by $20$--$65\%$ across three examples. We then propose two additional variants of GRIS, both based on sliding-window grouping (as opposed to NOL grouping). The first applies a fixed weight sliding window (FSW) across all (cyclic) shifts of the sliding window, and the second allows a variable-weight sliding window (VSW). The FSW scheme improves on the NOL one, and the VSW improves even further, as will be demonstrated numerically.

</details>

### [44] [Challenging the $p$-type Paradigm: Intrinsic $n$-type Mobility in Antiferromagnetic Cr$_2$O$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26269)
*Á. A. Carrasco Álvarez,S. Poncé*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理玻尔兹曼输运方程计算，证明了氧化铬（Cr2O3）本质上为n型半导体，其电子迁移率在宽温度范围内始终高于空穴迁移率，推翻了其作为p型透明导电氧化物的传统观点，并揭示了迁移率不对称性源于电子结构而非声子散射差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管氧化铬（Cr2O3）被广泛视为p型透明导电氧化物（transparent conducting oxide），但其本征输运特性一直存在争议。本文旨在通过从头算方法澄清这一根本性问题。

Method: 采用第一性原理玻尔兹曼输运方程（ab initio Boltzmann transport equation），计算了声子限制下的电子和空穴迁移率，并分析了散射机制对二者的影响。

Result: 在宽温度范围内，电子迁移率系统性地高于空穴迁移率，表明Cr2O3本征为n型。声子散射对电子和空穴的影响相似，迁移率不对称性主要由电子结构决定——即价带具有更大的有效质量（effective mass）和多谷特征（multi-valley character）。

Conclusion: Cr2O3的本征n型特性结合适中的空穴迁移率，使其具备双极输运（bipolar transport）能力，从而重新定义了其在透明电子学中的角色。本迁移率研究补充了以往的缺陷形成能研究，表明通常观察到的p型行为是外禀的（extrinsic），为Cr2O3建立了完整的化学-输运范式。

Abstract: Chromium oxide (Cr$_2$O$_3$) is widely considered a $p$-type transparent conducting oxide despite ongoing debate regarding its intrinsic transport character. Here, we resolve this question by computing phonon-limited electron and hole mobilities using the ab initio Boltzmann transport equation. We find that electron mobility systematically exceeds hole mobility over a wide temperature range, demonstrating that Cr$_2$O$_3$ is intrinsically $n$-type. Analysis of scattering mechanisms reveals that scattering with phonons affects electrons and holes similarly, and that the mobility asymmetry originates from the electronic structure, namely the larger effective mass and multi-valley character of the valence band. The intrinsic $n$-type character, combined with moderate hole mobility, enables bipolar transport and revises the role of Cr$_2$O$_3$ in transparent electronics. Additionally, our results on mobility complement previous studies on defect formation indicating that the commonly observed $p$-type behavior is extrinsic. These insights provide a complete chemical-transport paradigm for Cr$_2$O$_3$, re-evaluating its role in functional transparent electronic and magneto-optoelectronic applications

</details>


### [45] [Nanoscale Phase Distribution Governs Exchange Bias in Multiphase Magnetic Nanoparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26330)
*Murtaza Bohra,Stefanos Giaremis,Vidyadhar Singh,Joseph Kioseoglou,Stephan Steinhauer,Panagiotis Grammatikopoulos*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过气相合成、磁性表征与第一性原理自旋动力学模拟，揭示了Ni-Cr/NiO纳米颗粒中交换偏置（exchange bias）效应受铁磁-反铁磁相的空间分布与界面拓扑（interfacial topology）主导，而非单纯由相存在决定；并通过理论-模拟耦合框架建立了超越超顺磁极限的纳米磁体设计路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交换偏置效应在铁磁-反铁磁（ferromagnet-antiferromagnet）界面的行为在复杂纳米异质结构（nanoscale heterostructures）中尚不清晰，亟需系统地理解其微观起源与调控机制。

Method: 采用气相合成（gas-phase synthesis）制备Ni-Cr/NiO纳米颗粒模型体系，结合先进磁性表征与基于第一性原理（first-principles）的自旋动力学（spin-dynamics）模拟进行分析。

Result: 在10 K下观察到显著的负交换偏置（0.8 kOe）与矫顽力增强（1.4 kOe）；Cr偏析或核心Cr积累均导致两种效应降低；磁性相竞争导致了从负到正的交换偏置反转以及从交换主导到偶极主导的交叉。

Conclusion: 建立了将密度泛函理论（density-functional-theory）计算直接链接至纳米颗粒系综自旋动力学模拟的预测框架，为设计超越超顺磁极限（superparamagnetic limit）的交换耦合纳米磁体提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Exchange bias at ferromagnet-antiferromagnet interfaces underpins magnetic memory, spintronic devices, and nanoscale electromagnetic technologies, yet its behaviour in complex nanoscale heterostructures remains poorly understood. Here we uncover how exchange bias emerges in functional multiphase metal-oxide nanoparticles by combining gas-phase synthesis, advanced magnetic characterisation, and first-principles-informed spin-dynamics simulations. Using Ni-Cr/NiO nanoparticles as a model system, we show that exchange bias is governed not simply by the presence of ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic phases, but critically by their nanoscale spatial distribution and interfacial topology. At 10 K, significant negative exchange bias (0.8 kOe) and coercivity enhancement (1.4 kOe) was exhibited; both decreased due to either Cr-segregation (at low Cr content) or to Cr accumulation inside the core (at high Cr content). The resulting competition between magnetic phases produces a temperature-driven inversion from negative to positive exchange bias and a crossover from exchange-dominated to dipolar interactions. By linking density-functional-theory calculations directly to spin-dynamics simulations of nanoparticle ensembles, we establish a predictive framework for designing exchange-coupled nanomagnets capable of operating beyond the superparamagnetic limit.

</details>


### [46] [Ductility Design Rules for Tungsten based Refractory High Entropy Alloys from Sparse Experimental Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26501)
*Avik Mahata,Nick Beaver*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究基于实验数据构建了物理信息驱动的机器学习模型，用于预测钨基难熔高熵合金（RHEAs）的室温延性。支持向量分类器（SVC）在稀疏数据集上泛化最佳，并识别出影响韧脆行为的关键特征（如交换关联参数、价电子浓度等）。模型预测Ti、Ni、Co的中等添加量可提升室温延性，而高Cr含量导致脆性，与已有实验观察一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钨基难熔高熵合金（tungsten-based refractory high-entropy alloys, RHEAs）在聚变应用中前景广阔，但室温下常呈现脆性，主要源于钨的高韧脆转变温度（ductile-to-brittle transition temperature, DBTT）。因此，亟需识别可改善延性的合金化策略。

Method: 首先整理实验报道的含钨合金数据集，开发基于成分的物理信息描述符（physics-informed descriptors）。采用嵌套交叉验证（nested cross-validation）评估三种分类器，以支持向量分类器（support vector classifier, SVC）为最优模型。利用Shapley加法解释（Shapley additive explanations, SHAP）识别影响韧脆行为的关键特征，并在训练数据凸插值域内生成合成成分，通过伪三元相图（pseudo-ternary diagrams）可视化延性趋势。

Result: 交换关联参数（exchange-correlation parameter）、价电子浓度（valence electron concentration）、压力场（pressure field）和电负性失配（electronegativity mismatch）是影响韧脆行为的最重要特征。模型预测Ti、Ni、Co的中等添加量有助于提高室温延性，而高Cr含量则促进脆性。这些预测与已发表的实验观察一致，且DFT弹性描述符（DFT-derived elastic descriptors）与SVC决策函数边界（decision-function margins）的一致性进一步支持了分类边界的物理相关性。

Conclusion: 尽管当前力学数据集仍有限且异质性较高，但模型捕捉到了与实验一致的延性趋势，为在聚变环境下筛选钨基RHEAs提供了一个可解释的、物理信息驱动的框架，可指导后续的定向模拟和实验验证。

Abstract: Tungsten-based refractory high-entropy alloys (RHEAs) are promising materials for fusion applications but often remain brittle at room temperature because of tungsten's high ductile-to-brittle transition temperature (DBTT). To identify alloying strategies that improve ductility, we compiled a curated dataset of experimentally reported tungsten-containing alloys and developed composition-based, physics-informed descriptors for machine learning. Three classifiers were evaluated using nested cross-validation, and a support vector classifier (SVC) showed the best generalization for this sparse dataset. Shapley additive explanations identified the exchange-correlation parameter, valence electron concentration, pressure field, and electronegativity mismatch as the most influential features governing ductile-brittle behavior. Synthetic compositions generated within the convex interpolation domain of the training data were evaluated and visualized on pseudo-ternary diagrams to map predicted ductility trends. The model predicts that moderate additions of Ti, Ni, and Co increase the likelihood of room-temperature ductility, whereas high Cr contents promote brittle behavior. These predictions agree with published experimental observations, including Ti-assisted ductility through solid-solution and electronic effects and embrittlement in Cr-rich refractory alloys. Agreement between DFT-derived elastic descriptors and SVC decision-function margins further supports the physical relevance of the learned classification boundary. Although the available mechanical dataset remains limited and heterogeneous, the model captures experimentally consistent trends and provides an interpretable, physics-informed framework for screening tungsten-based RHEAs for targeted simulation and experimental validation in fusion environments.

</details>


### [47] [Topological phase transition driven by in-plane spin rotation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26548)
*Xinyue Zhu,Yu Xie,Yifei Hao,Fei Gao,Yue Li,Junting Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过连续面内自旋旋转（in-plane spin rotation）可逆切换拓扑态的新机制，基于磁点群（magnetic point group）对称性对Berry曲率分布的约束。以二维Kagome铁磁Chern绝缘体（ferromagnetic Chern insulator）为原型，展示了60°面内磁化旋转即可反转Chern数（Chern number）符号并经过拓扑平庸态。微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulation）证实该机制可在极低磁场和超快时间尺度下运行，为拓扑态的高效低能耗操控提供了新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性拓扑绝缘体中磁性与非平庸能带拓扑之间的内在耦合使得外磁场成为操控拓扑态的有力工具，但传统的磁控机制（如驱动磁相变或完全反转磁化）通常需要大磁场且缺乏连续可调性。本文旨在建立一种通过连续面内自旋旋转实现拓扑态可逆切换的对称性框架，以克服上述局限性。

Method: 本文首先建立了基于磁点群对称性对Berry曲率（Berry curvature）分布约束的理论框架，用于描述通过连续面内自旋旋转可逆切换拓扑态的机制。然后以二维Kagome铁磁Chern绝缘体为原型系统，结合微磁模拟验证了该方案的有效性。

Result: 研究发现，在Kagome铁磁Chern绝缘体中，60°的面内磁化旋转即可使Chern数符号反转，并在此过程中经历一个拓扑平庸态。微磁模拟进一步证实，这种自旋重取向（spin-reorientation）驱动的开关机制可在极低外磁场条件下实现，且切换过程达到超快时间尺度。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个基于对称性约束的高效低能耗拓扑态操控新范式（paradigm），通过面内自旋旋转替代传统大磁场驱动方式，为未来拓扑电子器件中的可逆、连续调控提供了新的物理原理和实现路径。

Abstract: The intrinsic coupling between magnetism and nontrivial band topology in magnetic topological insulators makes external magnetic fields a powerful tool for manipulating topological states. However, conventional magnetic control mechanisms, such as driving magnetic phase transitions or fully reversing magnetization, typically demand large magnetic fields and lack continuous tunability. Here, we establish a symmetry framework for the reversible switching of topological states via continuous in-plane spin rotation, governed by magnetic point group constraints on the Berry curvature distribution. Using a two-dimensional kagome ferromagnetic Chern insulator as a prototype, we demonstrate that a 60°in-plane magnetization rotation reverses the sign of the Chern number, transitioning through a topologically trivial state. Crucially, micromagnetic simulations confirm that this spin-reorientation-driven switching operates under exceptionally small magnetic fields and on ultrafast timescales. This work provides a highly efficient, low-energy paradigm for the manipulation of topological states.

</details>


### [48] [Shape-Constrained Bayesian Active Learning of Self-Limiting Saturation Curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26577)
*Pouyan Navabi,Christos G. Takoudis*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种基于贝叶斯单调I-样条回归（Bayesian monotonic I-spline regression）的主动学习平台，用于从稀疏、有噪声的数据中准确学习自限性饱和曲线（self-limiting saturation curves）。该平台无需预设动力学模型，能保证后验曲线严格单调递增、从零开始且不出现非物理波动，在20次测量预算内即可达到噪声水平精度，显著优于标准高斯过程（Gaussian process）替代模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自限性饱和曲线广泛存在于气体吸附、酶动力学、剂量-反应药理学及原子层沉积（atomic layer deposition, ALD）等关键领域，但每条曲线需靠少量昂贵测量来构建，这是共同的瓶颈。标准替代模型——静态核高斯过程（stationary-kernel Gaussian process）——未施加形状约束，在稀疏、有噪声的数据上会产生非物理的凹陷（dips），进而扭曲推断出的曲线及用于选择下一次实验的不确定性估计。

Method: 平台的核心是贝叶斯单调I-样条回归（Bayesian monotonic I-spline regression），确保每一条后验曲线从零开始严格递增、永不下降。饱和水平（plateau）由最大暴露量处的实测值设定而非先验假设；任意饱和度水平对应的输入值通过水平穿越（level crossing）从后验中读取，无需假设任何动力学模型。主动学习通过普通的不确定性采样（uncertainty sampling）驱动。

Result: 在五种动力学性质不同的等温线族（Langmuir、解离型Michaelis-Menten、S型Sips、对数型Elovich、色散型Kohlrausch-Williams-Watts）上逐条验证，以ALD工艺开发为实例：同一固定替代模型恢复每条曲线至测量噪声水平，且未产生任何非单调后验样本。无噪声扫描显示该基函数本身在各族的所有区域中接近精确。在主动学习驱动下，平台在每个区域均可在20次测量预算内达到噪声水平精度，最少仅需7次测量；而随机采样仅在五个区域中的两个成功。预测的脉冲时间在接近饱和时偏向保守（较长脉冲）。

Conclusion: 由于该基函数不偏向任何特定动力学形式，该平台适用于任何需要从稀疏数据中学习自限性响应的场景，具有广泛的跨领域适用性。

Abstract: Self-limiting saturation curves, monotone responses that rise from zero to a plateau, govern gas adsorption, enzyme kinetics, dose-response pharmacology, and the growth per cycle of atomic layer deposition (ALD), yet mapping each curve from a handful of costly measurements is a shared bottleneck. The standard surrogate, a stationary-kernel Gaussian process, enforces no shape constraint: on sparse, noisy data it produces unphysical dips that corrupt both the inferred curve and the uncertainty used to choose the next experiment. We present an active-learning platform built on Bayesian monotonic I-spline regression, in which every posterior curve rises from exactly zero and never decreases, the plateau is set by a measurement at maximum exposure rather than a prior, and the input at any saturation level is read from the posterior by level crossing with no kinetic model assumed. Benchmarked isotherm by isotherm on five kinetically distinct families (Langmuir, dissociative Michaelis-Menten, sigmoidal Sips, logarithmic Elovich, and dispersive Kohlrausch-Williams-Watts), with ALD process development as the working example, the same fixed surrogate recovers every curve to within measurement noise without a single non-monotone posterior draw, and noise-free sweeps show the basis itself is near-exact across each family's regimes, locating its single capacity boundary at the sharpest sigmoidal onset. Driven by ordinary uncertainty sampling, the platform reaches noise-floor accuracy within a 20-measurement budget in every regime, in as few as seven measurements, whereas random sampling succeeds in only two of the five; the predicted pulse times err only on the conservative side, toward longer pulses, near saturation. Because the basis privileges no kinetic form, the platform applies wherever a self-limiting response must be learned from scarce data.

</details>


### [49] [Lattice Reconstruction and Orbital Hybridization Suppress Magnetism in TaCo$_2$Te$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26644)
*Ulysse Chazarin,Bharat C. Bathu,Zuned Ahmed,Marta Zonno,Chiara Bigi,Francois Bertran,Adolfo O. Fumega,Orlando J. Silveira,Shawulienu Kezilebieke*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过多种实验与理论手段，揭示了低维量子材料TaCo₂Te₂中晶格重构如何通过轨道杂化（orbital hybridization）抑制磁性不稳定性，并导致电子对称性从六角晶格转变为类方形电子结构，从而建立了一个结构重构调控磁性与关联物相（correlated phases）的模型体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维量子材料中的结构重构（structural reconstruction）可能通过轨道杂化显著改变电子对称性与磁稳定性，然而其具体机制尚不清晰。本文旨在探究层状范德瓦尔斯（van der Waals）化合物TaCo₂Te₂中晶格重构、电子结构与磁性不稳定性之间的相互作用。

Method: 结合扫描隧道显微镜/扫描隧道谱（STM/STS）、非接触原子力显微镜（nc-AFM）、角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）以及密度泛函理论（DFT）进行综合研究。nc-AFM用于解析原子结构，STM/STS用于探测电子局域态密度，ARPES用于测量能带结构，DFT用于理论计算与轨道投影分析。

Result: nc-AFM显示扭曲的六角形Te表面晶格，但STM/STS呈现显著的类方形电子对称性；ARPES揭示了强各向异性费米面（Fermi surface）与重构的低能态。偏压依赖的STM衬度并非源于占据态与未占据态的简单反转，而是由特定能量下具有相反空间衬度的电子态主导的能量积分局域态密度（local density of state）决定。DFT计算表明，结构重构通过增强轨道杂化抑制了未畸变结构中的磁性不稳定性，稳定了非磁性基态。

Conclusion: TaCo₂Te₂被确立为一个模型体系，其中晶格重构能够重组电子对称性并抑制磁性，凸显了结构重构作为调控低维量子材料中关联物相与磁性相（magnetic phases）的有效途径。

Abstract: Structural reconstruction in low-dimensional quantum materials can strongly modify electronic symmetry and magnetic stability through orbital hybridization. Here, we investigate the interplay between lattice reconstruction, electronic structure, and magnetic instability in the layered van der Waals compound TaCo$_2$Te$_2$ using scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy (STM/STS), non-contact atomic force microscopy (nc-AFM), angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES), and density functional theory (DFT). While nc-AFM resolves a distorted hexagonal Te surface lattice, STM/STS reveal a pronounced square-like electronic symmetry that does not directly follow the atomic structure. ARPES further shows a strongly anisotropic Fermi surface and reconstructed low-energy states. Spatially resolved spectroscopy and orbital-projected DFT demonstrate that the bias-dependent STM contrast does not arise from a simple reversal between occupied and unoccupied states, but from the energy-integrated local density of states dominated by electronic states exhibiting opposite spatial contrast at selected energies. DFT calculations further show that reconstruction suppresses the magnetic instability present in the undistorted structure, stabilizing a nonmagnetic ground state through enhanced orbital hybridization. These results establish TaCo$_2$Te$_2$ as a model system in which lattice reconstruction reorganizes electronic symmetry and suppresses magnetism, highlighting structural reconstruction as a route for controlling correlated and magnetic phases in low-dimensional quantum materials.

</details>


### [50] [Preconditioning Magnetic Systems in Kohn-Sham Density Functional Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26693)
*Clémentine Barat,Antoine Levitt,Marc Torrent*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论（Kohn-Sham density functional theory）中的自洽场迭代（self-consistent field iterations）在磁性系统中常因介电矩阵（dielectric matrix）出现小本征值而收敛缓慢，这一现象与电子相变（electronic phase transitions）密切相关。本文旨在研究并缓解此类收敛问题。

Method: 提出一种新的预处理（preconditioning）方案，该方案受Stoner模型（Stoner model）启发，基于非相互作用磁化率（non-interacting susceptibility），并忽略轨道变化（orbital variations）的影响。

Result: 在一系列铁磁系统（ferromagnetic systems）上的实验表明，该方法在磁相变（magnetic phase transitions）附近能够显著减少达到收敛所需的迭代次数。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于Stoner模型的预处理方案有效缓解了磁性系统中自洽场迭代的收敛难题，为处理含相变的密度泛函计算提供了实用的加速手段。

Abstract: The convergence of the self-consistent field iterations in Kohn-Sham density functional theory can be significantly hindered by the presence of small eigenvalues in the dielectric matrix, which are often associated with electronic phase transitions in magnetic systems. In this work, we study this type of convergence issues and propose a new preconditioning scheme to mitigate them. Our preconditioning scheme is inspired by the Stoner model and based on a non-interacting susceptibility that neglects orbital variations. We demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach on a range of ferromagnetic systems, showing that it can significantly reduce the number of iterations required to achieve convergence in the vicinity of magnetic phase transitions.

Method: 利用纳米颗粒中声子（phonon）局域化（phonon confinement）对声子态密度（density of states）产生的尺寸依赖性修改：两个相连纳米颗粒中较小的颗粒施加更强的声子局域化，从而产生整流（rectifying）声子输运；将该概念扩展到宏观尺度，构建两层不同尺寸纳米颗粒的重叠层，实现宏观声子二极管。通过激光光斑局部加热，使用红外成像（infrared imaging）测量声子二极管上的温度分布。

Conclusion: 尽管当前整流强度有限，但存在大量优化可能性，使得该方法在纳米和宏观尺度下均有望实现超低体积热绝缘（ultra-low volume thermal insulation）。

Abstract: Thermal insulation remains an important technological challenge across the vast number of applications, from living quarters to quantum technology. The smaller of the two connected nanoparticles imposes stronger phonon confinement leading to rectifying phonon transport. This concept is extended to the macroscale by constructing two overlapping layers of differently sized nanoparticles, thereby realizing a macroscopic phonon diode. Following the localized heat deposition by laser light, the temperature profiles across a phonon-diode were measured by infrared imaging. Although the rectifying strength is moderate, the abundance of optimization possibilities makes this method promising for ultra-low volume thermal insulation at both the nano- and macroscale

Abstract: The interaction between hydrogen and screw dislocations in bcc iron is central to understanding hydrogen embrittlement. Our results show good agreement with the limited density functional theory data available in the literature. ### [54] [Giant and Broadband Circular Dichroism from Particle-Hole Symmetry Breaking in Weyl Semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26810)
*Xiangyu Jiang,Zeping Shi,Yuhan Du,Haonan Chen,Jiayu Wang,Wenbin Wu,Guangyi Wang,Congming Hao,Mingfan Yao,Mingsen Zhou,Xin Chen,Chenyao Xu,Zhongbo Yan,Cheng Zhang,Hai-Zhou Lu,Junhao Chu,Xiang Yuan*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Circular dichroism originates from symmetry breaking of material structure, leading to differential absorption of left- and right-circularly polarized light. However, circular dichroism in most materials is inherently weak and spectrally narrow, especially in the mid-to-far infrared. Here, we uncover giant infrared circular dichroism in the magnetic-field-forced Weyl semimetal Mn(Bi,Sb)2Te4, driven by extreme particle-hole symmetry breaking. Helicity-resolved magneto-infrared spectroscopy reveals circular dichroism exceeding 3000 mdeg (~130 mdeg/nm) with above-degree response extending over the 6-13 μm spectral range. The optical resonances are enhanced by a strong band nesting effect intrinsic to the Landau levels of type-II Weyl dispersion. A symmetry-based kp model reproduces these magneto-infrared responses and demonstrates that magnetization-induced asymmetric spin-orbit coupling generates particle-hole symmetry breaking, suppressing spin-up, parity-even wavefunction components in the valence Landau band and thereby producing pronounced optical helicity selectivity. Our findings establish particle-hole symmetry breaking as an effective route toward helicity-resolved optical control in quantum materials.

### [56] [HF Etching and Silanization: Evidence for the Role of Surface Hydroxyl Groups in Silicon Nitride Resonator Loss](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26838)

Abstract: Silicon nitride $SiN_x$ nanomechanical resonators are central to sensing, quantum technologies, and fundamental physics experiments due to their exceptional mechanical quality factors (Q). However, as resonator thickness approaches the nano-scale, surface-related dissipation limits performance. Here, we investigate the role of surface chemistry in low-stress Si-rich SiNx membranes through a combination of hydrofluoric acid (HF) etching and trimethylchlorosilane (TMCS) silanization, correlated with surface characterization and mechanical measurements. Preliminary analysis by TEM-EELS, XPS, RBS/ERDA, and XRR reveals a native oxide surface layer (1-2 nm). While HF etching effectively removes the native oxide and TMCS introduces hydrophobic $Si-(CH_3)_3$ termination, neither oxide thickness nor surface energy correlates with mechanical dissipation. TMCS treatments produce the largest enhancements, increasing $Q_{int}$ by up to 50%, whereas HF etching alone yields lower gains of 20-25%. ### [58] [Investigation on the temperature dependence of substrate-induced in-plane uniaxial magnetic anisotropy in Ni thin films grown on 128° Y-cut LiNbO3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27255)
*Kalani Perera,Morton Greenslit,Luke Doucette,Mauricio Pereira da Cunha,Nicholas S Bingham*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本论文报道了在128° Y-cut LiNbO3衬底上磁控溅射沉积的连续Ni薄膜中，衬底诱导磁各向异性的温度依赖性。超薄薄膜在低温下表现出各向同性行为和反常的磁滞分支交叉，而退火可抑制该现象并建立单轴各向异性，其强度随温度变化，源于晶格失配和热膨胀系数（CTE）失配共同决定的残余应变，且与薄膜厚度无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Ni薄膜在压电衬底（128° Y-cut LiNbO3）上因衬底诱导产生的磁各向异性随温度变化的规律，并揭示退火处理对该各向异性的影响机制。

Method: 采用磁控溅射（magnetron sputtering）在128° Y-cut LiNbO3衬底上室温沉积连续Ni薄膜；通过温度依赖的磁化测量，对比as-grown薄膜与退火薄膜的磁滞回线和各向异性行为；分析残余应变中晶格失配与热膨胀系数（coefficient of thermal expansion, CTE）失配的贡献。

Result: 超薄薄膜在低温下呈现各向同性行为和反常的磁滞分支交叉（hysteresis branch crossing），退火薄膜在相同温度范围内无分支交叉；退火后薄膜建立了具有明确易轴和难轴的单轴各向异性（uniaxial anisotropy），其强度随温度演化；该各向异性由Ni薄膜与衬底间的晶格失配和CTE失配共同决定的残余应变主导，且5 nm和100 nm薄膜的行为与厚度无关。

Conclusion: 退火增强了薄膜-衬底界面处的磁弹性耦合（magnetoelastic coupling），使磁响应开始遵循由晶格失配和CTE失配所施加的各向异性应变，从而建立了单轴磁各向异性。

Abstract: We report the temperature dependence of the substrate-induced magnetic anisotropy in continuous Ni thin films deposited at room temperature using magnetron sputtering on a 128° Y-cut LiNbO3 substrate. Ultrathin films exhibit a pronounced temperature dependence in magnetization, with as-grown films showing isotropic behavior and an unconventional hysteresis branch crossing at relatively low temperatures, whereas no branch crossing is observed in annealed films over the investigated temperature range, indicating suppression of the underlying mechanism. Temperature-dependent magnetization measurements show that post-deposition annealing establishes uniaxial anisotropy with well-defined easy and hard axes, whose strength evolves with temperature due to the nature of residual strain governed by both lattice mismatch and coefficient of thermal expansion (CTE) mismatch between the Ni film and the 128° Y-cut substrate, independent of film thickness for both 5 nm and 100 nm films. The emergence of this anisotropy following annealing indicates enhanced magnetoelastic coupling at the film-substrate interface, as the magnetic response begins to follow the anisotropic strain imposed by lattice mismatch and CTE mismatch.

</details>


### [59] [3D Imaging of Complex Skyrmion and Hopf Topologies in an Extended Sample](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27365)
*I. Binnie,H. Fang,B. Shearer,A. Grafov,N. Jenkins,Y. Shao,C. O'Leary,Y. Liao,T. Feggeler,A. Oh,S. Yazdi,J. Zou,B. Wang,E-E. Cating,S. A. Montoya,D. Shapiro,J. Miao,H. C. Kapteyn,M. M. Murnane*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用矢量叠层断层扫描（vector ptycho-tomography）这一相干衍射成像技术，首次无先验假设地实验揭示了Fe/Gd多层膜中三维（3D）斯格明子（skyrmion）与霍普夫子（Hopf）拓扑自旋织构，观察到桶形斯格明子管及其手性扭转（twisted helicity），并重建了包含24个斯格明子的扩展晶格，填补了高分辨三维磁成像的关键空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋织构（spin textures）是拓扑保护（topological protection）等新兴磁性现象的核心，也是赛道存储器（racetrack memory）、逻辑门（logic gates）和神经形态计算（neuromorphic computing）等自旋电子器件范式的基础。然而，目前缺乏能够高分辨、无先验假设地重建扩展三维自旋织构的实验手段，这限制了对磁性材料中三维拓扑复杂性的深入探索。

Method: 采用一种称为矢量叠层断层扫描（vector ptycho-tomography）的相干衍射成像技术，结合对噪声鲁棒的算法，对斯格明子（skyrmion）和霍普夫子（Hopf）拓扑结构进行三维磁织构成像，过程中不对样品施加任何先验假设。该方法可实现元素特异性的高分辨三维重建。

Result: 实验首次揭示了扩展的三维斯格明子晶格，包含24个拓扑荷（topological charge）为1的斯格明子，其平均深度依赖的畴壁宽度（domain wall width）为23-40 nm，深度依赖的扭转手性（twisted helicity）从±155°变化至±30°，分数霍普指数（fractional Hopf index）为±0.3。Fe/Gd多层膜中偶极稳定（dipole stabilized）的斯格明子呈现桶形（barrel-shaped）斯格明子管，具有扭转手性，从表面的Néel型缠绕过渡到体相的顺时针和逆时针Bloch型缠绕，可描述为分数霍普夫子（fractional hopfions）。超过10 TB数据经分析后，在>0.4 μm³体积内实现了奈奎斯特极限（Nyquist limit）8 nm的高保真三维重建。

Conclusion: 该方法填补了当前磁成像领域的关键空白，实现了全视野扩展自旋织构的高分辨、元素特异性三维重建，为在三维空间中探索磁性材料的拓扑复杂性提供了新途径。

Abstract: Spin textures are key for emergent magnetic phenomena such as topological protection and underpin novel spintronic device paradigms based on racetrack memory, logic gates, and neuromorphic computing. Using a coherent diffractive imaging technique called vector ptycho-tomography, in combination with algorithms that are robust to noise, we image the 3D magnetic texture of skyrmion and Hopf topologies with no prior assumptions about the sample. This directly reveals experimentally for the first time an extended 3D skyrmion lattice, including the domain wall shape, topological charge, helicity, and Hopf index. Our findings demonstrate experimentally that dipole stabilized skyrmions in Fe/Gd multilayers exhibit barrel-shaped skyrmion tubes with a twisted helicity, transitioning from N$é$el-type winding at the surfaces to both clockwise and counterclockwise Bloch-type winding in the bulk, that can also be described as fractional hopfions. We image a lattice of 24 skyrmions with topological charge 1, average depth-dependent domain wall width of 23 to 40 nm, depth-dependent twisted helicity from $\pm$155$°$ to $\pm$30$°$, and fractional Hopf index of $\pm$0.3. Over 10 TB of data were analyzed to yield a fully-resolved 3D reconstruction over a >0.4 $μ$m$^3$ volume, with high fidelity down to the Nyquist limit of 8 nm. This method fills a key gap in the current landscape of magnetic imaging by enabling high-resolution, element-specific 3D reconstructions of full-field extended spin textures - offering a new route for exploring the topological complexity of magnetic materials in three dimensions.

### [60] [Spectral expansion of LQG heat trace and KPZ scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26958)
*Nathanaël Berestycki,Jakob Klein*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文研究了二维有界区域上刘维尔量子引力（LQG）热迹在短时间极限下的渐近行为，发现预期热迹谱展开的第二项受KPZ关系给出的非平凡指数控制，并解决了热核退火渐近行为的相关猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解LQG热核在短时间尺度上的精细结构，特别是谱展开中除主项之外的次领头项行为，并验证KPZ关系（Knizhnik–Polyakov–Zamolodchikov relation）在热迹渐近中的体现。

Method: 基于全平面高斯自由场（Gaussian free field）和二维有界区域，分析LQG热迹（定义为LQG热核对角元在区域上的积分）在$t\to 0$时的渐近展开，结合KPZ标度关系进行理论推导。

Result: 证明了预期热迹在$t\to 0$时，其谱展开的第二项由KPZ关系确定的非平凡指数控制；对于热含量（heat content）的类似结果几乎必然成立；解决了热核退火渐近行为的猜想，并证明了适当重标度后的热核所有矩均有限。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了LQG热迹短时渐近中KPZ关系的非平凡作用，并为随机几何中热核行为的严格分析提供了新结果。

Abstract: Let $h$ be a whole plane Gaussian free field, and let $Ω$ be a bounded domain in two dimensions. We study the asymptotics as $t\to 0$ of the Liouville quantum gravity (LQG) heat trace, defined as the integral over $Ω$ of the on-diagonal LQG heat kernel. Our main result is to show that the second term in the spectral expansion as $t\to 0$ of the expected heat trace is governed by a nontrivial exponent, given by the KPZ (Knizhnik--Polyakov--Zamolodchikov) relation. A similar but stronger (almost sure) result applies to the related notion of heat content. Along the way we obtain various results on the short-term behaviour of the heat kernel, notably solving a conjecture of \cite{BW} concerning its annealed asymptotics, and showing the finiteness of all moments of the properly rescaled heat kernel.

### [61] [Non-colliding space-time inhomogeneous Markov chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27261)
*Theodoros Assiotis,Miles Foster Nyamundanda*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文建立了一类可积时空非齐次马尔可夫链碰撞时间尾部概率的显式首项渐近行为（带定量误差界），通过最陡下降法与Karlin-McGregor半群展开的新组合策略，解决了空间非齐次离散性带来的技术挑战，并验证了相互作用粒子系统中条件过程的最新预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了严格推导可积时空非齐次马尔可夫链（integrable space-time inhomogeneous Markov chains）碰撞时间（collision times）尾部概率的首项渐近行为，并验证相互作用粒子系统（interacting particle systems）中局部推阻相互作用（local push-block interactions）条件下过程的最新理论预测。

Method: 采用一种新颖的最陡下降法（steepest-descent analysis）与基于主导指标贡献（dominant-index contributions）的Karlin-McGregor半群展开（Karlin-McGregor semigroup expansion）相结合的策略，以规避空间非齐次的离散性质导致无法使用布朗运动耦合（coupling-with-Brownian-motion）技术的局限。

Result: 在离散时间和连续时间两种情形下，建立了一类可积时空非齐次马尔可夫链碰撞时间尾部概率的显式首项渐近行为，并给出了定量误差界（quantitative error bound）。该结果证实了相互作用粒子系统中条件过程的最新预测。

Conclusion: 所建立的首项渐近理论与定量误差界为理解可积时空非齐次马尔可夫链的碰撞行为提供了严格的理论基础，并为相互作用粒子系统中的相关预测提供了数学证明。

Abstract: We establish the explicit leading order asymptotics, with a quantitative error bound, of tail probabilities of collision times for a class of integrable space-time inhomogeneous Markov chains, in discrete and continuous time. The corresponding process conditioned not to intersect arises in interacting particle systems with local push-block interactions thereby confirming a recent prediction. The generic discrete nature of the spatial inhomogeneities rules out powerful coupling-with-Brownian-motion techniques, so our proof strategy proceeds instead via a novel steepest-descent analysis combined with a Karlin--McGregor semigroup expansion in terms of dominant-index contributions.

### [62] [Anomalous Hall viscosity of altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26239)
*Iksu Jang,Rui Aquino,Jörg Schmalian,Rafael M. Fernandes*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上证明，零磁场下的声子霍尔粘度（phonon Hall viscosity）是探测交变磁性（altermagnetism）的有效探针，能够明确区分交变磁体与铁磁体和传统反铁磁体，并揭示电子谱特征（如狄拉克点能隙和Lifshitz相变）及应变空间的贝里曲率（Berry curvature）拓扑结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的交变磁体研究中，通常利用动量空间（momentum-space）中的贝里曲率多极矩来表征其拓扑性质，但缺乏对交变磁性与其它磁有序态（如铁磁和反铁磁）的明确区分手段。本文旨在探索零磁场下声子霍尔粘度是否能够作为交变磁性的独特探测工具。

Method: 作者首先从对称性分析出发，证明霍尔粘度张量的有限元能够明确区分交变磁体与铁磁体和传统反铁磁体；随后在d波和g波交变磁体的模型中进行微观计算，分析霍尔粘度对电子能谱特征的敏感性。

Result: 发现霍尔粘度对电子能谱特征（如带隙狄拉克点和Lifshitz相变）具有强烈敏感性；这种敏感性来源于应变空间（strain-space）中的贝里曲率单极子（monopole），与交变磁体中标准动量空间贝里曲率的多极子（multipolar）特征形成对比。

Conclusion: 由于霍尔粘度可通过磁声学测量（magneto-acoustic measurements）进行实验探测，因此提供了一种强有力的方法来探测绝缘态交变磁体中的对称性破缺和拓扑性质。

Abstract: We show that the phonon Hall viscosity at zero magnetic field is a natural probe of altermagnetism. First, we demonstrate that the finite elements of the Hall viscosity tensor unambiguously distinguish altermagnets from ferromagnets and conventional antiferromagnets. We then microscopically compute the Hall viscosity in models for d-wave and g-wave altermagnets, and find a strong sensitivity to electronic spectrum features such as gapped Dirac points and Lifshitz transitions. This sensitivity reflects a strain-space Berry curvature monopole, which contrast to the multipolar character of the standard momentum-space Berry curvature in altermagnets. Since the Hall viscosity can be probed experimentally through magneto-acoustic measurements, it provides a compelling method to probe the broken symmetries and topology of insulating altermagnets.

</details>


### [63] [Quantum Hall effect in three-dimensional lattice induced by Wannier-Stark-Landau localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26444)
*D. -H. -Minh Nguyen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索平行电场和磁场共同作用下立方晶格中的三维量子霍尔效应（quantum Hall effect）及其拓扑性质。

Result: 能谱呈现三维Hofstadter蝴蝶结构，谱中心处等距共振，边界处出现分立能级；当费米能位于谱隙时，垂直于场平面的霍尔电导（Hall conductance）量子化，其他电导张量分量为零；开边界条件下出现由体陈数（bulk Chern numbers）保护的拓扑手性铰链模（chiral hinge modes）。

Conclusion: 该结果为在固态异质结和人工晶格中研究量子霍尔效应提供了新平台。

Abstract: We study the quantum Hall effect in a cubic lattice subjected to parallel electric and magnetic fields aligned along a crystal axis. The dual fields confine electrons in three dimensions with their classical orbits residing on the surface of a finite-size cylinder. In the quantum limit, the spectrum yields a three-dimensional generalization of the Hofstadter butterfly, featuring equidistant resonances near the spectral center and discrete levels near the boundaries. When the Fermi energy lies within these spectral gaps, the Hall conductance in the plane normal to the fields is quantized while other components of the conductance tensor vanish. Under open boundary conditions, this quantum Hall state exhibits topological chiral hinge modes protected by bulk Chern numbers. Our results offer a novel platform for studying the quantum Hall effect in both solid-state heterostructures and synthetic lattices.

### [64] [Photo-thermal origin of pulse laser induced orientation of crystallographic c axis in Tellurium thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26499)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在不同照射条件下系统研究碲样品的重定向行为；测量光致重定向的阈值通量随激光脉冲数量的变化关系；构建基于阿伦尼乌斯定律的最小动力学模型（minimal kinetic model）与实验数据进行比对；利用该模型预测其他二维各向异性材料的控制条件。

Result: 实验发现，光学重定向的阈值通量（threshold fluence）依赖于激光脉冲数量；该依赖关系与基于阿伦尼乌斯定律的最小动力学模型吻合良好。

Conclusion: 激光诱导碲薄膜晶体重定向的机制可通过阿伦尼乌斯型动力学模型描述；该模型可用于预测黑磷、WTe₂和SnSe等二维材料的光轴控制条件，为基于各向异性材料的电光器件开发提供指导。

Abstract: Recent studies have shown that the orientation of crystallographic c axis of Tellurium thin films can be controlled using picosecond long laser pulses. This method provides spatially programmable control of the crystal orientation and is therefore highly attractive for practical applications in functional optical and electronic devices. Previously, it was suggested that laser-induced selective melting and recrystallization can cause the laser-induced reorientation. However, this interpretation remains inconclusive due to limited data. To clarify the mechanism, here we systematically study Te samples under different irradiation conditions. We find that the threshold fluence for inducing optical reorientation depends on the number of laser pulses. The results agrees well with a minimal kinetic model based on the Arrhenius law. Using the model developed, we investigate the condition required to control the optic axis in other two-dimensional materials, such as black phosphorus, WTe2, and SnSe. These findings provide a guide for developing functional electro-optical devices based on anisotropic materials.

### [65] [Photon-Assisted Tunneling in Double Quantum Dot: Application of Scattering Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26622)
*Miyu Umebayashi,Mikio Eto*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上研究了一个双量子点（DQD）中平行光子辅助隧穿（PAT）的相干输运现象，利用散射理论求解含时薛定谔方程，发现通过极化激元能级发生共振隧穿，并观测到主峰和子峰中的阿哈罗诺夫—玻姆（Aharonov–Bohm）效应，同时提出了通过被辐照量子点进行相位测量的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在交流（AC）场辐照下一个量子点（QD）的双量子点（DQD）系统中光子辅助隧穿（PAT）的物理机制，特别是相干输运和量子干涉效应。

Method: 利用散射理论（scattering theory）求解含时薛定谔方程，分别处理单个量子点和双量子点（DQD）中的光子辅助隧穿（PAT）问题，同时引入磁通量以研究阿哈罗诺夫—玻姆（Aharonov–Bohm）效应。

Result: 当隧穿耦合Γ远小于光量子能量ℏω时，共振隧穿发生在极化激元（polariton）能级ε₀+Nℏω上（光子辅助隧穿PAT）；当Γ远大于ℏω时，通过瞬态能级ε(t)发生绝热输运（adiabatic transport）。在双量子点（DQD）中，阿哈罗诺夫—玻姆效应不仅出现在主峰（N=0）中，也出现在子峰（N≠0）中。在三端几何结构中，通过被辐照量子点测得的相位偏移在主峰和子峰附近均从0连续变化到π。

Conclusion: 光子辅助隧穿（PAT）通过极化激元态实现相干输运，阿哈罗诺夫—玻姆（Aharonov–Bohm）效应在多个能级通道中均被观测到；所建立的散射理论框架可扩展至三端几何结构并实现相位测量。

Abstract: We theoretically examine the photon-assisted tunneling (PAT) in a double quantum dot (DQD) in parallel when one of the quantum dots (QDs) is irradiated by an AC field. First, we formulate the PAT in a single QD by solving the time-dependent Schrödinger equation using the scattering theory. The QD has an oscillating energy level, $\varepsilon(t)=\varepsilon_0+eV_{\mathrm{AC}}\cosωt$, and is connected to two leads by the tunnel coupling $Γ$. We show that the resonant tunneling takes place through energy levels of the polariton, $\varepsilon_0+N\hbarω$ ($N=0,\pm 1, \pm 2, \cdots$), when $Γ\ll \hbarω$ (PAT) and through the energy level $\varepsilon(t)$ when $Γ\gg \hbarω$ (adiabatic transport). Then, the scattering theory is applied to the PAT in the DQD in the presence of magnetic flux penetrating between the QDs. We observe the Aharonov--Bohm effect not only in the main peak ($N=0$) but also in subpeaks ($N \ne 0$), indicating coherent transport through the polariton states. Our theory is also applicable to the DQD in the three-terminal geometry. We demonstrate the phase measurement through the irradiated QD and show that the measured phase shift changes continuously from 0 to $π$ around both the main peak and subpeaks.

</details>


### [66] [Floquet-Engineered Chern Insulator in two-dimensional $d_{x^2-y^2}$-Wave Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26632)
*Hosein Cheraghchi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本论文通过Floquet工程在圆偏振光照下的二维$d_{x^2-y^2}$波交变磁体（altermagnet）中实现了光控量子反常霍尔相（quantum anomalous Hall phase），陈数（Chern number）可达$\pm 3$，并建立了相应的相图（phase diagram），展示了交变磁体作为非平衡拓扑态（nonequilibrium topological states）平台的潜力。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在二维$d_{x^2-y^2}$波交变磁体中，通过圆偏振光的非共振辐照实现Floquet工程化拓扑相（topological phases）的可能性，并揭示其低能连续极限下的自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和类塞曼磁化（Zeeman-like magnetization）机制。

Method: 采用晶格模型（lattice model）结合Floquet理论（Floquet theory）描述交变磁体在圆偏振光辐照下的电子结构；通过计算反常霍尔电导（anomalous Hall conductivity）以及纳米带（nanoribbon）版本中的边缘模（edge modes）来验证光诱导的拓扑相图；并在低能连续极限下对Floquet哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）进行展开分析。

Result: 光辐照诱导出陈数高达$\pm 3$的量子反常霍尔相；相图通过反常霍尔电导和纳米带边缘模得到验证；低能连续极限下，出现了线性和高阶动量依赖的自旋-轨道耦合以及类塞曼磁化；高阶自旋-轨道耦合产生了额外的无质量狄拉克点（gapless Dirac points），与高对称性能隙闭合（gap-closing）共同增强了贝里曲率（Berry curvature）和高陈数；光照有效打破了静态$d_{x^2-y^2}$波磁对称性，混入了各向同性的光致$s$波修正。

Conclusion: $d$波交变磁体被确认为实现非平衡拓扑物态（nonequilibrium topological states of matter）的有前景的平台，光辐照可作为调控拓扑性质的灵活手段。

Abstract: We investigate Floquet-engineered topological phases in two-dimensional $d_{x^2-y^2}$-wave altermagnets irradiated by circularly polarized light in the off-resonant regime. These materials exhibit large momentum-dependent spin-splitting governed by distinctive magnetic symmetries. Using a lattice model combined with Floquet theory, we demonstrate that irradiation induces the light-tunable quantum anomalous Hall phases with the Chern numbers up to $\pm 3$. The resultant phase diagram is verified by calculating the anomalous Hall conductivity and also the edge modes inside the band gap of a nanoribbon version of the altermagnet. Our findings establish d-wave altermagnets as promising platforms for realizing nonequilibrium topological states of matter.
  The low-energy continuum limit of the lattice-based Floquet Hamiltonian results in a linear and higher-order-in-momentum spin-orbit couplings, and also a Zeeman-like magnetization, all arising from light-induced virtual photon processes. The resulting higher-order spin-orbit coupling generates the additional gapless Dirac points which, together with the high-symmetry gap-closings, yield enhanced Berry curvature and high Chern numbers. The light irradiation effectively breaks the static $d_{x^2-y^2}$-wave magnetic symmetry mixing in an isotropic photo-induced $s$-wave correction.

### [67] [Floquet Topological Phases and Anomalous Hall Signatures in Irradiated Two-dimensional $d_{xy}$-Wave Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26667)
*Hosein Cheraghchi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用晶格Floquet方法，研究了在圆偏振光驱动和外禀交换耦合面外磁化下，二维$d_{xy}$-波交变磁体（altermagnet）中的Floquet拓扑相。系统由驱动参数$\beta$控制，$|\beta|>1$时出现高对称点各向异性Dirac点，对应陈数（Chern number）$|\mathcal{C}|=2$；$|\beta|<1$时在布里渊区产生四族光致离对称$G$点，可实现$|\mathcal{C}|=4$的高阶陈相。低能分析揭示了$G$点处广义二维各向异性Dirac点的完全动量依赖赝自旋结构及其对贝里曲率（Berry curvature）分布的影响，同时指出反常霍尔电导（anomalous Hall conductivity）是金属态下这些Floquet拓扑相的实验特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非共振圆偏振光驱动的二维$d_{xy}$-波交变磁体在外禀交换耦合面外磁化条件下的Floquet拓扑相，分析驱动参数$\beta$如何控制拓扑相变与陈数变化。

Method: 采用晶格Floquet方法（lattice Floquet formulation）建立系统模型，结合低能有效分析（low-energy analysis）研究高对称点与$G$点处Dirac费米子（Dirac fermions）的能带结构和赝自旋（pseudospin）特征。

Result: $|\beta|>1$时，高对称点的各向异性Dirac点主导拓扑，陈数$|\mathcal{C}|=2$；$|\beta|<1$时，布里渊区出现四族光致$G$点，可实现$|\mathcal{C}|=4$的高阶陈相。$G$点实现具有完全动量依赖赝自旋结构的广义二维各向异性Dirac点，产生不同的贝里曲率分布。金属态下反常霍尔电导在局域能隙闭合区域附近表现出与贝里曲率累积对应的尖锐特征。

Conclusion: 驱动参数$\beta$可调控交变磁体中Floquet拓扑相的陈数（从$|\mathcal{C}|=2$到$|\mathcal{C}|=4$），$G$点Dirac点的赝自旋结构具有完全动量依赖性，与高对称点Dirac费米子本质不同。反常霍尔电导可作为这些Floquet拓扑相的实验可观测信号。

Abstract: We study Floquet topological phases in two-dimensional $d_{xy}$-wave altermagnets driven by off-resonant circularly polarized light and subject to an out-of-plane magnetization induced via extrinsic exchange coupling from a proximate ferromagnet. Using a lattice Floquet formulation, we show that the system is governed by a driving parameter $β$ that controls the emergence of distinct gap-closing points and associated topological phases. For $|β|>1$, topology is dominated by anisotropic Dirac points at high symmetry points, leading to Chern phases with $|\mathcal{C}|=2$. For $|β|<1$, light-induced off-symmetry $G$ points appear in four families in the Brillouine zone, enabling higher Chern phases up to $|\mathcal{C}|=4$.
  Low-energy analysis reveals that high symmetry points host anisotropic massive Dirac fermions, while $G$ points realize generalized two-dimensional anisotropic Dirac points with fully momentum-dependent pseudospin structure, leading to distinct Berry curvature distributions. In the metallic regime, the anomalous Hall conductivity provides an experimental signature of these Floquet topological phases, exhibiting sharp features associated with Berry curvature accumulation near local gap-closing regions.

### [68] [Perfect Absorption in the Strong Coupling Regime via Degenerate Critical Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26708)

Method: 通过对紧凑光子晶体（PhC）架构（集成二维半导体）中的麦克斯韦方程组进行严格求解，提出基于简并临界耦合（degenerate critical coupling）的单端口激子-极化激元（exciton-polariton）完美吸收通用方法。

Abstract: Perfect absorption (PA) represents a fundamental limit of light-matter interaction and a means to maximize nanoscale energy conversion. While PA is now a well-established phenomenon, both the theoretical feasibility and a practical mechanism for achieving it under single-beam excitation within the strong coupling regime is unknown. Through rigorous solution of Maxwells equations for a compact photonic crystal (PhC) architecture incorporating a two-dimensional semiconductor, we present a general method based on degenerate critical coupling for single-port PA of exciton-polaritons. At the crossing of two polariton branches, we achieve near-unity absorption exceeding 99.8 \% in a structure thinner than $100\,$nm. This effect is robust under realistic Gaussian beam excitation, and can be realized across different temperatures and excitonic materials by tailoring the PhC geometry. ### [69] [Rashba and Electrostatic Control of Charge-Visible Spin Demons in Two-Dimensional d-Wave Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26871)
*Muhammad Irfan Sarwar,Mohsin Raza,Kashif Sabeeh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本论文提出在二维d波交变磁体（d-wave altermagnet）中，通过结合Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）和静电栅极屏蔽（electrostatic gate screening），可以将原本电荷暗（charge-dark）的纵向自旋恶魔（longitudinal spin demon）模式调谐为电荷可见（charge-visible）的集体激发，同时保持其自旋主导特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Spin demons（自旋恶魔）是d波交变磁体中的声学集体模式，具有弱净电荷涨落，因此寿命长但难以被电荷敏感探针探测。论文旨在寻找一种方法，使这些原本电荷暗的模式能够被电荷探针观测到，从而为实验研究提供可行途径。

Method: 在Rashba-交变磁体连续介质模型（Rashba-altermagnetic continuum model）框架下，采用随机相位近似（random phase approximation, RPA）进行分析。Rashba耦合将自旋守恒问题转化为广义电荷-自旋响应问题，使密度通道与自旋通道之间的混合磁化率（mixed susceptibilities）变得有限；静电栅极屏蔽则独立调控库仑反馈，从而控制集体模式的色散关系（dispersion）和质量因子（quality factor）。

Result: Spin demon模式在中等自旋-轨道混合下仍然存活，具有有限的电荷可见性比（charge-visibility ratio），并在相关控制范围内保持主导的Sz自旋特征。Rashba强度和栅极距离的参数扫描显示电荷可见性与模式质量因子之间存在权衡关系，识别出激发仍保持欠阻尼（underdamped）且对电荷探针更可及的参数区间。

Conclusion: Rashba自旋-轨道耦合和静电屏蔽可作为二维交变磁体平台中可调谐、电荷可见的spin demons的控制机制，为这类长寿命集体模式的实验探测提供了理论途径。

Abstract: Spin demons in d-wave altermagnets are acoustic collective modes formed by nearly out-of-phase oscillations of spin-split quasiparticle populations. Their weak net charge fluctuation makes them long lived, but also makes them difficult to access with charge-sensitive probes. We propose a route to tune and brighten these modes in a two-dimensional d-wave altermagnet by combining Rashba spin-orbit coupling with electrostatic gate screening. Rashba coupling converts the spin-conserving problem into a generalized charge-spin response problem, in which mixed susceptibilities between density and spin channels become finite. As a result, the originally charge-dark longitudinal spin demon acquires finite charge spectral weight while remaining predominantly spin-like. Electrostatic gate screening provides an independent control of the Coulomb feedback and tunes the collectivemode dispersion and quality factor. Within a Rashba-altermagnetic continuum model and randomphase approximation, we show that the spin-demon ridge survives moderate spin-orbit mixing, develops a finite charge-visibility ratio, and retains dominant Sz character over the relevant control range. Parameter scans in Rashba strength and gate distance reveal a trade-off between charge visibility and mode quality, identifying regimes where the excitation remains underdamped while becoming more accessible to charge probes. These results establish Rashba spin-orbit coupling and electrostatic screening as control mechanisms for tunable, charge-visible spin demons in twodimensional altermagnetic platforms.

Result: MCS的自旋极化分布具有明确的特征：在垂直于面内磁场的方向上，两个MCS的自旋极化符号相反。局部电导的大小与非局部电导的符号分别与MCS自旋密度的符号以及探测探针的自旋极化精确关联。该技术还可探测SOTSC中边缘态等更高能量准粒子态的自旋密度分布。所有特征对强静态无序（static disorder）具有高度鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的自旋分辨输运协议为实验验证SOTSC中MCS及其他准粒子的自旋结构提供了清晰路径，并可用于检测MCS的辫子操作，这对推动拓扑量子计算具有重要价值。

Abstract: We investigate numerically the spin and transport properties of two-dimensional second-order topological superconductors (2D SOTSCs) hosting a pair of Majorana corner states (MCSs). First, we show that MCSs in the considered setup are characterized by a distinct spatial distribution of electronic spin polarization in the direction perpendicular to an applied in-plane magnetic field, with opposite signs for each MCS. Such a property can be used to label MCSs in a pair by their electronic spin. We propose a comprehensive spin-resolved transport protocol for measuring such a spin texture and further detecting the braiding (exchange) of a pair of MCSs, a crucial prerequisite for topological quantum computing. To be specific, we show that the magnitude of local conductance and the sign of nonlocal conductance are precisely linked to the sign of the electronic part of the MCS spin density and the spin polarization of the probe. Moreover, we show that the proposed technique can be used to detect the spin density profile of higher-energy quasiparticle states, e.g., edge states hosted in the SOTSC. We showed that all analyzed features are highly robust to strong static disorder , which makes our findings a clear experimental pathway to verify the spin structure of MCS and other quasiparticles hosted in SOTSCs.

Abstract: Commencing from the low-energy Bistritzer-MacDonald continuum model of twisted bi-layer graphene (tBLG) with proximity-induced Ising, Rashba, and intrinsic spin-orbit couplings (SOCs), we construct the corresponding Bogoliubov-de Gennes Hamiltonian with conventional $s$-wave pairing and theoretically investigate the emergence of topological superconductivity in it. ### [73] [Low-energy model for doped graphene nanoribbons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27102)
*J. Ferrer,A. García-Fuente,Y. Yang,S. Volosheniuk,H. S. J. van der Zant*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过将石墨烯纳米带（graphene nanoribbons）的扩展Hubbard模型和on-site Hubbard模型精确映射为包含铁磁交换和pair-hopping相互作用的Kanamori模型，解析求解了库仑矩阵元及其随宽度和长度的标度行为，并提出了低能Kanamori哈密顿量，可用于描述开放壳层、高自旋多体态及相应的壳层和自旋阻塞响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解自由悬挂掺杂石墨烯纳米带（化学势位于体单粒子带内）的多体行为（many-body behavior），为其在纳米电子学中作为输运通道的应用提供理论依据。

Method: 将扩展Hubbard模型和on-site Hubbard模型精确映射为包含铁磁交换（ferromagnetic exchange）和pair-hopping相互作用的Kanamori模型，并解析求解库仑矩阵元及其随纳米带宽度和长度的标度行为（scaling behavior）。

Result: 解析确定了库仑矩阵元及其标度行为，提出了低能Kanamori哈密顿量（low-energy Kanamori Hamiltonian），并发现该模型及纳米带参数可产生开放壳层、高自旋多体态（open-shell, high-spin many-body states）。

Conclusion: 所提出的模型和参数能够产生导致壳层阻塞（shell-blockade）和自旋阻塞（spin-blockade）响应的多体态，为石墨烯纳米带在纳米电子学中的输运应用奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: We analyse in this article the many-body behavior of free-standing doped graphene nanoribbons where the chemical potential lies inside the bulk single-particle bands. We perform an exact mapping from both an extended and an on-site Hubbard model of the ribbons to a Kanamori model, which includes ferromagnetic exchange and pair-hopping interactions. We determine the resulting Coulomb matrix elements analytically, and identify their scaling behavior as a function of ribbon width and length. We propose a low-energy version of the Kanamori Hamiltonian to address the response of the ribbons to external fields, with a view to their use as transport channels in nanoelectronics. We find that the model and the proposed ribbon parameters can produce open-shell, high-spin many-body states that can lead to shell- and spin-blockade responses.

</details>


### [74] [Magnetoresistance in chiral systems driven by inter-band spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27121)
*Misa Nozaki,Takatoshi Fujita*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过多带模型与GKSL主方程模拟，理论研究了非平衡稳态电流中的手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS），发现带间自旋-轨道耦合与在位库仑相互作用可产生超过25%的自旋极化，揭示了多带效应对CISS机制的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性诱导自旋选择性（chiral-induced spin selectivity, CISS）在自旋电子学中具有重要应用前景，但定量理解仍不充分，主要原因在于先前研究多依赖单带模型（single-band model），无法捕捉真实体系中的多带效应。

Method: 采用多带模型（multi-band model）理论框架，通过Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad（GKSL）主方程（master equation）模拟非平衡稳态电流，计算磁电阻-CISS中的自旋极化。

Result: 在现实的带间自旋-轨道耦合强度（inter-band spin-orbit coupling strength）下，同时存在在位库仑相互作用（on-site Coulomb interaction）时，自旋极化（spin polarization）可超过25%。

Conclusion: 带间自旋-轨道耦合（inter-band spin-orbit coupling）在CISS机制中扮演关键角色，该发现有助于推动对CISS的定量理解。

Abstract: Chiral-induced spin selectivity (CISS), in which electrons transmitted through nonmagnetic chiral materials exhibit strong spin-dependent transport, has attracted growing interest for spintronic applications. However, a quantitative understanding of CISS remains elusive, partly because most previous studies rely on single-band models. In this work, we theoretically investigate multi-band effects on magnetoresistance (MR)-CISS, which is typically observed in experiments using magnetic conductive atomic force microscopy. To evaluate the spin polarization in MR-CISS, we simulate the nonequilibrium steady-state current using the Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad master equation. We find that spin polarization exceeding 25\% can be achieved for realistic inter-band spin-orbit coupling strengths in the presence of on-site Coulomb interactions. These findings highlight the crucial role of inter-band spin-orbit coupling in the mechanism of CISS.

### [75] [Phase-Shifted Planar Hall and Magnetoresistive Responses in Weyl Semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27167)
*Sandip Bera,Sudhansu S. Mandal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过图解Kubo公式（diagrammatic Kubo-formula approach）识别出外尔半金属（Weyl semimetals）中一个被半经典描述忽略的固有二次磁场（quadratic magnetic-field）贡献，解释了平面霍尔（planar Hall）电阻率和磁电阻率（magnetoresistivity）实验中观测到的异常角度依赖性，即极值偏移和符号反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论预期外尔半金属的平面霍尔电阻率和磁电阻率分别呈现 $\sin 2φ$ 和 $\cos 2φ$ 的角度依赖，但实验发现了平面霍尔信号的极值偏移以及磁电阻率在 $φ< π/4$ 时的符号反转，这些异常现象无法被传统半经典描述（semiclassical description）解释，亟需理论上的微观机制阐明。

Method: 采用图解Kubo公式（diagrammatic Kubo-formula approach）对平面输运响应进行微观计算，识别出传统半经典描述中缺失的、与磁场二次方成正比的固有贡献（intrinsic quadratic magnetic-field contribution）。

Result: 该固有贡献在横向电导率（transverse conductivity）和纵向电导率（longitudinal conductivity）中分别引入与 $\cos 2φ$ 和 $\sin 2φ$ 成正比的附加项，导致平面霍尔和磁电阻响应均呈现相移形式 $\sin 2(φ+φ_r)$ 和 $\cos 2(φ+φ_r)$。从纵向和横向响应中独立提取的相同相移 $φ_r$ 能够定量描述现有实验数据。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了外尔半金属中观测到的异常角度依赖性的微观起源（microscopic origin），指出该效应源于一个固有的二次磁场贡献，而非传统半经典图像所能涵盖。

Abstract: The planar Hall resistivity and magnetoresistivity of Weyl semimetals are conventionally expected to exhibit $\sin 2φ$ and $\cos2φ$ angular dependences, respectively, where $φ$ is the angle between electric and magnetic fields. However, experiments reveal shifted extrema in the planar Hall signal and sign reversals in magnetoresistivity at $φ< π/4$. Here, using a diagrammatic Kubo-formula approach, we identify an intrinsic quadratic magnetic-field contribution to the planar transport response that is absent in conventional semiclassical description. This contribution introduces an additional term proportional to $\cos 2 φ$ and $\sin 2φ$, respectively, in transverse and longitudinal conductivities. Consequently, both planar Hall and magnetoresistive responses acquire a phase-shifted form $\sin 2(φ+φ_r)$ and $\cos 2(φ+φ_r)$, respectively. The same phase shift extracted independently from longitudinal and transverse responses quantitatively describes available experimental data. Our results establish a microscopic origin of the anomalous angular dependence observed in Weyl semimetals.

</details>


### [76] [Strong coupling between propagating spin wave and microwave photons in a superconducting resonator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27279)
*Yi Li,Jinho Lim,Xingzhi Wang,Tomas Polakovic,Carissa Kiehl,Moojune Song,Phuoc Cao Van,Ralu Divan,Ulrich Welp,Charudatta Phatak,Jong-Ryul Jeong,Kab-Jin Kim,Jian-Min Zuo,Axel Hoffmann,Valentine Novosad*

Conclusion: 该工作展示了将自旋波非互易性（spin-wave nonreciprocity）引入混合量子系统的可能性，为整合自旋波量子学与腔量子学（cavity magnonics）以及开发量子信息科学中的应用开辟了新方向。

Abstract: We demonstrate strong coupling between propagating spin wave modes and microwave photons in superconducting resonator-magnetic thin film hybrid circuits. By fabricating the resonator directly on yttrium iron garnet thin films grown on rare-earth-free Y$_3$Sc$_2$Ga$_3$O$_{12}$ substrates, we achieve strong coupling of both Damon-Eshbach and backward-volume spin wave modes to the resonator, with coupling strengths exceeding both the magnon and photon damping rates. Furthermore, we observe nonreciprocal spin wave radiation of the hybrid magnonic mode in the Damon-Eshbach configuration, highlighting the potential for incorporating intrinsic spin-wave nonreciprocity into hybrid magnonic systems. These results open new avenues for integrating spin-wave magnonics with cavity magnonics, and for harnessing spin waves for potential applications in quantum information science.

### [77] [Specific absorption rate of uniaxial single-domain nanomagnets: stochastic spin dynamics versus linear response theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27351)
*H. Kachkachi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过随机Langevin-Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert数值模拟与基于Debye磁化率的线性响应理论两种方法，计算了单轴单畴纳米磁体在交变磁场下的比吸收率，发现两者在小场幅值时等价，但在不同频率-弛豫时间乘积下存在显著偏差：低频时LRT高估、高频时LRT可低估高达~70%，偏差由无量纲乘积ωτ_N和线性参数ξ共同决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性纳米颗粒在交变磁场中的比吸收率（specific absorption rate, SAR）对磁热疗等应用至关重要，但广泛使用的线性响应理论（linear response theory, LRT）在大场幅值下的适用性缺少定量评估。本文旨在系统比较LRT与全随机Langevin模拟（LLL方法）的差异，明确LRT的适用范围与偏差大小。

Method: 采用两种方法计算单轴单畴纳米磁体在交变磁场下的SAR：(i)直接对随机Langevin-Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert方程（LLL方法）进行数值积分；(ii)基于Debye磁化率（Debye susceptibility）与Néel弛豫时间τ_N的线性响应理论（LRT）。首先从解析上证明两者在小场幅值下等价，随后定义偏差Λ ≡ SAR_LLL/SAR_LRT − 1，作为磁场幅值和温度的函数进行数值计算。

Result: 在小场幅值下两种方法等价。偏差Λ的符号与大小由无量纲乘积ωτ_N（其中ω为驱动频率）以及线性参数ξ = μ_s B_0/(k_B T)共同决定。在共振以下（ωτ_N < 1），LRT高估SAR；在共振以上（ωτ_N > 1，即阻塞纳米颗粒的典型区域），LRT可低估SAR，在ξ ~ 2时偏差高达约70%。

Conclusion: 该工作为磁热疗及相关纳米尺度热输运问题中线性响应理论的使用提供了定量指导，同时可作为单颗粒基准，为后续向多自旋体系及相互作用体系扩展奠定基础。

Abstract: We compute the specific absorption rate of a uniaxial single-domain nanomagnet driven by an alternating magnetic field by two methods: i) direct numerical integration of the stochastic (Langevin) Landau--Lifshitz--Gilbert equation (the LLL approach), and ii) linear response theory (LRT) based on the Debye susceptibility with the Néel relaxation time $τ_\mathrm{N}$. We first analytically show that both methods are equivalent for small magnetic field amplitude, and then compute their deviation $Λ\equiv \mathrm{SAR}_{\mathrm{LLL}}/\mathrm{SAR}_{\mathrm{LRT}}-1$ as a function of the magnetic field amplitude for two temperatures chosen on opposite sides of the Debye resonance. One of the main results is that the sign and magnitude of $Λ$ are governed by the dimensionless product $ωτ_\mathrm{N}$, in addition to the linearity parameter $ξ=μ_{s}B_{0}/k_{B}T$ for the easy-axis geometry considered here. Indeed, below resonance ($ωτ_\mathrm{N}<1$), linear response theory overestimates the specific absorption rate. In contrast, above resonance ($ωτ_\mathrm{N}>1$, the regime typical of blocked nanoparticles), linear response theory can underestimate the specific absorption rate by up to $\sim70\%$ at $ξ\sim2$. We expect this work to provide quantitative guidance for the use of linear response theory in magnetic hyperthermia and related nanoscale heat-transport problems, and to serve as a single-particle benchmark for extensions to many-spin and interacting systems.

</details>

### [78] [A semi-analytic model of the bouncing barrier for protoplanetary dust aggregates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26491)
*Sota Arakawa,Haruto Oshiro,Yuki Yoshida,Kiwamu Yoshii*

Main category: astro-ph.EP

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个半解析模型，用于计算原行星盘中尘埃聚合体的碰撞粘附概率，并基于最弱环节统计（weakest-link statistics）解释了较大聚合体更容易反弹的机制。模型校准后能够复现离散元模拟的粘附-反弹边界，且预测的反弹屏障与ALMA观测推断的尺度-速度范围一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原行星盘中尘埃聚合体的碰撞反弹限制了其增长，但反弹行为对聚合体大小、碰撞速度和填充因子（filling factor）的依赖关系尚不清晰。现有研究缺乏能够同时捕捉压缩与分离阶段物理机制的半解析模型。

Method: 将每次聚合体碰撞分为压缩阶段和分离阶段。压缩阶段采用弹塑性接触模型（elastoplastic contact model），确定最大接触半径和压缩后的排斥能；分离阶段将颗粒间键的断裂处理为随机网络的断裂过程，并使用最弱环节统计评估断裂能。

Result: 模型自然预测出较大聚合体更容易反弹，因为较大的接触区域更可能包含弱键。与离散元方法模拟对比表明，模型能复现模拟得到的粘附-反弹边界。将校准后的模型应用于ALMA观测推断的中等多孔聚合体，预测的反弹屏障（bouncing barrier）恰好在观测推断的尺度-速度范围内。

Conclusion: 该半解析模型为预测原行星盘尘埃聚合体的碰撞演化提供了一个有用的理论框架。

Abstract: Collisional bouncing limits the growth of dust aggregates in protoplanetary disks, but its dependence on aggregate size, collision velocity, and filling factor remains poorly understood. Here we develop a semi-analytic model for the sticking probability of colliding dust aggregates. We divide each aggregate collision into two phases: a compression phase and a separation phase. The compression phase is described with an elastoplastic contact model, which determines the maximum contact radius and repulsive energy after compression. The separation phase is treated as fracture of a stochastic network of interparticle bonds, whose fracture energy is evaluated using weakest-link statistics. The model naturally predicts that larger aggregates bounce more readily because larger contact regions are more likely to contain weak bonds. Comparison with distinct element method simulations shows that the model reproduces the simulated sticking--bouncing boundary. Furthermore, applying the calibrated model to moderately porous aggregates inferred from ALMA observations of protoplanetary disks, we find that the predicted bouncing barrier passes through the observationally inferred size--velocity range. Thus, our semi-analytic model provides a useful framework for predicting the collisional evolution of protoplanetary dust aggregates.

</details>

### [80] [Physical Neural Networks Need Nonlinearity, Amplification, and Suppression for Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26989)

Abstract: The exponential growth in energy consumption of artificial intelligence systems has spurred interest in physical computing paradigms that exploit the relaxation of physical systems toward steady states. However, many existing physical networks are fundamentally linear and incapable of performing nonlinear operations crucial for meaningful machine learning tasks. Here we use simulations to show that nonlinearity alone is insufficient; physical learning systems must also support signal amplification and suppression to perform nontrivial computations. We present physically plausible circuit designs that incorporate these essential features, enabling effective nonlinear information processing. Our findings clarify the limitations of linear physical networks and provide guidance for developing energy-efficient physical learning architectures capable of general machine learning tasks.
