### [81] [Electric-Field Switchable Magnetic Spin Hall Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26988)
*Mingbo Dou,Xu Chen,Qin Zhang,Xianjie Wang,Xue-Zeng Lu,Jia Zhang,L. L. Tao*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文通过自旋群（spin-group）分析，证明铁电交变磁体（ferroelectric altermagnets）中的时间反演奇（$\mathcal{T}$-odd）磁自旋霍尔效应（magnetic spin Hall effect）可由电场而非仅由时间反演操作切换，源于铁电开关引起的非相对论自旋劈裂（nonrelativistic spin splitting）反转，并在VOI$_2$单层中通过密度泛函理论（DFT）和有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）分析加以验证，为低功耗电控自旋电子器件提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为时间反演奇（$\mathcal{T}$-odd）物理量的极性只能通过时间反演操作（$\mathcal{T}$ operation）翻转。作者希望探索是否可以利用电场（而非耗散性的磁场或自旋流）来实现$\mathcal{T}$-odd磁自旋霍尔效应的开关，从而为低功耗可编程自旋电子器件提供新策略。

Method: 采用自旋群（spin-group）分析，直接证明铁电交变磁体中$\mathcal{T}$-odd磁自旋霍尔效应可由电场切换；推导非中心对称自旋点群（non-centrosymmetric spin point groups）中同时切换极化和磁自旋霍尔效应的自旋群操作；结合密度泛函理论（DFT）计算和有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）分析，以铁电交变磁体VOI$_2$单层为实例进行验证。

Result: 发现铁电切换会导致非相对论自旋劈裂反转，从而交换倒易空间（reciprocal space）中自旋向上和自旋向下通道的角色；因此，与自旋极化电导差成正比的$\mathcal{T}$-odd自旋电导率（spin conductivity）会在极化切换时反转极性；在VOI$_2$单层中具体验证了上述现象。

Conclusion: 研究不仅提供了利用无耗散电场切换磁自旋霍尔效应的新颖策略，也为电可编程自旋电子器件（electrically programmable spintronic devices）开辟了有前景的发展方向。

Abstract: It is established that the polarity of a time-reversal-odd ($\mathcal{T}$-odd) physical quantity can be reversed under the $\mathcal{T}$ operation. Here, we use the spin-group analysis to directly demonstrate that the $\mathcal{T}$-odd magnetic spin Hall effect in ferroelectric altermagnets can be switchable by electric fields beyond the $\mathcal{T}$ operation. This arises from the ferroelectric switching of the nonrelativistic spin splitting, which swaps the roles of spin up and down channels in the reciprocal space. As a result, the $\mathcal{T}$-odd spin conductivity that are proportional to the spin-polarized conductivity difference reverses its polarity upon polarization switching. We identify spin-group operations to switch both the polarization and the magnetic spin Hall effect simultaneously for non-centrosymmetric spin point groups. Then, we exemplify those phenomena in the ferroelectric altermagnet VOI$_2$ monolayer based on density functional theory calculations and an effective Hamiltonian analysis. Our findings not only provide novel strategies to switch the magnetic spin Hall effect using the dissipation-free electric field but also open a promising avenue for electrically programmable spintronic devices.

</details>

### [82] [Quantum statistics on atom-ion Feshbach resonances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26995)
*Joachim Siemund,Fabian Thielemann,Jonathan Grieshaber,Wei Wu,Patrick Mullan,Panagiotis Giannakeas,Krzysztof Jachymski,Tobias Schaetz*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过将单个Ba⁺离子浸入Li原子双组分费米气体中，在原子-离子Feshbach共振附近测量三体复合损失率，发现离子损失率对自旋极化呈现显著非线性依赖，表明全同费米子复合路径的贡献被抑制。实验结果支持两步复合图像和绝热超球面方法，证明了交换对称性效应在热平均下依然保持稳健。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子统计（quantum statistics）在原子-原子-离子三体复合（three-body recombination）中的作用，并验证交换对称性（exchange symmetry）是否能在热平均条件下保持可观测效应。

Method: 将单个Ba⁺离子浸入Li原子双组分费米气体（two-component Fermi gas）中，在原子-离子Feshbach共振（atom-ion Feshbach resonance）附近，通过改变自旋组成（在恒定密度和温度下）来调控量子统计效应，并测量离子损失率。

Result: 测得的离子损失率对自旋极化呈现显著非线性依赖，表明涉及全同费米子的复合路径贡献已被压低。该现象在实验可观测量的层面上即可显现。

Conclusion: 实验结果与两步复合模型和绝热超球面方法（adiabatic hyperspherical approach）一致，其中反对称化（antisymmetrization）限制了可用入射通道，并在不可区分的复合路径之间产生干涉。该工作将原子-离子系统确立为通过量子统计控制三体碰撞的平台，并表明交换对称性效应即使在热平均掩盖了底层阈值律行为的情况下仍然稳健。

Abstract: We investigate three-body recombination in a hybrid atom-ion system consisting of a single trapped Ba$^+$ ion immersed in a two-component Fermi gas of Li atoms near an atom-ion Feshbach resonance. By tuning the spin composition at constant density and temperature, we isolate the role of quantum statistics in atom-atom-ion collisions. The measured ion loss rate exhibits a pronounced nonlinear dependence on spin polarization, revealing a reduced contribution of recombination pathways involving identical fermions already at the level of experimental observables. The observations are consistent with a two-step recombination picture and an adiabatic hyperspherical approach, where antisymmetrization restricts the available entrance channels and gives rise to interference between indistinguishable recombination pathways. Our work establishes atom-ion systems as a platform for controlling three-body collisions via quantum statistics and demonstrates that exchange-symmetry effects remain robust even under thermal averaging that obscures the underlying threshold-law behavior.

### [83] [The fate of odd-parity magnetism in one dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26222)
*Kasper Rettedal Eikeland,Sondre Duna Lundemo,Asle Sudbø*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在玻色化（bosonization）框架下构建了一维p波磁体（p-wave magnet）模型，该模型由扩展哈伯德模型（extended Hubbard model）的巡游电子与局域磁矩链通过近藤耦合（Kondo exchange）构成。分析表明，自旋链呈现出与p波磁体对称性一致的准长程序（quasi long-range order），该序在特定电子填充下诱导出附加相互作用，赋予电子谱函数（spectral function）显著的p波特征；在非公度填充下，该相互作用成为无关项，p波特征随之消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一维p波磁体（p-wave magnet）中巡游电子与局域磁矩耦合系统的奇特物性，特别是由对称性驱动的准长程序如何影响电子行为。

Method: 采用玻色化（bosonization）框架，将扩展哈伯德模型描述的巡游电子与通过近藤耦合（Kondo exchange）连接的局域磁矩链进行玻色化处理，转化为耦合的Luttinger液体（Luttinger liquids）描述，并分析弱耦合相图（weak-coupling phase diagram）。

Result: 自旋链展现出与p波磁体联合时间反演-平移对称性（combined time-reversal and translation symmetry）一致的准长程序（quasi long-range order）。该序在特定电子填充（commensurate filling）下产生公度条件（commensurability condition），引入附加相互作用，使电子谱函数（spectral function）呈现显著p波特征（p-wave character）；在非公度填充下，这些相互作用变为无关项（irrelevant），p波特征消失。

Conclusion: 在一维p波磁体系统中，电子填充的公度性是实现电子p波特征的关键条件，填充偏离公度值将破坏该特征。该结果揭示了磁序与电子填充之间的深刻相互制约关系。

Abstract: We consider a one-dimensional model for a $p$-wave magnet within the bosonization framework. The model consists of itinerant electrons described by an extended Hubbard model coupled to a chain of localized moments through the Kondo exchange. The classical ground state of the local-moment system captures the salient features of an odd-parity magnet. By bosonizing the coupled system, a description in terms of coupled Luttinger liquids follows, giving rise to a rich weak-coupling phase diagram. It is shown that the spin chain develops quasi long-range order consistent with the combined time-reversal and translation symmetry defining the $p$-wave magnet. We highlight the peculiar role played by this order in establishing a commensurability condition on the electronic filling under which additional interactions appear in the bosonic field theory. It is demonstrated that these interactions endow the electron spectral function with a pronounced $p$-wave character. Away from commensurate filling, these interactions are rendered irrelevant and the ensuing $p$-wave character is lost.

</details>


### [84] [Toric code made subsystem: a framework for topological subsystem codes using anticommuting quantum spin liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26226)
*Vaibhav Sharma,Sumiran Pujari*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于反交换量子自旋液体（anticommuting quantum spin liquid）的拓扑子系统码（topological subsystem code）构建框架。该代码通过将环面码（toric code）进行空间修改，使其丧失稳定子码（stabilizer code）性质，转而依赖大量反交换局域守恒算符产生的亚系统自由度（subsystem degrees of freedom）。在方格和kagome晶格上给出了具体构造实例，分别需要重量-4和重量-3的局域校验算符（check operator）测量。该码的独特之处在于，除逻辑量子比特外，还拥有大量未被校验算符扰动的局域规范量子比特（local gauge qubit）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有拓扑子系统码的构造方法有限，缺乏基于反交换量子自旋液体的系统性框架。本文旨在填补这一空白，提供一种可在多种晶格或图几何上生成新型拓扑子系统码的通用模板。

Method: 从[Phys. Rev. B 113, 064402 (2026)]中描述的反交换量子自旋液体类出发，将其中典范模型视为环面码（toric code）的空间修改，利用其大量反交换局域守恒算符及由此产生的巨量基态简并（extensive ground state degeneracy）来构建子系统自由度。在方格和kagome晶格上给出了具体构造，分别涉及重量-4和重量-3的局域校验算符。

Result: 提出了两种具体的拓扑子系统码构造：一种在方格几何上，校验算符重量为4；另一种在kagome晶格几何上，校验算符重量为3。这些代码继承了量子自旋液体的多体拓扑序（many-body topological order），属于拓扑子系统码。与其他子系统码相比，其独特性质在于存在大量不被校验算扰动的局域规范量子比特。

Conclusion: 该框架为在不同晶格或图几何上生成新型拓扑子系统码提供了通用模板，有望适用于多种量子硬件平台。

Abstract: We introduce a framework of constructing topological subsystem codes based on the class of anticommuting quantum spin liquids described in [Phys. Rev. B 113, 064402 (2026)]. A canonical model from this class can be considered as a spatial modification of the toric code that voids its stabilizer code property. Rather, these models contain an extensive set of anticommuting local conserved operators that lead to an extensive ground state degeneracy. This degeneracy forms the basis of the subsystem degrees of freedom in the associated quantum error correcting code. The code inherits the many-body topological order of the quantum spin liquid, making it a topological subsystem code. We present two concrete and detailed examples for constructing these codes on a square lattice and a kagome lattice geometry, requiring weight-4 and weight-3 local check operator measurements respectively. In contrast to other subsystem codes, a unique property of these codes is the presence of an extensive number of local gauge qubits that are left undisturbed by the check operators apart from the logical qubits. Our construction provides a template for generating this new category of topological subsystem codes on different lattice or graph geometries, suitable for implementation on various quantum hardware platforms.

</details>


### [85] [Bobkingite, a new coupled sawtooth chain platform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26243)
*P. Peter Stavropoulos,Aleksandar Razpopov,Harrison LaBollita,Michael R. Norman,Antia S. Botana,Roser Valentí*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算发现矿物 bobkingite (\ce{Cu5(OH)8Cl2(H2O)2}) 可作为锯齿链（sawtooth chain）模型的准一维磁性实现材料，其三维相互作用被晶体几何强烈抑制，并可能表现出有限温经典自旋液体（classical spin liquid）行为及降维级联相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找锯齿链（sawtooth chain）模型的真实材料载体，以研究该几何阻挫（geometric frustration）系统的奇特磁性行为。现有锯齿链候选材料存在垂直链间耦合（vertical interchain coupling）过强等问题，bobkingite 可能提供更干净的实验平台。

Method: 采用第一性原理（ab initio）方法计算 bobkingite 的磁交换耦合参数，并分析其完整交换网络；对经典自旋模型进行简并态构型分析，并使用自旋波理论（spin-wave theory）研究量子涨落的领头阶效应。

Result: bobkingite 中存在准一维锯齿链，残余三维相互作用被晶体几何强烈抑制。经典模型展示出具有涌现二维特征的大量近乎简并态；自旋波理论表明这些简并态在量子涨落领头阶下以伊辛自由度（Ising degrees of freedom）持续存在。与其它锯齿链候选材料不同，bobkingite 的垂直链间耦合可忽略，即使在有序态中仍保持一维简并性，暗示任何长程序（long-range order）都很弱。

Conclusion: 热涨落可能在 bobkingite 中稳定有限温经典自旋液体态，冷却过程中将发生级联相变（cascade of transitions），系统依次进入更低维度的简并态。bobkingite 是一个极具吸引力的研究锯齿链物理的实验平台。

Abstract: We investigate the mineral bobkingite, \ce{Cu5(OH)8Cl2(H2O)2}, as a potential realization of the sawtooth chain. Using \textit{ab initio} methods, we estimate the magnetic exchange couplings and find that bobkingite hosts quasi-one-dimensional sawtooth chains, with residual three-dimensional interactions strongly suppressed by the crystal geometry. Examining the full exchange network, we find that the classical model exhibits an extensive manifold of nearly degenerate states with emergent two-dimensional character, which spin-wave theory shows to persist to leading order in quantum fluctuations as Ising degrees of freedom. Unlike other sawtooth candidates, bobkingite has negligible vertical interchain coupling, preserving a one-dimensional degeneracy even in the presence of ordering, suggesting that any long-range order is weak. Thermal fluctuations may thus stabilize a finite-temperature classical spin liquid regime, with a cascade of transitions upon cooling into successively lower-dimensional degenerate states, making bobkingite a compelling platform for exploring sawtooth chain physics.

</details>


### [86] [Odd-parity electronic order near the semiconductor limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26338)
*Jack Tregidga,Dibyata Rout,Johannes Hielscher,Josiah Turner,Stephen D. Wilson,John W. Harter*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究在磷化物半导体家族 LnCd₃P₃（Ln = La, Ce, Pr, Nd）中发现了由稀薄载流子驱动的自发奇宇称电子有序相，通过光学二次谐波产生、超快瞬态反射率测量和密度泛函理论建模，揭示了该相涉及对称性破缺和费米面畸变，为稀载流子半导体中的相互作用驱动宇称破缺提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找稀薄载流子（dilute carriers）经历强库仑相互作用的材料平台，是探索相互作用驱动量子相（interaction-driven quantum phases）的核心挑战。弱载流子屏蔽可诱发超越常规费米液体（Fermi liquid）范式的多种集体不稳定性，但此类稀薄强相互作用电子体系的实验实现仍极为稀缺。

Method: 利用光学二次谐波产生（optical second harmonic generation, SHG）观测体反演和旋转对称性破缺以及面内极轴的出现；采用二次谐波显微镜（second harmonic microscopy）识别由 120° 旋转联系的三个畴变体；通过超快瞬态反射率测量（ultrafast transient reflectivity measurements）探测跃迁过程中的电子重构；结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）建立价态的四带模型（four-band model）。

Result: 在轻自空穴掺杂的 LnCd₃P₃ 化合物中观测到自发奇宇称相变；该有序相仅在轻自空穴掺杂样品中出现，在绝缘的 SmCd₃P₃ 中不存在。四带模型表明适度的相互作用即可稳定奇宇称电子有序（odd-parity electronic order），该相同时包含自发费米面畸变（spontaneous Fermi surface distortion）和动量依赖的双层极化（momentum-dependent bilayer polarization），从而打破反演对称性。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了在稀载流子半导体中实现相互作用驱动宇称破缺的路径，并将蜂窝状双层体系（honeycomb bilayer systems）识别为奇宇称电子相的有前景平台。

Abstract: Identifying materials platforms in which dilute carriers experience strong Coulomb interactions is a central challenge in the search for interaction-driven quantum phases. In such systems, weak carrier screening can promote a variety of collective instabilities beyond the conventional Fermi liquid paradigm, including superconductivity, Wigner crystallization, and odd-parity electronic order. Experimental realizations of such dilute, strongly interacting electronic systems remain rare in crystalline materials. Here we report a spontaneous odd-parity phase transition in the phosphide semiconductor family $\textit{Ln}$Cd$_3$P$_3$ ($\textit{Ln}$ = La, Ce, Pr, Nd). Using optical second harmonic generation, we observe the onset of bulk inversion and rotational symmetry breaking accompanied by the emergence of an in-plane polar axis. Second harmonic microscopy reveals three domain variants related by 120$^\circ$ rotations, while ultrafast transient reflectivity measurements uncover a pronounced electronic reconstruction across the transition. Remarkably, the ordered phase appears only in lightly self-hole-doped compounds and is absent in insulating SmCd$_3$P$_3$, indicating an essential role for itinerant carriers despite their extremely low concentration. Guided by density functional theory, we develop a four-band model of the valence states and show that modest interactions can stabilize odd-parity electronic order. The resulting phase combines a spontaneous Fermi surface distortion with a momentum-dependent bilayer polarization that breaks inversion symmetry. Our results establish a route to interaction-driven parity breaking in dilute-carrier semiconductors and identify honeycomb bilayer systems as a promising platform for odd-parity electronic phases.

</details>


### [87] [Coexistence of static order and spin dynamics in an S = 5/2 frustrated triangular antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26921)
*U. Jena,B. Sana,Satish Kumar,M. Pregelj,A. Bandyopadhyay,P. Manuel,J. S. Lord,D. T. Adroja,P. Khuntia*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过热力学、μSR、中子衍射实验及第一性原理计算，系统研究了三角晶格反铁磁体MnSnB₂O₆中的磁有序与低能激发，发现其有序态符合3D Ising型反铁磁，并在有序态下方观察到反常幂律比热行为C∝T^{1.37}及持续的自旋动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阻挫三角晶格反铁磁体（frustrated triangular-lattice antiferromagnet）在高自旋经典极限下，竞争交换作用、各向异性与集体自由度之间的耦合可导致非传统低能激发、反常临界行为及持续动力学响应，但迄今缺乏高质量模型体系的实验验证。

Method: 综合运用热力学测量（比热、磁化率）、μSR（μ子自旋弛豫，muon spin relaxation）实验、中子衍射实验以及第一性原理计算（first-principles calculation），对近乎完美的二维三角晶格反铁磁材料MnSnB₂O₆（Mn²⁺, S=5/2）进行表征。

Result: 居里-外斯拟合给出居里-外斯温度θ_CW ≈ -12 K，表明Mn²⁺间以反铁磁相互作用为主；比热在T_N ≈ 1 K处出现长程磁有序转变，并在有序态下方呈现反常幂律行为C ∝ T^{1.37}；零场μSR在50 mK以下证实磁有序的存在，并与静磁有序共存持续的自旋动力学；中子衍射显示序参量的温度演化符合3D Ising型反铁磁图像。

Conclusion: MnSnB₂O₆是一个近乎理想的二维三角晶格反铁磁模型体系，其有序态表现为3D Ising型反铁磁，并伴随非平凡的低能激发与持续自旋动力学，为研究竞争交换相互作用驱动的涌现现象提供了理想的实验平台。

Abstract: Frustrated triangular-lattice antiferromagnets in the classical high-spin limit provide a paradigmatic setting in which the interplay of competing exchange interactions, anisotropy, and collective degrees of freedom can lead to unconventional low-energy excitations, anomalous criticality, and persistent dynamical responses. Here, we present comprehensive thermodynamic, $μ$SR, and neutron diffraction experiments, along with first-principles calculations, on a triangular-lattice antiferromagnet, MnSnB$_2$O$_6$, where Mn$^{2+}$ ($S=5/2$) moments form a nearly perfect 2D triangular network without any anti-site disorder. The Curie-Weiss fit to the magnetic susceptibility yields a moderate Curie-Weiss temperature of $-12$ K, indicating dominant antiferromagnetic interactions between Mn$^{2+}$ moments, which is supported by first-principles calculations. Specific-heat measurements reveal the onset of long-range magnetic order at $T_{\rm N}\approx 1$ K, which is ascribed to intraplane exchange interactions. The specific heat exhibits pronounced short-range correlations above $T_{\rm N}$ and an unconventional power-law behavior, $C\propto T^{1.37}$, deep in the ordered state, suggesting the presence of non-trivial low-energy excitations. Zero-field $μ$SR experiments down to 50~mK confirm the presence of magnetic ordering below $T_{\rm N}$, in agreement with thermodynamic and neutron diffraction experiments. The $μ$SR measurements detect persistent spin dynamics coexisting with static magnetic order. The temperature evolution of the order parameter down to 50~mK from neutron diffraction suggests that the ordered state is consistent with a 3D Ising-like antiferromagnet. This family of archetypal frustrated magnets offers a promising venue for the experimental realization of emergent phenomena governed by competing exchange interactions and exotic low-energy excitations.

</details>


### [88] [Hidden-ordered Dirac fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27368)
*Bitan Roy*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种Lorentz对称Dirac理论的Hermitian扩展，通过引入另一个反交换的类质量Dirac算符，定义了一类新的对称保护准粒子激发——隐序Dirac费米子（hidden-ordered Dirac fermions）。该理论在任意维度下均呈现线性能量-动量关系，且隐序会重整化费米速度并推动量子相变向绝缘态发展，但在量子临界点附近隐序可能存续或消失，取决于绝缘序参量与类质量Dirac算符之间的代数结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Lorentz对称Dirac理论的Hermitian扩展，发现一类由隐藏有序（hidden ordering）保护的新型狄拉克准粒子激发，并理解其对称性保护机制、响应特性及在量子临界点附近的行为。

Method: 通过补充一个反交换的类质量Dirac算符（masslike anticommuting Dirac operator）到标准Dirac哈密顿量中，构建Hermitian扩展的理论框架；基于内部代数结构分析隐序对量子相变的影响；构造格点模型（lattice models）以实现该理论。

Result: 该理论在任意维度下均保持线性能量-动量关系；隐序在d>1时会将量子相变推向更强耦合的绝缘态；隐序在量子临界点附近的存续与否取决于绝缘序参量与类质量Dirac算符之间的内部代数关系。

Conclusion: 提出了隐序Dirac费米子这一新的准粒子概念，其响应行为与原始Dirac系统类似但费米速度被重整化；建立了相应的格点模型，并指出了数值与实验上可验证该理论预测的平台。

Abstract: I propose a Hermitian extension of the Lorentz-symmetric Dirac theory by complementing the associated Hamiltonian with another \emph{masslike} anticommuting Dirac operator. The resulting theory manifests the iconic linear energy-momentum relationship in any dimension ($d$) and hence the emergent nodal quasiparticle excitations are named \emph{hidden-ordered Dirac fermions}, which are symmetry protected and their responses are analogous to those in original Dirac systems, however, in terms of a renormalized (due to the hidden ordering) Fermi velocity. Typically, such a hidden ordering pushes any quantum phase transition into an insulation toward even stronger coupling in any $d>1$. However, depending on the internal algebra between the candidate insulating order parameter and masslike Dirac operator, the hidden-ordering may survive or disappear near the corresponding itinerant quantum critical point. I construct lattice models for such hidden-ordered massless Dirac fermions and outline promising platforms (numerical and experimental) to test these predictions.

</details>


### [89] [Finite temperature precursors of Mottness in the Fermi Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27204)
*Sayantan Roy,Abhisek Samanta,Nandini Trivedi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用精确行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）方法，在自旋有序温度之上研究排斥性哈伯德模型（repulsive Hubbard model）中Mottness的有限温度前驱现象。研究发现，即使在单粒子谱无能隙的情况下，电荷涨落已被显著压制，表明Mottness首先通过双粒子响应在反常金属态（anomalous metallic regime）中出现，随后才体现在单粒子谱函数中。态密度的能隙形成源于谱权重在布里渊区内的动量分辨重新分布，该过程始于反常金属态的开始而非单个动量点上的能隙打开。掺杂后，这一反常金属态会产生掺杂Mott绝缘体特征的输运和谱学信号，说明这些异常不需要半满时已完全形成的Mott绝缘体，而是源自半满时在前驱反常金属态中发展出的强电荷响应重整化与谱权重重新分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究排斥性哈伯德模型中Mottness（Mott物理）在有限温度下、自旋有序温度之上的前驱行为，厘清Mottness在单粒子与双粒子响应通道中的出现顺序，以及反常金属态在其中的角色。

Method: 采用数值精确的行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）方法，对排斥性哈伯德模型进行有限温度数值模拟。

Result: (1) 在自旋有序温度之上、单粒子谱仍无能隙时，电荷涨落已被显著抑制，Mottness首先通过双粒子响应在反常金属态中显现。(2) 态密度的能隙形成源于谱权重在布里渊区（Brillouin zone）内的动量分辨重新分布，此过程始于反常金属态的开始，而非单个动量点上的能隙打开。(3) 掺杂后，该反常金属态产生与掺杂Mott绝缘体相似的输运和谱学异常特征。

Conclusion: 掺杂哈伯德模型中的输运与谱学异常不需要半满时已完全形成的Mott绝缘体作为前提，而是起源于半满时在前驱反常金属态中发展出的强电荷响应重整化（charge-response renormalization）与谱权重重新分布（spectral-weight redistribution）。

Abstract: We investigate finite-temperature precursors of Mottness in the repulsive Hubbard model above the spin-ordering temperature, using numerically exact determinant quantum Monte Carlo. We show that the finite-temperature crossover is accompanied by a pronounced suppression of charge fluctuations, despite the presence of a gapless single-particle spectra, demonstrating that Mottness first emerges via two-particle response in an anomalous metallic regime, before appearing in single-particle spectral functions. We further show that a gap formation in the density of states occurs through momentum-resolved redistribution of spectral weight across the Brillouin zone, that begins at the onset of anomalous metallic regime, rather than through gap formation in single-particle spectral functions at individual momenta. Upon doping, the anomalous-metallic regime generates transport and spectroscopic signatures characteristic of doped Mott insulators. This shows that the transport and spectroscopic anomalies of the doped Hubbard model do not require the presence of a fully formed Mott insulator at half-filling, but instead originate from the strong charge-response renormalization and spectral-weight redistribution that develop within the precursor anomalous metallic regime at half-filling.

</details>

Method: 采用多种算法对电子和缪子进行识别，并将其与带电强子（charged hadrons）分离开来；具体算法细节摘要中未展开说明。

Result: 给出了 Belle II 实验在 Run 1 期间、基于能量不对称正负电子对撞机 SuperKEKB、质心系能量接近 Υ(4S) 共振峰、积分亮度达 428 fb⁻¹ 的数据集上所获得的性能表现。

Conclusion: 轻子识别算法已成功应用于 Belle II 实验的 Run 1 数据，其性能满足实验物理需求。

Abstract: Effective particle identification capabilities are a strategic priority for the physics program of the Belle~II experiment. We describe the algorithms used at Belle~II for identifying electrons and muons and separating them from charged hadrons. We present the performance obtained by the experiment during Run 1, which consists of 428 fb$^{-1}$ of data collected at the energy-asymmetric $e^+e^-$ collider SuperKEKB between 2019 and 2022 at center-of-mass energies near the mass of the $Υ(4S)$.

### [91] [Precision luminosity measurement in proton-proton collisions at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV with the CMS detector at the Large Hadron Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26832)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: CMS实验利用束流分离技术和Z玻色子产率校准，在13 TeV质子-质子对撞中实现了0.73%的总积分亮度（integrated luminosity）精度，创下了聚束强子对撞机（bunched-beam hadron collider）上亮度测量的最高纪录，为检验标准模型（Standard Model）和即将到来的高亮度大型强子对撞机（HL-LHC）时代奠定了关键基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发现新基础物理需要精确识别理论预测与实验数据之间的细微偏差，而这高度依赖于对积分亮度（integrated luminosity）——即对撞机实际递送的粒子相互作用数量的精确测量。现有精度尚不足以满足亚百分点级系统不确定度控制的需求。

Method: 通过专用束流分离技术对多个独立监测器进行校准，并利用高理解的Z玻色子产生率（Z boson production rates）严格验证监测器的长期稳定性，从而全面映射并最小化系统不确定性。

Result: 在整个数据集上实现了0.73%的总积分亮度精度，这是聚束强子对撞机（bunched-beam hadron collider）上迄今最精确的亮度测量结果，首次在每数据采集年内跨越了亚百分之一（sub-percent）的精度阈值。

Conclusion: 该结果从根本上提升了检验标准模型（Standard Model）的能力，并为即将到来的高亮度大型强子对撞机（High-Luminosity LHC）时代确立了关键的基线参考。

Abstract: Discovering new fundamental physics requires spotting subtle deviations between theoretical predictions and experimental data. This delicate comparison hinges on the precise knowledge of the integrated luminosity, the measure of how many particle interactions were actually delivered by the collider. Here, we report a landmark measurement of the integrated luminosity by the Compact Muon Solenoid (CMS) experiment for proton-proton collisions at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV at the CERN Large Hadron Collider (LHC). By calibrating multiple independent monitors through specialized beam-separation techniques and rigorously validating their long-term stability against well-understood Z boson production rates, we comprehensively map and minimize systematic uncertainties. Combining the findings yields a total integrated luminosity precision of 0.73% for the entire data set. This marks the most precise luminosity measurement ever achieved at a bunched-beam hadron collider. Crossing the sub-percent precision threshold per data taking year fundamentally sharpens our ability to test the standard model and establishes a vital baseline for the upcoming High-Luminosity LHC era.

</details>


### [92] [Calibration and Performance of proANUBIS: A proof-of-concept detector for the ANUBIS experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26856)
*Giulio Aielli,Oleg Brandt,Jude Burling,Patrick Collins,Jonas Dej,Cayetano Fernandez Ruiz,Christopher Lester,Kaijia Liu,Luca Pizzimento,Ludovico Pontecorvo,Theo Reymermier,Michael Revering,Aashaq Shah,Tom Spencer,Paul Swallow*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: ANUBIS实验通过在ATLAS cavern顶部安装阻性板室（Resistive Plate Chamber）探测器，旨在扩展对长寿命粒子（long-lived particles，寿命τ>10皮秒）的探测灵敏度。其原型探测器proANUBIS已安装并完成性能验证，探测效率与时间分辨率均符合预期，满足ANUBIS的性能要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多具有暗物质候选者的标准模型（Standard Model）扩展理论预言了寿命τ>10皮秒的长寿命粒子（long-lived particles）。现有实验灵敏度有限，ANUBIS实验旨在通过改造ATLAS cavern顶部空间来提升对此类粒子的探测能力。

Method: ANUBIS实验在ATLAS洞穴顶部安装阻性板室（Resistive Plate Chamber）探测器，利用ATLAS探测器上方充满空气的体积，重建长寿命粒子衰变产生的顶点（vertices）。原型探测器proANUBIS被安装在ATLAS cavern中，使用LHC的质子-质子对撞（pp collision）数据进行μ子和强子通量的原位测量，以验证探测器技术可行性。

Result: 基于proANUBIS收集的数据与重建技术，探测效率（detection efficiency）与时间分辨率（timing resolution）均与预期一致，满足ANUBIS的性能要求。

Conclusion: proANUBIS探测器成功验证了ANUBIS实验所需的探测器技术，其性能指标符合设计需求，为ANUBIS实验的全面部署奠定了基础。

Abstract: Long-lived particles with lifetimes $τ>10$~ps are predicted by many extensions of the Standard Model with viable dark matter candidates. The ANUBIS experiment proposes to extend the experimental sensitivity to long-lived particles by instrumenting the ceiling of the ATLAS cavern with Resistive Plate Chamber detectors in order to reconstruct vertices from long-lived particle decays in the air-filled volume above the ATLAS detector. The proANUBIS detector has been installed in the ATLAS cavern to validate the detector technology planned for ANUBIS and to take in-situ measurements of muon and hadron fluxes inside the ATLAS cavern using $pp$ collision data from the LHC. In this paper, the data collected, reconstruction techniques used, and performance of the \proanubis detector are discussed. The detection efficiency and timing resolution are found to be consistent with expectations and to meet the performance requirements of ANUBIS.

</details>


### [93] [Projected sensitivity of the ANUBIS detector to heavy neutral leptons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26862)
*Martin Bauer,Rachel Bentham,Oleg Brandt,Sofie Nordahl Erner,Anna Mullin,David Peng,Theo Reymermier,Paul Swallow*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文评估了ANUBIS探测器对长寿命粒子（LLPs）中重中性轻子（HNLs）的投影灵敏度，在最小马约拉纳HNL模型下，对电子耦合和缪子耦合的最大灵敏度分别达到$|V_{1e}|^2=1.8\times10^{-8}$和$|V_{1μ}|^2=1.9\times10^{-8}$，为LHC的HNL参数空间提供了与其他实验互补的覆盖范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长寿命粒子（Long-Lived Particles, LLPs）是标准模型（Standard Model, SM）多种扩展方案中的共同特征，这些扩展旨在解决标准模型的已知局限性。ANUBIS探测器被提议用于扩展LHC上ATLAS实验对LLPs的探测灵敏度，通过在ATLAS探测器洞穴顶部安装探测器实现。

Method: 本文采用SET-ANUBIS框架来评估ANUBIS探测器对各种长寿命粒子模型的灵敏度。研究中考虑了一个最小马约拉纳（Majorana）重中性轻子（Heavy Neutral Lepton, HNL）模型，该模型仅耦合到单一轻子味（电子$e$或缪子$μ$）。

Result: 对于耦合到电子的HNL，ANUBIS在HNL质量$m_{N_1}=6.4$ GeV时达到最大灵敏度$|V_{1e}|^2=1.8\times10^{-8}$；对于耦合到缪子的HNL，在质量$m_{N_1}=6.3$ GeV时达到最大灵敏度$|V_{1μ}|^2=1.9\times10^{-8}$。

Conclusion: ANUBIS在HNL参数空间中为其他已提出的LLP实验提供了互补的覆盖范围，并且通过在ANUBIS数据采集期间改进分析策略，具有进一步提升灵敏度的潜力。

Abstract: Long-Lived Particles (LLPs) are a common feature in various extensions to the Standard Model (SM) that seek to address known limitations. The ANUBIS detector has been proposed to extend the sensitivity of the ATLAS experiment at the LHC to LLPs by instrumenting the ceiling of the ATLAS detector cavern. This article presents the projected sensitivity of ANUBIS to Heavy Neutral Leptons (HNLs). For a minimal Majorana HNL model that only couples to a single flavour of lepton ($e$ or $μ$) ANUBIS reaches a maximum sensitivity of $|V_{1e}|^2=1.8\times10^{-8}$ and $|V_{1μ}|^2=1.9\times10^{-8}$ for a HNL mass of $m_{N_1}=6.4$ GeV and 6.3 GeV respectively. This provides complementary coverage to other proposed LLP experiments in the HNL parameter-space, with potential for significant improvement during ANUBIS data-taking through advances in analysis strategies. The results are obtained with SET-ANUBIS, a flexible framework to evaluate the sensitivity of ANUBIS to a variety of LLP models.

</details>


### [94] [Study of Supernova Neutrinos at ESSnuSB](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27007)
*ESSnuSB,:,J. Aguilar,M. Anastasopoulos,D. Barčot,E. Baussan,A. K. Bhattacharyya,A. Bignami,M. Blennow,M. Bogomilov,B. Bolling,E. Bouquerel,F. Bramati,A. Branca,G. Brunetti,I. Bustinduy,C. J. Oglakci,T. Ohlsson,M. Olvegård,P. Panda,M. Pari,D. Patrzalek,G. Petkov,Ch. Petridou,P. Poussot,A. Psallidas,F. Pupilli,D. Saiang,D. Sampsonidis,A. Scanu,C. Schwab,F. Sordo,G. Stavropoulos,M. Stipčević,R. Tarkeshian,F. Terranova,T. Tolba,M. Topp-Mugglestone,E. Trachanas,R. Tsenov,A. Tsirigotis,S. E. Tzamarias,M. Vanderpoorten,G. Vankova-Kirilova,N. Vassilopoulos,S. Vihonen,J. Wurtz,V. Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文研究了ESSnuSB实验的远探测器对超新星中微子的灵敏度，通过估算不同超新星通量模型下的预期事件率，并评估其区分这些模型的能力，同时讨论了系统误差和探测器效率的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ESSnuSB是一个拟建在瑞典的长基线中微子实验（long-baseline neutrino experiment），其538 kt水切伦科夫探测器（water Cherenkov detector）主要用于通过研究第二振荡极大值来探测轻子相位δ_CP。然而，鉴于其巨大的探测器体积，如果在运行期间发生超新星爆发，该探测器将对超新星中微子（supernova neutrinos）具有极佳的灵敏度，这激发了本文的研究。

Method: 首先针对三种不同的超新星通量通量模型（supernova flux models），估算ESSnuSB远探测器上的预期事件率；进而探测该探测器区分这些通量模型的能力；此外，还考察了系统误差（systematic errors）和探测器效率（detector efficiency）的影响。

Result: 结果表明，基于不同的超新星中微子模型，在地球上探测到的预期事件数存在显著差异。同时，ESSnuSB远探测器在区分这些通量模型方面可能具有卓越的潜力，但这一能力取决于超新星爆发的距离、系统误差以及探测器效率。

Conclusion: ESSnuSB远探测器除了其设计目标外，在超新星中微子探测方面也展现出良好的应用前景，其区分不同通量模型的能力受到多种因素的影响。

Abstract: In this paper, we have studied the sensitivity of the ESSnuSB far detector to supernova neutrinos. ESSnuSB is a proposed long-baseline neutrino experiment in Sweden, which will use a 538 kt water Cherenkov detector to probe the leptonic phase $δ_{\rm CP}$ by studying the second oscillation maximum. However, given the very large detector volume, it will have an excellent sensitivity to supernova neutrinos if a supernova explosion occurs during the run-time of ESSnuSB. Motivated by this, we first estimate the expected event rates at the ESSnuSB far detector for three different supernova flux models and then we probe its capability to distinguish these flux models. Additionally, we also investigate the impact of systematic errors and detector efficiency. Our results show that depending on the model of the supernova neutrinos, the expected number of events detected at Earth varies significantly. Our results also show that the ESSnuSB far detector may have excellent potential in distinguishing these flux models depending upon the distance of the supernova explosion, systematic errors and detector efficiency.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CMS实验中针对长寿命粒子（LLPs）的搜索常涉及非传统的事件拓扑（unconventional event topologies），标准触发策略难以高效筛选此类事件，因此需要开发专用触发系统以提升灵敏度。

Method: 开发并部署了高多重触发（High Multiplicity Trigger, HMT）系统，基于CMS阴极条室（CSC）缪子探测器中异常高的击中数进行事件筛选；采用优化的击中多重阈值（hit multiplicity thresholds）控制触发率，使其适应高亮度、高堆叠（pileup）条件。

Result: HMT在高亮度、高堆叠条件下能够维持可接受的触发率，并在广泛的长寿命粒子寿命和运动学范围内保持高效率。触发性能通过模拟事件样本和LHC Run~3质子-质子对撞数据得到验证。

Conclusion: HMT显著扩展了CMS对与LLP衰变相关的非标准信号（non-standard signatures）的灵敏度，并为未来寻找超出标准模型（Standard Model, SM）的新物理提供了灵活的平台。

Abstract: Searches for long-lived particles (LLPs) at the CMS experiment often involve unconventional event topologies that are difficult to efficiently select using standard trigger strategies. To improve sensitivity to such signatures during LHC Run~3 operation, a dedicated High Multiplicity Trigger (HMT) has been developed and deployed in the CMS trigger system. The trigger targets events containing unusually large numbers of hits in the CMS cathode strip chamber (CSC) muon detectors, a characteristic signature of several LLP scenarios involving displaced decays in the muon system. The HMT implementation, trigger logic, rate dependence with pileup, and operational stability are described. Optimized hit multiplicity thresholds are used to maintain acceptable trigger rates under high-luminosity and high-pileup conditions while preserving high efficiency across a broad range of LLP lifetimes and kinematic regimes. The trigger performance is evaluated using both simulated event samples and proton-proton collision data collected during Run~3 of the LHC. The HMT substantially extends the CMS sensitivity to non-standard signatures associated with LLP decays and provides a flexible platform for future searches for physics beyond the Standard Model.

### [96] [Discrete Space-Time Wave Kernels on Regular Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27083)
*Amar Bašić,Lejla Smajlović,Zenan Šabanac*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文针对齐次(q+1)-正则树上的前向离散时空波动方程，推导了两种基本波核的显式公式，分别用离散I-贝塞尔函数和离散J-贝塞尔函数表示，并给出了渐近行为分析和离散时间下传播有限性的证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在离散结构（如树图）上建立波动方程的解表示，填补离散波动核显式公式的空白，并探索离散情形下经典连续理论的模拟（analogue）。

Method: 在齐次(q+1)-正则树T_{q+1}上定义与两参数广义拉普拉斯算子（generalized Laplacian）相关的前向离散时空波动方程；在算子非负性假设下，利用离散I-贝塞尔函数（discrete I-Bessel functions）推导波核的显式公式；在谱边界情形下，使用离散J-贝塞尔函数（discrete J-Bessel functions）获得另一显式表示；通过解析和数值方法研究波核在径向距离、时间和树度趋于无穷时的渐近行为（asymptotic behavior）。

Result: 获得了两种基本波核的显式公式，分别由离散I-贝塞尔函数和离散J-贝塞尔函数给出；建立了离散情形下经典的I↔J关系（I↔J relation）的类比；波核表达式为有限和形式，确保每个离散时间步的传播公式均保持有限；完成了波核在大径向距离、大时间和大树度条件下的解析与数值渐近分析。

Conclusion: 在离散树图上成功构建了波动方程解的卷积表示，推广了连续波动理论到离散时空框架，并保证了传播过程的有限性，为离散空间上的波传播研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study the forward discrete space-time wave equation on the homogeneous $(q+1)$-regular tree $T_{q+1}$ associated with a two-parameter generalized Laplacian. Under the natural nonnegativity assumption on this operator, we derive explicit formulas for the two fundamental wave kernels. The formulas are given in terms of discrete $I$-Bessel functions and yield convolution representations for solutions with general initial conditions.
  In the boundary case corresponding to the bottom of the spectrum, we obtain another explicit representation of the wave kernel in terms of discrete $J$-Bessel functions. This representation leads to a discrete analogue of the classical $I\!\leftrightarrow\!J$ relation. We also perform both analytic and numerical studies of the asymptotic behavior of the wave kernels, including large radial distance, large time, and large degree of the tree.
  An important feature of our analysis is that the wave kernels are expressed as finite sums; hence, the propagation formulas remain finite for every discrete time.

### [97] [Homogeneity actions, N-manifolds, and the Frobenius theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27135)
*Janusz Grabowski,Asier López-Gordón*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究由齐次性作用诱导的 ℕ-分次超流形（ℕ-graded supermanifold），证明其具有纤维丛结构，给出齐次 Frobenius 定理的简洁证明，并与现有 ℕ-流形定义建立等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为 ℕ-分次超流形建立一种由齐次性作用（homogeneity action）诱导的刻画框架，并利用该框架简化齐次 Frobenius 定理的证明，同时统一不同文献中对 ℕ-流形的定义。

Method: 通过考虑实数乘法幺半群的光滑作用 ℝ ∋ t ↦ h_t 来定义齐次性作用；证明 h_0 是一个光滑收缩映射（smooth retraction），且 h_0: ℳ → M 是以 ℝ^{m|n} 为典型纤维的纤维丛（fiber bundle）。在额外假设 h_{-1} 作为宇称算符（parity operator）时，给出与 Bursztyn、Cueca 和 Mehta 用分次代数层（sheaves of graded algebras）定义的 ℕ-流形等价的几何刻画。

Result: 得到了齐次 Frobenius 定理的一个简洁证明；并将 Bursztyn–Cueca–Mehta 的 ℕ-流形 Frobenius 定理作为本文更一般结果的特例。

Conclusion: 齐次性方法为 ℕ-分次超流形提供了统一的几何基础，其齐次 Frobenius 定理推广了现有结论，有助于理解分次几何（graded geometry）中不同构造之间的内在联系。

Abstract: This paper is devoted to $\mathbb{N}$-graded supermanifolds $\mathcal{M}$ whose grading is induced by a homogeneity action, i.e., a smooth action $\mathbb{R}\ni t\mapsto h_t$ of the multiplicative monoid of real numbers on $\mathcal{M}$. We show that the map $h_0$ is a smooth retraction onto a submanifold $M=h_0(\mathcal{M})$, and that $h_0:\mathcal{M}\to M$ is a fiber bundle with typical fiber $\mathbb{R}^{m|n}$. Using this homogeneity approach, we obtain a simple proof of a homogeneous version of the Frobenius theorem. If, in addition, $h_{-1}$ acts as the parity operator on $\mathcal{M}$, we provide a geometric characterization equivalent to the recent definition of $\mathbb{N}$-manifolds due to Bursztyn, Cueca, and Mehta in terms of sheaves of graded algebras with prescribed local models. As a consequence, the homogeneous Frobenius theorem for $\mathbb{N}$-manifolds proved by these authors appears as a special case of our more general result.

### [98] [Symmetries of the Generalized Yang--Baxter Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26510)
*Pramod Padmanabhan,Somnath Maity,Akash Sinha,Vladimir Korepin*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本论文系统刻画了广义Yang-Baxter方程（generalized Yang-Baxter equations，即多站点版本的Yang-Baxter方程）的连续与离散对称性，并建立了解的等价类。研究发现，此类方程的对称性依赖于方程所支持的站点数，在某些情况下比标准Yang-Baxter方程具有更多的对称性，从而对不等价解的数量及相关可积模型施加了严格限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义Yang-Baxter方程（generalized Yang-Baxter equations）是标准Yang-Baxter方程的多站点推广。当引入谱参数（spectral parameters）时，这类方程有望导出具多自由度局域相互作用的可积哈密顿量（integrable Hamiltonians）。因此，系统分析这些方程的对称性结构，对于理解其解的分类及构造相关可积模型具有重要意义。

Method: 本文对广义Yang-Baxter方程的连续对称性（continuous symmetries）和离散对称性（discrete symmetries）进行了刻画，用以建立解的等价类（equivalence class of solutions）。通过比较不同站点数下对称性的差异，分析了对称性结构对方程解集的影响。

Result: 研究发现，广义Yang-Baxter方程的对称性集合依赖于方程所支持的站点数。在多种情况下，这些对称性数量多于标准Yang-Baxter方程，从而对不等价解的数量和关联的可积模型（integrable models）形成了显著约束。

Conclusion: 广义Yang-Baxter方程的对称性结构比标准情形更为丰富且依赖于站点数，这为求解和分类相关可积模型提供了新的约束条件。

Abstract: The generalized Yang-Baxter equations are multi-site versions of the standard Yang-Baxter equation. When spectral parameters are included, such equations are expected to lead to integrable Hamiltonians with local interactions involving multiple degrees of freedom. In this work we characterize both the continuous and discrete symmetries of these equations required to establish an equivalence class of solutions. We find that the set of such symmetries depend on the number of sites on which the equation is supported. In several cases there are more symmetries than the standard Yang-Baxter equation, thus placing heavy constraints on the number of inequivalent solutions and the associated integrable models.

### [99] [Integrable pentagram-type maps on polyhedra via partial difference operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26526)
*Bao Wang*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文从多边形上的五角星映射推广到（扭曲）多面体上的自然泛化族，并通过偏差分算子证明其可积性。重点研究了一个典型特例——离散共轭网的离散拉普拉斯变换。建立了射影等价类与双周期偏差分算子谱数据之间的双射，并将该映射等同于伪偏差分算子的泊松-李群上的重构映射，从而证明完全可积性，给出显式拉克斯表示和r-矩阵诱导的泊松括号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典五角星映射（pentagram map）从多边形情形推广到更高维的（扭曲）多面体（twisted polyhedra），并探索其可积结构。

Method: 引入偏差分算子（partial difference operators）描述广义五角星映射族；建立$\mathbb{RP}^3$中多面体的射影等价类（projective equivalence classes）与双周期偏差分算子的谱数据（spectral data）之间的规范双射；将该映射等价于伪偏差分算子（pseudo partial difference operators）的泊松-李群（Poisson-Lie group）上的重构映射（refactorization maps），从而给出显式拉克斯表示（Lax representation）和r-矩阵（$r$-matrix）诱导的泊松括号。

Result: 获得了广义五角星映射族的完全可积性（complete integrability）证明，并建立了其与离散共轭网拉普拉斯变换（discrete Laplace transformation of discrete conjugate nets）在典型特例下的对应关系。

Conclusion: 本文建立的代数识别方法不仅统一了五角星映射的高维推广，还通过拉克斯表示和泊松结构揭示了其几何动力学的可积性本质。

Abstract: This paper introduces a family of natural generalizations of the pentagram map from polygons to (twisted) polyhedra and proves their integrability through the partial difference operators. A canonical special case, which corresponds to the discrete Laplace transformation of discrete conjugate nets, is investigated in detail. We first establish a canonical bijection between the projective equivalence classes of these polyhedra in $\mathbb{RP}^3$ and the spectral data of doubly periodic partial difference operators modulo the gauge actions. Furthermore, we prove the complete integrability of these pentagram-type maps by explicitly identifying them with the refactorization maps on the Poisson-Lie group of pseudo partial difference operators. This algebraic identification naturally yields an explicit Lax representation and an $r$-matrix induced Poisson bracket for the geometric dynamics.

### [100] [On Support Cardinality for Discrete Schrödinger Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26149)
*Linjun Li*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究离散薛定谔方程（discrete Schrödinger equation）非平凡解的最小非零支撑大小（support size），证明了一个维数约化原理（dimension-reduction principle）：支撑大小的下界不会随维数增加而减小，并利用这一原理在四维空间中得到了接近最优的下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究离散薛定谔方程非平凡解在给定非零条件下能稀疏到何种程度，即支撑集大小的最小可能值，并理解该最小值与空间维数的关系。

Method: 在有限d维格点盒子（lattice box）上考虑带任意实势场的Dirichlet解（Dirichlet solutions），通过构造维数约化原理，建立高维问题与低维问题之间的下界传递机制。

Result: 证明了支撑大小最小值的下界不会随维数增加而降低；在四维情形下获得了近乎尖锐的下界，与目前最优的二维构造（two-dimensional constructions）相比仅差一个对数因子（logarithmic factor）。

Conclusion: 维数约化原理为离散薛定谔方程稀疏解的下界研究提供了一个统一的证明框架，使得低维结果可以直接推广到高维，从而在四维中逼近最优稀疏性下界。

Abstract: How sparse can a nontrivial solution of a discrete Schrödinger equation be? In this note we study Dirichlet solutions on a finite $d$-dimensional lattice box, allowing an arbitrary real potential, and measure sparsity by the number of lattice sites at which the solution is nonzero (assuming it is nonzero at the origin). Our main result is a dimension-reduction principle: the minimal possible support size cannot decrease when the dimension increases. Consequently, any lower bound proved in dimension $d-1$ automatically yields the same lower bound in dimension $d$. As an application, we obtain a nearly sharp lower bound in four dimensions, matching the best-known two-dimensional constructions up to a logarithmic factor.

</details>


### [101] [The Colored Hofstadter Butterfly as a Many-Body Quantum Hall Phase Diagram](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26256)
*Giovanna Marcelli,Tadahiro Miyao,Domenico Monaco,Stefan Teufel,Marius Wesle*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明，对于一大类弱相互作用晶格费米子系统，彩色霍夫施塔特蝴蝶（colored Hofstadter butterfly）具有多体解释：在任意磁通量下，通过准绝热延拓（quasi-adiabatic continuation）与分母无关的磁微扰估计，可在无有限磁单胞的情况下构造出局域唯一的有能隙基态，并证明霍尔电导（Hall conductivity）是量子化的整数倍，从而非相互作用的霍夫施塔特蝴蝶的整数颜色可作为相互作用量子霍尔相的标签持久存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 希望证明霍夫施塔特蝴蝶谱中的整数颜色（即非相互作用的拓扑相标签）在弱相互作用下依然能够存活，从而为相互作用量子霍尔系统提供一个多体解释和严格的拓扑分类依据。

Method: 结合准绝热延拓（quasi-adiabatic continuation）与分母无关的磁微扰估计（denominator-independent magnetic perturbation estimates），在三维参数空间（磁场b、化学势μ、相互作用强度λ）中构造无限大体系统计有唯一能隙的基态；方法覆盖有理与无理磁通，无需依赖有限的磁单胞（magnetic unit cell）。

Result: 在满足非相互作用平面λ=0的连通均匀有能隙区域上，证明了一个多体能隙标定理（many-body gap-labeling theorem）：宏观欧姆定律（Ohm's law）中的霍尔电导（Hall conductivity）是常数且量子化的，满足2πσ^H ∈ ℤ。

Conclusion: 非相互作用的霍夫施塔特蝴蝶的整数颜色可以作为相互作用量子霍尔相的霍尔电导标签持续存在，即弱相互作用不会破坏该拓扑量子化现象。

Abstract: We prove that the colored Hofstadter butterfly has a many-body interpretation for a broad class of weakly interacting lattice fermion systems. Starting from a spectral gap of a Hofstadter-like one-particle Hamiltonian at arbitrary magnetic flux $b$, we construct an open region in the three-dimensional parameter space $(b,μ,λ)$ of magnetic field, chemical potential, and interaction strength on which the infinite-volume interacting system has locally unique gapped ground states. The construction combines quasi-adiabatic continuation in the interaction strength with denominator-independent magnetic perturbation estimates, and therefore covers both commensurate and incommensurate fluxes, where no finite magnetic unit cell exists. On connected uniformly gapped regions meeting the non-interacting plane $λ=0$, we prove a many-body gap-labeling theorem: the Hall conductivity appearing in the macroscopic Ohm's law is constant and quantized, satisfying $2πσ^{\mathrm{H}}\in\mathbb{Z}$. Thus the integer colors of the non-interacting Hofstadter butterfly persist as Hall-conductivity labels of interacting quantum Hall phases.

</details>


### [102] [A new formulation of metriplectic dynamics with an application to quasigeostrophic ocean modeling with advected quantities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26388)
*Francisco J. Beron-Vera,Erwin Luesink*

Method: 研究首先提出度量-辛动力学的通用公式，核心是通过两个反对称（skew-symmetric）括号的乘积构造度量-辛四括号（metriplectic four-bracket）。随后将该形式应用于包含平流量的广义二维准地转上层海洋模型（以热QG模型为特例），从而在动力学中引入不可逆性。

Result: 所构建的度量-辛动力学能够确保系统内能（internal energy）守恒，同时熵（entropy）增加，符合热力学第一定律和第二定律。该公式允许灵活指定不可逆性的类型，范围涵盖从近似保持位涡（potential vorticity）物质守恒的机制，到代表二维QG海洋建模中实际强迫与耗散的机制。

Conclusion: 本文提出的度量-辛动力学形式为在带有平流量的二维QG海洋模型中引入不可逆性提供了统一且灵活的理论框架，既保证了热力学一致性，又能够适应从理想化到现实场景的不同建模需求。

Abstract: A general formulation of metriplectic dynamics is presented, where the metriplectic four-bracket is constructed by multiplying two skew-symmetric brackets. The new formulation is then used to introduce irreversibility in a generalized two-dimensional (2D) quasigeostrophic (QG) upper-ocean model involving advected quantities, with the thermal QG model as a special case. By construction, the resulting dynamics ensure the conservation of internal energy and the generation of entropy, in accordance with the first and second laws of thermodynamics. Our metriplectic dynamics formulation allows for a flexible specification of irreversibility, ranging from a type that results in nearly material conservation of potential vorticity to the representation of realistic forcing and dissipation in 2D QG ocean modeling with advected quantities.

### [103] [Weak-Strong Resurgence Duality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26637)
*Gerald V. Dunne,Ayssar I. Farah*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本论文揭示了弱耦合展开与强耦合展开之间存在明确的复现对偶（resurgent duality）关系，适用于一种展开收敛半径为零而另一种展开收敛半径为无穷大的情形。通过Airy和Pearcey突变积分加以说明，并应用于零维标量φ⁴理论中的Dyson-Schwinger方程以及Gross-Neveu模型中扭结-反扭结晶鞍点构型的热核迹短时与长时展开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前已有研究讨论了两类展开中一方为有限收敛半径的收敛级数、或双方均为零收敛半径级数时的对偶情形，但尚缺乏对“一种展开收敛半径为零、另一种为无穷大”这一互补情形下的复现对偶关系的系统论证。

Method: 采用复现（resurgence）理论框架，通过分析Airy积分和Pearcey突变积分解析地建立弱-强耦合展开之间的对偶关系；随后将这一形式化框架分别应用于零维标量φ⁴理论的Dyson-Schwinger方程和Gross-Neveu模型中的热核迹展开问题。

Result: 在零维标量φ⁴理论中，弱耦合展开系数呈阶乘增长（收敛半径为零），强耦合展开系数则递减（收敛半径为无穷大），两者之间存在复现对偶；在Gross-Neveu模型中，热核迹的短时展开（收敛半径为零）与长时展开（收敛半径为无穷大）同样满足这一对偶关系。

Conclusion: 复现对偶在弱-强耦合展开和短-长时展开中普遍存在，并不限于两个展开均为零收敛半径的典型情形，从而扩展了复现理论的应用范围。

Abstract: We show that there is an explicit resurgent duality between weak and strong coupling expansions when one of the expansions has zero radius of convergence and the other has infinite radius of convergence. This complements the situation where the convergent expansion has finite radius of convergence, or when both expansions have zero radius of convergence. We illustrate this phenomenon for the Airy and Pearcey catastrophe integrals, and we apply it to two physical examples: the weak and strong coupling expansions of Dyson-Schwinger equations in zero-dimensional scalar $φ^4$ theories, and the short and long time expansions of the heat kernel trace for the fluctuation operator of the kink-antikink crystal saddle configuration in the Gross-Neveu model.

### [104] [Wave-Particle Decomposition for Kinetic Equations I: Theory and Numerics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26915)
*Chang Liu,Kun Xu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于局部演化时间尺度与动力学视界（kinetic horizon）的波粒分解（WPD）方法，将分布函数分解为解析累积的波分量与纯动力学粒子分量，构建了覆盖整个努森（Knudsen）谱的统一波粒系统，并设计了保守宏微观数值方法，在PDE层面实现了局部时间步长分割的渐进保持与跨尺度模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的统一气体动力学波粒（UGKWP）方法采用全局时间步分裂，缺乏PDE层面的局部分解机制。本文旨在建立一种连续的、基于局部演化时间尺度与动力学视界的波粒分解框架，使分解在PDE层面定义，从而更自然地实现跨努森数（Knudsen number）谱的统一描述。

Method: 利用特征积分（characteristic integral）解，将分布函数分解为解析累积的波分量与纯动力学粒子分量，后者由超出局部视界的无碰撞输运定义。连续形式的系统包含无源总守恒律、波动方程与粒子方程。离散层面采用保守宏微观方法：总守恒变量通过有限体积更新推进，通量由纳维-斯托克斯（Navier-Stokes）气体动力学波通量与粒子通量（离散纵标法$S_N$或蒙特卡洛表示）之和构成。分解在PDE层面由演化时间尺度与松弛时间的局部比值控制。

Result: 形式分析证明了该方法的渐进保持（asymptotic-preserving）连续极限、稀薄区域一致性以及活跃动力学自由度的跨区域自适应缩放。一维、二维和三维数值测试验证了框架的精度、多尺度能力与计算效率。

Conclusion: 所提出的波粒分解方法在PDE层面实现了局部时间步分割，克服了UGKWP方法全局分裂的局限性，能够统一描述从连续流到稀薄流的全努森谱流动，且数值实验证明了其可靠性与高效性。

Abstract: This paper presents a wave-particle decomposition (WPD) for kinetic relaxation equations, formulated around a local evolution timescale and its associated kinetic horizon. By leveraging the characteristic integral solution, we decompose the distribution function into an analytically accumulated wave component and a purely kinetic particle component. The latter is defined by the collisionless transport that survives beyond a prescribed local domain of influence, termed the horizon. This continuous formulation yields a unified wave-particle system valid across the entire Knudsen spectrum, comprising a source-free total conservation law, a wave equation, and a particle equation. The wave operator admits a Chapman--Enskog expansion, whose moments yield Euler and Navier--Stokes fluxes with horizon-dependent coefficients, while the particle equation governs the remaining non-equilibrium kinetic transport.
  At the algorithmic level, this system is discretized by a conservative macro-micro method. The total conservative variables are advanced by a finite-volume update using the sum of a Navier--Stokes gas-kinetic wave flux and a particle flux computed by either a deterministic discrete-ordinate $(S_N)$ method or a Monte Carlo representation. Unlike the global time-step splitting in the unified gas-kinetic wave-particle (UGKWP) method, the present partition is defined at the PDE level and governed by the local ratio of evolution timescale to relaxation time. The particle component is therefore a fractional kinetic population generated by the collisionless factor of the integral solution. Formal analysis establishes the asymptotic-preserving continuum limit, rarefied-regime consistency, and regime-adaptive scaling of active kinetic degrees of freedom. Numerical tests in one, two, and three dimensions validate the accuracy, multiscale capability, and efficiency of the framework.

Conclusion: 本文为随机曲面上的临界伊辛模型与(3,4)拓扑极小模型之间的等价关系提供了严格数学证明，为双标度极限和矩阵模型与共形场论（conformal field theory）之间的联系建立了更坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: We prove that the differential of the log of the partition function for the $2$-matrix model with quartic interactions converges in a certain double-scaling regime to the differential of the $\boldsymbolτ$-function for the $(3,4)$ string equation. This confirms the convergence of the critical Ising model on random surfaces to the $(3,4)$ topological minimal model, which was stated in the works of Douglas and Shenker, Brézin and Kazakov, and Gross and Migdal. Our analysis is based on a steepest-descent analysis of a Riemann-Hilbert problem associated to a family of biorthogonal polynomials. ### [107] [Geometric bulk-edge correspondence for $\mathbb{Z}_2$-topological insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27318)
*Alexis Drouot,Jacob Shapiro,Xiaowen Zhu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了二维费米子时间反演不变绝缘体（class AII）在弯曲界面下的几何体边对应关系：界面系统的Z2边缘指标等于两个体Z2指标之差与边界-测量区域几何交点数模2的乘积，是Hall绝缘体曲界面连接公式的Z2类似物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Z2版本的几何连接公式（geometric connection formula），通过将弯曲边界的交点数（intersection number）与体Z2指标差以及边缘Z2指标相关联，建立模2代数关系。该论证是Hall绝缘体弯曲界面连接公式（DZ24）的Z2类比推广。

Result: 推导出核心公式：弯曲界面系统的Z2边缘指标 = (体Z2指标差) × (几何交点数) mod 2。该结果将拓扑绝缘体的体边对应从平直界面推广到弯曲几何情形。

Conclusion: 建立了二维class AII绝缘体在弯曲界面下的几何体边对应定理，揭示了体拓扑与界面几何之间的深层联系，为处理具有复杂几何边界的拓扑绝缘体系统提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Fermionic time-reversal-invariant insulators in two dimensions--class AII in the Kitaev table--come in two topological phases. These phases are characterized by a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-valued invariant, the Fu-Kane-Mele index. We prove a geometric bulk-edge correspondence for curved interfaces: if two such insulators occupy complementary regions separated by a curved boundary, then the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ edge index of the interface system is the product, modulo two, of the difference of the two bulk $\mathbb{Z}_2$ indices and a geometric intersection number associated with the boundary and the measurement region. The argument is a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ analogue of the curved-interface connection formula proved for Hall insulators in \cite{DZ24}.

### [108] [$\mathrm{W}^*$-algebraic Integration Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27366)
*Jan Głowacki,Yui Kuramochi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了算子值积分（operator-valued integration）的泛函分析框架：定义并研究了以W*-代数（von Neumann代数）取值的函数关于POVM（positive operator-valued measure）的积分，证明了积分映射是忠实、正规、单位完全正（CP）映射，并建立了Leibniz法则和Fubini定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为算子值函数关于POVM的积分建立严格的数学框架，填补将标量值测度论推广至算子值情形的理论空白，并为后续量子信息与算子代数交叉研究提供基础工具。

Method: 利用空间张量积（spatial tensor product）构造积分 $\int f \otimes d\mathsf{E} \in \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S} \bar{\otimes} \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{R}$；定义一致有界超弱可测函数空间 $B_b(Σ,\mathcal{F},\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S})$ 并商去E-零函数得到 $L^\infty_\mathsf{E}(Σ,\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S})$；通过Stinespring分解（Stinespring factorization）经Naimark dilation证明完全正性。

Result: 当 $(\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{R})_*$ 可分时，$L^\infty_\mathsf{E}(Σ,\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S}) \cong \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S} \bar{\otimes} L^\infty_\mathsf{E}(Σ)$ 是W*-代数；积分映射是忠实正规单位完全正映射，对PVM（投影值测度，projection-valued measure）是$*$-同态，对局部化POVM（localizable POVM）是等距；积分映射可等同于空间张量积 $\boldsymbol{1}_{\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S}} \hat{\otimes} Φ_\mathsf{E}$；建立了算子值Leibniz法则和Fubini定理。

Conclusion: 该工作为W*-代数框架下的算子值积分提供了统一而严格的数学基础，揭示了积分映射与空间张量积、POVM诱导的正规正映射之间的深层联系，并推广了经典测度论中的Fubini定理至算子值情形。

Abstract: Given a pair of $\mathrm{W}^*$-algebras $(\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S},\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{R})$ with $(\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S})_*$ separable, a measurable space $(Σ, \mathcal{F})$ and a POVM $\mathsf{E}: \mathcal{F} \to \mathcal{E}(\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{R})$, the integral of a function $f: Σ\to \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S}$ is defined as an element of the spatial tensor product $\int f \otimes d\mathsf{E} \in \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S} \bar{\otimes} \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{R}$. The space $B_b(Σ,\mathcal{F},\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S})$ of uniformly bounded ultraweakly measurable functions is the universal domain of integration; once $\mathsf{E}$ is fixed it refines to the quotient $L^\infty_\mathsf{E}(Σ,\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S}) = B_b(Σ,\mathcal{F},\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S})/\mathcal{N}_\mathsf{E}$ by $\mathsf{E}$-null functions. When $(\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{R})_*$ is also separable, $L^\infty_\mathsf{E}(Σ,\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S}) \cong \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S} \bar{\otimes} L^\infty_\mathsf{E}(Σ)$ is a $\mathrm{W}^*$-algebra. The integration map is a faithful normal unital completely positive (CP) map, a $*$-homomorphism for PVMs and an isometry for localizable POVMs. It can be identified with the spatial tensor product $\boldsymbol{1}_{\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S}} \hat{\otimes} Φ_\mathsf{E}$ where $Φ_\mathsf{E}: L^\infty_\mathsf{E}(Σ) \to \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{R}$ is the faithful normal positive map corresponding to $\mathsf{E}$. Complete positivity of integration maps is derived from Stinespring factorization through Naimark dilation. We establish an operator-valued Leibniz rule and Fubini theorem.

</details>

### [109] [New Superconductors in the PtPb$_3$Bi Structure Type](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26258)
*Lior Verbitsky,Amira Merino,Scott B. Lee,Jaime M. Moya,Sigalit Aharon,Fatmagül Katmer,Sudipta Chatterjee,Grigorii Skorupskii,Josh Leeman,Gabrielle Carrel,Leslie M. Schoop*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究发现并系统表征了$M$Pb$_{4-x}$Bi$_x$（$M$ = Au, Pd, Rh）家族的超导电性，其中PtPb$_3$Bi为成员之一；通过输运与热力学测量确认了体超导态，揭示其为中等各向异性的第二类超导体（type-II superconductor），并指出该体系为研究无序与Pb-Bi混合对重元素金属间化合物超导电性的调控提供了平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找新型超导体兼具基础研究与技术应用价值；近期人工智能方法成功预测PtPb$_3$Bi为超导体，激发了对其所属材料家族的实验探索需求。

Method: 合成了$M$Pb$_{4-x}$Bi$_x$（$M$ = Au, Pd, Rh, Ni）系列化合物；通过电输运（electrical resistivity）、磁化率（magnetization）和比热（specific heat）测量表征超导态，确定临界场、特征长度尺度及各向异性比。

Result: $M$ = Au、Pd、Rh的样品分别于4.9 K、4.2 K和3.4 K进入超导态；三者均为中等各向异性的第二类超导体，上临界场各向异性比$H_{c2}^{\parallel c}/H_{c2}^{\perp c} \approx 1.2$–$1.5$；当$M$ = Ni（半径显著较小）时结构塌缩为不同的Pb取代NiBi$_3$型；化学配比参数$x$随三种化合物变化，使总价电子数（valence electron count）维持在每化学式单元约20个。

Conclusion: $M$Pb$_{4-x}$Bi$_x$（$M$ = Au, Pd, Rh）构成一个各向异性超导体家族，为研究位点无序（site disorder）和Pb-Bi混合如何调控重元素金属间化合物中的超导电性提供了实验平台。

Abstract: The quest for new superconductors is of both fundamental and technological importance. Recently, an artificial intelligence method correctly predicted PtPb$_3$Bi to be a superconductor. In this work, we find superconductivity in the newly synthesized $M$Pb$_{4-x}$Bi$_x$ ($M$ = Au, Pd, and Rh), of which PtPb$_3$Bi is a member. When $M$ = Ni, whose radius is considerably smaller, the structure instead collapses into the different, Pb-substituted NiBi$_3$ type. Interestingly, the stoichiometric parameter $x$ shifts across the three compounds to keep the total valence electron count close to 20 per formula unit. The superconducting transitions occur at 4.9, 4.2, and 3.4 K, for $M$ = Au, Pd, and Rh, respectively. Using electrical resistivity, magnetization, and specific heat measurements, we establish the bulk nature of the superconducting state and determine the critical fields, characteristic length scales, and anisotropy ratios. All three compounds are moderately anisotropic type-II superconductors, with modest upper critical field anisotropies of $H_{c2}^{\parallel c}/H_{c2}^{\perp c} \approx 1.2$ to $1.5$. These results establish $M$Pb$_{4-x}$Bi$_x$ as a family of anisotropic superconductors and a platform for studying how site disorder and Pb-Bi mixing govern superconductivity in heavy-element intermetallics.

</details>


### [110] [Fluctuation-Induced Magnetoelectric Effect in Noncentrosymmetric Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26261)
*Jaglul Hasan,Daniel Shaffer,Maxim Dzero,Alex Levchenko*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了非中心对称二维材料在超导转变温度以上，超导涨落对自旋磁化率和核磁共振弛豫率的影响，发现即使在纯s波单重态配对下，超导涨落也能通过涨落诱导的库珀对产生直接的磁电效应，并增强NMR弛豫率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非中心对称超导体中，由于Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的存在，超导涨落可能产生不同于中心对称体系的新奇磁电响应。本文旨在阐明该体系中超导涨落对自旋磁化率（spin susceptibility）和NMR弛豫率（NMR relaxation rate）的微观机制。

Method: 采用包含线性Rashba自旋-轨道耦合的微观模型（microscopic model），在考虑任意强度杂质散射（impurity scattering）的条件下，计算超导转变温度以上超导涨落对自旋磁化率和NMR弛豫率的贡献。

Result: 超导涨落通过涨落诱导的库珀对（fluctuation-induced Cooper pairs）对自旋磁化率产生直接贡献，即使在纯s波单重态配对（s-wave singlet pairing）下也能产生这种涨落驱动的磁电效应（magnetoelectric effect），该效应在中心对称体系中被禁止。该效应与态密度抑制和量子干涉局域化（quantum-interference localization）造成的磁化率降低相互竞争。此外，超导涨落使NMR弛豫率增强至正常态Korringa值以上，自旋-轨道耦合进一步放大了该效应。

Conclusion: 非中心对称二维材料中，超导涨落可诱导出中心对称体系中不存在的直接磁电响应，且自旋-轨道耦合显著影响涨落对NMR弛豫率的增强行为，提示这一体系在超导涨落物理中具有独特的可观测效应。

Abstract: We study the effect of superconducting fluctuations on the spin susceptibility and NMR relaxation rate in noncentrosymmetric two-dimensional materials above the superconducting transition temperature, considering arbitrary strength of impurity scattering. Employing a microscopic model with linear Rashba spin-orbit coupling, we show that superconducting fluctuations give rise to a direct contribution to the spin susceptibility through fluctuation-induced Cooper pairs. This fluctuation-driven magnetoelectric effect is possible even for purely $s$-wave singlet pairing, a mechanism that is forbidden in centrosymmetric systems. It competes with the reduction of the susceptibility below the Pauli value arising from the combined effects of the suppression of the density of states and quantum-interference localization processes. In contrast, superconducting fluctuations enhance the NMR relaxation rate above its normal-state Korringa value, with spin-orbit coupling providing an additional amplification of this effect.

</details>


### [111] [Quasiclassical theory of nonlinear response in d-wave superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26909)
*Aidan Steineman,Samuel Awelewa,Maxim Dzero*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用自洽的 Keldysh--Nambu 准经典理论，系统研究了清洁 d 波超导体中的两种非线性光学现象——Eliashberg 效应和三次谐波产生。结果表明，在接近临界温度且领先阶近似下，d 波超导体不存在像 s 波超导体那样的 Eliashberg 增强；而在三次谐波产生中，电荷密度涨落通道显著主导 Schmid--Higgs 振幅模贡献，这一行为源自节状准粒子的非平衡动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: d 波超导体（d-wave superconductor）中的光致非线性现象尚未被充分理解，尤其是在与 s 波超导体的对比方面。本研究旨在通过自洽的准经典理论，系统解析清洁 d 波超导体中的两个关键非线性效应：Eliashberg 效应（光致序参量静态修正）和三次谐波产生（third-harmonic generation），以揭示其物理机制与 s 波情形的本质差异。

Method: 采用自洽的 Keldysh--Nambu 准经典理论（self-consistent Keldysh--Nambu quasiclassical theory），对非平衡状态下的 Eilenberger 方程（Eilenberger equation）进行系统的微扰求解，从而导出 Keldysh 传播子（Keldysh propagator）并计算序参量的稳态修正以及三次谐波响应。

Result: 对于稳态修正，发现在接近临界温度且以能隙幅度 Δ 的领先阶近似下，光致序参量变化在所有驱动频率下均为零——清洁 d 波超导体在此阶次不显示 Eliashberg 增强；s 波情形中驱动该效应的能隙增强型准粒子重新分布通道在 d 波情形中被额外的 Δ 幂次抑制。对于三次谐波产生，在宽频率范围内电荷密度涨落（粒子-空穴）通道显著主导 Schmid--Higgs 振幅模贡献，两者仅在 ω≈2√2 Δ 的窄共振窗口附近可比拟（若忽略正常态电流的抗磁部分）。

Conclusion: 清洁 d 波超导体中的非线性光学行为与 s 波超导体有显著差异，这源自其节状准粒子（nodal quasiparticles）的非平衡动力学。节状准粒子必须被显式保留，并且使得响应对外场的偏振方向敏感。这些结论为理解不同对称性超导体的光致非线性现象提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We use a self-consistent Keldysh--Nambu quasiclassical theory to study two related nonlinear phenomena in clean d-wave superconductors: the photo-induced static correction to the order parameter -- the Eliashberg effect -- and third-harmonic generation. Both follow from a systematic perturbative solution of the out-of-equilibrium Eilenberger equation for the Keldysh propagator. For the steady-state correction to the pairing amplitude we find that at temperatures close to the critical temperature and to leading order in the gap magnitude $Δ$, the photo-induced change of the order parameter is zero at all drive frequencies: in contrast to s-wave superconductors, a clean d-wave superconductor exhibits no Eliashberg enhancement at this order. The gap-enhancing quasiparticle-redistribution channel that drives the effect in the s-wave case is suppressed by an additional power of $Δ$ in the d-wave case. For third-harmonic generation we find that the charge-density-fluctuation (particle--hole) channel significantly dominates the Schmid--Higgs amplitude-mode contribution over a broad frequency range, the two becoming comparable only in a narrow window near the resonance frequency $ω\approx 2\sqrt{2}\,Δ$ if one neglects the diamagnetic part of the current in the normal state. We trace this to the nonequilibrium dynamics of nodal quasiparticles, which must be retained explicitly and which also makes the response sensitive to the orientation of the driving field.

</details>


### [112] [High temperature transitions in Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates La$_{n+1}$Ni$_{n}$O$_{3n+1}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27040)
*P. Reiss,A. Shevchenko,P. S. Lizama,J. Nuss,R. Dinnebier,P. A. van Aken,M. Hepting,M. Isobe,Y. E. Suyolcu,H. Takagi,B. Keimer,P. Puphal*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管无限层镍酸盐 (Nd,Sr)NiO₂ 中 15 K 超导及 Ruddlesden–Popper 相 La₃Ni₂O₇ 中 80 K 超导的发现开启了镍酸盐研究的新纪元，但不同报告之间仍存在显著分歧，亟需系统研究以厘清争议。

Method: 采用粉末 X 射线衍射（PXRD）、单晶 X 射线衍射、电子显微镜、热容、差示扫描量热法、磁化率及输运测量等综合实验手段，在 2–1000 K 宽温区内对高质量单晶进行研究。

Conclusion: 该发现揭示了 Ruddlesden–Popper 镍酸盐中一个被忽视的结构转变，为进一步理解其物理性质及超导机制提供了重要线索。

Abstract: The discovery of superconductivity at $15\,\mathrm{K}$ in the infinite-layer nickelate $(\mathrm{Nd},\mathrm{Sr})\mathrm{NiO}_2$, followed by superconductivity at $80\,\mathrm{K}$ in the Ruddlesden--Popper phase $\mathrm{La}_3\mathrm{Ni}_2\mathrm{O}_7$, has ushered in a new era of nickelate research. Despite this progress, large discrepancies between reports exist. Here, we investigate the complete series of bulk-stable $\mathrm{La}_{n+1}\mathrm{Ni}_n\mathrm{O}_{3n+1}$ compounds using a comprehensive set of experimental techniques, including PXRD, single-crystal XRD, electron microscopy, heat capacity, differential scanning calorimetry, magnetic susceptibility, and transport measurements, over a broad temperature range from $2$ to $1000\,\mathrm{K}$. By studying high-quality single crystals, we identify a previously underappreciated high-temperature phase transition in Ruddlesden--Popper nickelates $\mathrm{La}_{n+1}\mathrm{Ni}_n\mathrm{O}_{3n+1}$ distinct from the one going to a tetragonal phase.

### [113] [Axial-Vector Lattice Benchmarks Reveal a Common Medium Response of Meson Screening in Hot QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26245)
*Jie Ren,Chen Chen,Fei Gao,Si-xue Qin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文结合格点QCD基准数据与Dyson-Schwinger方程基线，通过对称性约束的介子屏蔽质量研究热QCD中强子关联的溶解，建立了一种由单点轴向矢量数据确定、其余数据检验、矢量数据验证的理论框架，并预测了轻-粲和含底夸克谱，其赝标量-标量扩展给出了常规手征伙伴体的保守下限估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解热QCD（thermal QCD）中强子关联（hadronic correlations）在高温下如何解离，以及如何通过介子屏蔽质量（meson screening masses）来系统追踪这一过程。

Method: 将格点QCD（lattice-QCD）基准数据与基于对称性保持的Dyson-Schwinger方程（Dyson–Schwinger equation）基线相结合，通过轴向矢量（axial-vector）通道的单点数据确定介质响应，用其余轴向矢量数据进行检验，并用矢量（vector）屏蔽质量进行零参数验证。框架进一步扩展到赝标量-标量（pseudoscalar–scalar）通道以估计手征伙伴（chiral partner）质量。

Result: 识别出味依赖的轴向矢量准自由起始（flavor-dependent axial-vector quasi-free onset）以及有限区间介质响应（finite-interval medium response）。矢量屏蔽质量在无需额外输入的情况下成功验证了该框架。框架预测了轻-粲（light-charm）和含底夸克（bottom-containing）谱，其赝标量-标量扩展给出了手征伙伴体质量的保守下限。

Conclusion: 该框架为热QCD中介子屏蔽质量提供了一种自洽且可检验的描述，可由少量输入构建完整味依赖的介子谱结构，并对手征对称性恢复条件给出保守约束。

Abstract: Meson screening masses trace the dissolution of hadronic correlations in hot QCD. Combining lattice-QCD benchmarks with a symmetry-preserving Dyson--Schwinger baseline, we identify a flavor-dependent axial-vector quasi-free onset and a finite-interval medium response. One axial-vector point fixes the response; remaining axial-vector data test it, and vector screening masses validate it without input. The framework predicts light-charm and bottom-containing spectra; its pseudoscalar--scalar extension gives conservative lower estimates for ordinary chiral partners.

</details>


### [114] [Thermal Emission of Dark Photons from Earth's Core](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26253)
*Hooman Davoudiasl*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出地球炽热核心可能产生亚电子伏特（sub-eV）区域的暗光子（dark photon），并利用地球核心冷却论证以及SENSEI和DAMIC-M等暗物质直接探测实验的约束，估算了暗光子与带电粒子耦合的动力学混合参数（kinetic mixing parameter）$\varepsilon$的界限。结果表明现有实验已能限制新的暗光子参数空间，而计划中的Oscura实验可能将$\varepsilon$的约束边界压低两到三个量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的暗光子产生机制通常聚焦于恒星内部等极端高温环境；本文旨在探讨地球核心这一温度较低但仍足够产生亚电子伏特暗光子的可能性，并评估其可观测的物理效应。

Method: 采用地球核心冷却能量损失论证，结合SENSEI和DAMIC-M暗物质直接探测实验的现有数据，推导暗光子动力学混合参数$\varepsilon$的约束上限；同时也对未来的Oscura实验的探测潜力进行了预估。

Result: 当前SENSEI和DAMIC-M实验的结果已能够覆盖之前未被探索的暗光子参数空间；对于暗光子质量约为$10^{-4}$ eV的情形，Oscura实验可能将$\varepsilon$的现有排除边界再压低两到三个数量级。

Conclusion: 地球核心可作为亚电子伏特暗光子的有效产生源，利用现有和未来的暗物质直接探测实验数据可以显著限制暗光子的动力学混合参数$\varepsilon$，拓展了暗光子理论在低能区的可检验性。

Abstract: Dark photons in the sub-eV regime may be produced by the Earth's hot core, representing a much less extreme environment than stellar cores. We consider this possibility and estimate constraints on the kinetic mixing parameter $\varepsilon$ that governs dark photon coupling to charged particles, using Earth core cooling arguments, as well as dark matter direct detection bounds from SENSEI and DAMIC-M experiments. Our estimates suggest that the current results from these experiments constrain new dark photon parameter space. We also find that the proposed Oscura experiment may reach two to three orders of magnitude below existing bounds on $\varepsilon$, for dark photon masses $\sim 10^{-4}$ eV, depending on the assumed parameters characterizing the Earth core.

### [115] [Unified study of hyperon semileptonic decays in a relativistic three-quark model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26596)
*Ru-Hui Ni,Zhen-Yang Wang,Jia-Jun Wu,Bing-Song Zou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于相对论性三夸克模型（R3QM）对基态八重态超子的半轻子衰变进行了统一理论研究。所有重子波函数通过拟合重子质谱确定，进而无自由参数地预言弱跃迁振幅、分支比、轻子普适性比值及完整的八重态跃迁形状因子（form factors）。计算与现有实验数据及格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）结果吻合良好，并预言了缺乏实验信息的衰变道。完整形状因子集分离了弱磁、第二类流及部分轴矢流守恒（PCAC）关系的极点贡献，揭示了弱磁项最强的道依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对基态八重态超子的半轻子衰变进行统一的理论研究，以连接夸克层次的重子自旋-味（spin-flavor）与空间结构，并为未来的超子半轻子衰变实验提供可检验的弱电流可观测量。

Method: 采用相对论性三夸克模型（relativistic three-quark model, R3QM），所有重子波函数通过半相对论性势模型（semirelativistic potential model）拟合重子质谱确定，从而无自由参数地预言弱跃迁振幅、分支比、轻子普适性比值（lepton flavor universality ratios）及完整的八重态跃迁形状因子。

Result: 计算的分支比与可用实验数据一致，并对实验信息有限的衰变道给出了预言。在Λ→p ℓ⁻ν̄ℓ道中，领头矢量形状因子f₁(0)和轴矢量形状因子g₁(0)与近期格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）结果吻合，g₁/f₁比值与BESIII测量一致。弱磁项f₂展现出最清晰的道依赖性，其在某些道中的较小值可能暗示纯qqq价成分未能完全饱和横向流强度。

Conclusion: 该框架有效连接了八重态超子弱形状因子与夸克层次的重子自旋-味和空间结构，为未来超子半轻子衰变测量提供了可检验的弱电流可观测量。

Abstract: We present a unified theoretical study of semileptonic decays of ground-state octet hyperons using the relativistic three-quark model (R3QM). A key innovation of our approach is that all baryon wave functions are determined by fitting the baryon mass spectrum with a semirelativistic potential model, leading to predictions for weak transition amplitudes without free parameters. With the same wave functions, we calculate the branching fractions and lepton flavor universality ratios for the octet channels. The calculated values agree with the available experimental data and give predictions for channels with limited experimental information. We further compute the complete set of octet transition form factors without any additional free parameters, so that the weak current can be examined beyond the rate observables. In the well-measured $Λ\to p \ell^-\barν_\ell$ channel, the calculated leading vector and axial-vector form factors, $f_1(0)$ and $g_1(0)$, agree well with recent lattice QCD results, and the $g_1/f_1$ ratio is consistent with recent BESIII measurements. Beyond the leading vector and axial-vector terms, the complete form factor set separates the weak magnetism, second class, and the pole contribution associated with the partially conserved axial current (PCAC) relation. The weak magnetism term $f_2$ shows the clearest channel dependence compared with lattice QCD results, and its smaller values in some channels may point to transverse current strength not fully saturated by pure $qqq$ valence components. This work provides a framework for connecting octet hyperon weak form factors to the spin--flavor and spatial structure of baryons at the quark level, and gives testable weak current observables for future hyperon semileptonic decay measurements.

</details>


### [116] [RG Running of Multiple Neutrino Mixing Parameters at Oscillation Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26720)
*Peter B. Denton,Shao-Feng Ge,Chui-Fan Kong,Pedro Pasquini*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究新物理尺度在微子振荡实验能标内时，重整化群（renormalization group）演化效应在不同实验间产生的可观测影响，并提出通过联合多个微子振荡实验（DUNE-ND、JUNO-TAO、FASERν2）来解耦多个RG运行参数。结果表明，实验组合对新物理的运行效应具有强灵敏度，尤其能解决非平凡简并性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当新物理尺度落在微子振荡实验能标范围内时，重整化群（renormalization group）运行效应可能在产生与探测过程之间以及不同实验之间产生影响，因此需要利用多个微子振荡实验来区分多个RG运行参数。

Method: 采用一般性的模型无关（model-independent）分析方法，针对多种味结构（flavor structures），在即将开展的DUNE-ND、JUNO-TAO和FASERν2实验背景下进行研究；这些实验覆盖了大范围的微子能量和多种味组合。

Result: 联合这些实验的组合对新物理的运行效应表现出强灵敏度（strong sensitivity），尤其具备解决非平凡简并性（non-trivial degeneracies）的能力。

Conclusion: 多个微子振荡实验的联合分析能够有效探测新物理的重整化群运行效应，并克服参数简并问题。

Abstract: If the new physics scale is within the energy scale of neutrino oscillation experiments, it may lead to a renormalization group (RG) running effect between the production and detection processes as well as between different experiments. It is then possible to use multiple neutrino oscillation experiments to disentangle the multiple RG running parameters. We investigate this effect in a general model-independent sense for a variety of flavor structures in the context of upcoming experiments DUNE-ND, JUNO-TAO, and FASER$ν$2 that span a large range in neutrino energies and many different flavor combinations. We find strong sensitivity to the running effects of new physics with combination of these experiments, especially the possibility of addressing the non-trivial degeneracies.

</details>


### [117] [The Effect of Topological Defects and Magnetic Flux on Fully-Heavy Tetraquarks and Mass Spectra of Heavy Quarkonia Using the Analytical Exact Iteration Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27363)
*N. H. Gerish,M. Abu-Shady,E. M. Khokha*

TL;DR: 本文采用解析精确迭代法（AEIM），在拓扑缺陷和外磁通存在下求解非相对论薛定谔方程，利用修正Cornell势（含谐振和反平方项）成功计算了重夸克偶素（c\bar{c}和b\bar{b}）及全重四夸克态（cc\bar{c}\bar{c}和bb\bar{b}\bar{b}）的能谱与质量，结果与理论预测和实验数据高度一致。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用解析精确迭代法（analytical exact iteration method, AEIM）在拓扑缺陷和外磁通存在下求解非相对论薛定谔方程；相互作用由修正Cornell势（modified Cornell potential）加上谐振项（harmonic term）和反二次项（inverse quadratic term）建模。

Result: 能级被拓扑缺陷参数α显著移动；成功计算了多个径向和轨道激发态下重夸克偶素及全重四夸克态的质量谱；底偶素（bottomonium）和粲偶素（charmonium）的计算质量与现有理论预测和实验发现吻合良好；全重四夸克态的结果与将四夸克视为双夸克-反双夸克（diquark-antidiquark）构型的理论研究一致。

Conclusion: 约束势（confining potential）与背景时空几何（background space-time geometry）之间的非平凡相互作用决定了这些奇特强子态的质量层级；该方法提供了与既有理论模型和实验基准高度一致的高精度数据。

Abstract: Investigating the non-perturbative behavior of QCD and the dynamics of strong interaction is crucial for the study of heavy quarkonia and the understanding of exotic fully-heavy tetraquarks. In this work, using the analytical exact iteration method (AEIM), the analytical eigenvalue solutions of the non-relativistic Schrödinger equation are obtained in the presence of topological defects and external magnetic flux. The interactions are modelled using a modified Cornell potential supplemented by harmonic and inverse quadratic terms. We demonstrate that the energy levels are distinctly shifted by the topological defect parameter ($α$). The mass spectra of heavy quarkonia ($c\bar{c}$ and $b\bar{b}$) and fully-heavy tetraquarks ($cc\bar{c}\bar{c}$ and $bb\bar{b}\bar{b}$) across several radial and orbital excitation states are successfully calculated using this approach. The computed masses of bottomonium and charmonium accord well with current theoretical predictions and experimental findings. Our findings for the heavy tetraquarks are in line with previous theoretical investigations that consider tetraquarks as configurations of diquarks and antidiquarks. The numerical results demonstrate that a nontrivial interaction between the confining potential and the background space-time geometry governs the mass hierarchy of these exotic hadronic states, providing high-precision data with excellent agreement with established theoretical models and experimental benchmarks.

### [118] [Torsional four-fermion interaction for Majorana neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26676)
*Indrajit Ghose,Amitabha Lahiri*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明费米子会产生时空挠率（spacetime torsion），而挠率可被消除后等效为四费米子相互作用（four-fermion interaction），该相互作用为中微子在介质中传播提供有效质量，与电弱相互作用中的Wolfenstein项类似。对于通过I型跷跷板机制（Type I SeeSaw mechanism）获得质量的马约拉纳中微子（Majorana fermions），挠率诱导的项还会通过惰性中微子（sterile neutrinos）与所有费米子的耦合以及新混合参数引入额外效应。研究分别考虑了挠率相互作用在质量基（mass basis）中对角化与非对角化情形下，含一个惰性中微子与一个或两个活性中微子的不同场景，并解析地找到了这些修正，最后在2+1场景中讨论了T破坏（T violation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索费米子产生的时空挠率如何通过等效四费米子相互作用影响中微子在介质中的传播，特别是对马约拉纳中微子通过跷跷板机制获得质量时的额外效应，并系统分析不同场景下的修正及T破坏。

Method: 采用解析方法，分别考虑含一个惰性中微子和一个或两个活性中微子的场景，区分挠率相互作用在质量基中对角化与非对角化两种情形，推导出相应的修正表达式。

Result: 费米子产生的时空挠率可被消除并等效为四费米子相互作用，该相互作用为中微子在介质中传播贡献有效质量，类似于电弱相互作用的Wolfenstein项。惰性中微子通过挠率诱导项与所有费米子耦合，引入额外效应和新混合参数。在2+1场景中讨论了T破坏的具体表现。

Conclusion: 时空挠率通过等效四费米子相互作用为中微子传播提供新的修正机制，该效应与跷跷板机制和马约拉纳中微子性质结合，在多个场景下产生可解析计算的物理修正，其中T破坏在特定场景中具有可讨论的特征。

Abstract: Fermions generate spacetime torsion, which can be eliminated, leaving behind an effective four-fermion interaction. This term will contribute an effective mass for neutrinos propagating through matter, similar to the Wolfenstein term coming from electroweak interactions. When the neutrinos are Majorana fermions and become massive via the Type I SeeSaw mechanism, there can be additional effects due to sterile neutrinos interacting with all fermions via the torsion-induced term, as well as due to the presence of new mixing parameters. We consider different scenarios with one sterile and one or two active neutrinos -- when the torsional interaction is diagonal in the mass basis and when it is not -- and analytically find these modifications. The T violation in the 2+1 scenario is discussed for some specific mixing between the torsion fields and the mass fields.
