### [119] [Coherent collective response in many-qubit systems for dark matter detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26736)
*Ryuichiro Kitano,Ryoto Takai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于 $N$ 叠加态 $(|0\rangle+ |1\rangle)^{\otimes N}$ 的拉姆齐型干涉仪阵列，用于探测波状暗物质（wave-like dark matter）。信号为检测到 0 和 1 的概率不平衡，信噪比正比于 $\sqrt{N} α$，灵敏度标度为 $δα\sim 1 / \sqrt{N}$。与拉比型方案相比，该方法无需纠缠态即可实现相同标度，可利用大量位于暗物质德布罗意波长内的量子比特进行测量。以离子阱量子比特（trapped-ion qubits）为例，当 $N \gtrsim 10^6$ 时，其投影灵敏度可匹敌或超越现有实验室、天体物理及宇宙学限制；该方法亦可推广至高频引力波探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有波状暗物质探测方案（如基于拉比型跃迁的方案）需要高度纠缠的多量子比特（entangled qubits）才能达到 $1/\sqrt{N}$ 的灵敏度标度，这限制了可扩展的量子比特数目。作者希望提出一种无需纠缠态即可实现相同灵敏度标度的新方案，从而允许使用大量量子比特（$N$ 可高达 $10^6$ 以上）来提升探测能力。

Method: 采用拉姆齐型干涉仪（Ramsey-type interferometer）阵列，利用 $N$ 个叠加态 $(|0\rangle+ |1\rangle)^{\otimes N}$ 作为传感器。暗物质波诱导致比特相干跃迁（coherent qubit transitions）后，通过测量检测到 0 和 1 的概率不平衡（imbalance）来提取信号。该方法不依赖纠缠态，只需将大量量子比特放置在暗物质的德布罗意波长（de Broglie wavelength）内即可实现 $N$ 的扩大。

Result: 拉姆齐型方案的信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, SNR）正比于 $\sqrt{N} α$，灵敏度对耦合常数 $α$ 的标度为 $δα \sim 1/\sqrt{N}$。在使用线性保罗阱（linear Paul trap）中的离子阱量子比特作为传感器时，当 $N \gtrsim 10^6$，投影灵敏度可匹敌或超越现有实验室、天体物理和宇宙学（astrophysical and cosmological）限制。该框架原则上还可用于高频引力波（high-frequency gravitational waves）的灵敏度评估。

Conclusion: 拉姆齐型干涉仪方案提供了一种无需纠缠态即可实现 $1/\sqrt{N}$ 灵敏度标度的暗物质探测方法，显著降低了大规模量子比特阵列的工程门槛。该通用框架（general framework）不仅适用于离子阱平台，还有望推广至其他量子传感平台（quantum sensing platforms），并拓展到引力波探测等领域。

Abstract: We propose an array of the Ramsey-type interferometers using $N$ superposition states, $(|0\rangle+ |1\rangle)^{\otimes N}$, as a sensor to detect wave-like dark matter. After the exposure to the dark matter wave, which induces the coherent qubit transitions, the signal is the imbalance between the probabilities of detecting 0 and 1. The signal-to-noise ratio in this scheme is proportional to $\sqrt{N} α$, where $α$ is the coupling of dark matter to the qubits, and thus the sensitivity to the coupling scales as $δα\sim 1 / \sqrt{N}$. For comparison, in the detection scheme based on the Rabi-type transition, $|0\rangle \to |1\rangle$, this scaling is achieved only when highly entangled $N$ qubits are used. Since the Ramsey-type measurement does not require entangled states, one can consider much larger $N$ by simply placing a large number of qubits within the de Broglie wavelength of the dark matter. We demonstrate that, using trapped-ion qubits in a linear Paul trap as the sensor, the projected sensitivity to the coupling matches or surpasses existing laboratory, astrophysical, and cosmological bounds for $N \gtrsim 10^6$. We also evaluate its sensitivity to high-frequency gravitational waves. Our general framework should, in principle, be useful for other quantum sensing platforms.

</details>


### [120] [Unitarity Cuts, t-channel Divergences and the KLN Theorem for Unstable Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26586)
*Marko Beocanin,Michael A. Schmidt*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对包含无质量或不稳定粒子的唯象计算中出现的发散问题，通过研究一个t-道发散示例模型，提出了一套实际应用Kinoshita-Lee-Nauenberg定理的操作方案，展示了多种正规化方案下的抵消机制，并朝着构建有限、固定阶、包含性t-道对撞可观测量迈出了关键步骤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 涉及无质量或不稳定粒子的唯象计算常常因中间粒子在壳发散而失效；尽管Kinoshita-Lee-Nauenberg定理在理论上保证通过求和所有物理简并过程可使发散抵消，但实际应用该定理时面临非连通图、分布性对象、阈值行为和正规化依赖等技术难题。

Method: 通过构造一个呈现t-道发散(t-channel divergence)的示例模型，制定处理上述技术问题的实际准则；在多种正规化方案(regularization schemes)下展示KLN抵消机制的细节，并与底层振幅的复解析结构(complex-analytic structure)建立联系。

Result: 在多个正规化方案中验证了KLN定理的精细抵消过程；揭示了发散抵消与振幅复解析结构之间的关联；初步构建了一个有限且包含性(inclusive)的t-道固定阶对撞可观测量。

Conclusion: 该工作既凸显了KLN定理的实用价值，也揭示了在实际应用中存在的技术微妙之处和未解决的问题，为进一步发展有限、包含性对撞观测量提供了系统性的方法论基础。

Abstract: Many phenomenological calculations involving massless or unstable particles suffer from divergences as mediating particles go on-shell. One way to deal with these divergences is via the Kinoshita-Lee-Nauenberg (KLN) theorem, which guarantees that by summing over all physically-degenerate processes, the divergences cancel and inclusive observables remain finite. However, actually implementing this theorem in practice requires handling disconnected diagrams, ill-defined distributional objects, threshold behavior and subtle regulator dependence. In this work, we formulate practical prescriptions for dealing with some of these issues by studying the KLN cancellation in an illustrative model exhibiting a t-channel divergence. We demonstrate intricate cancellations across several regularization schemes, connect our results to the complex-analytic structure of the underlying amplitudes, and take steps towards constructing a finite, fixed-order, inclusive t-channel collider observable. This work highlights both the utility of the KLN theorem, and also the technical subtleties and open questions involved with applying it in practice.

### [121] [CHESS: CHEbyshev pSeudo-Spectral transport for Feynman integral differential equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26691)
*Yuanche Liu,Yang Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文介绍CHESS（CHEbyshev pSeudo Spectrum）——一个基于Wolfram Language的高精度软件包，用于求解费曼主积分（Feynman master integrals）的ε因子化微分方程（ε-factorized differential equations）。该程序结合切比雪夫-洛巴托谱配置法（Chebyshev-Lobatto spectral collocation）、稀疏矩阵组装、ε展开顺序传播以及基于留数的虚假正则奇点正则化技术，在多尺度积分族基准测试中展现出快速节点收敛、与参考数据吻合良好以及更短的运行时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理中费曼积分（Feynman integrals）的精确与高效数值求解对多圈计算至关重要，但现有方法在处理多尺度积分族时面临计算效率与精度的挑战。开发一种兼具高精度与高性能的数值求解工具是推动相关领域研究的实际需求。

Method: CHESS 软件包的核心方法包括：(1) 将微分一次形式（differential one-form）沿选定路径拉回（pullback）得到矩阵，该矩阵可直接提供或由常数矩阵与预计算的标量拉回组装而成；(2) 采用切比雪夫-洛巴托谱配置法（Chebyshev-Lobatto spectral collocation）进行离散化；(3) 利用稀疏矩阵组装（sparse matrix assembly）提升计算效率；(4) 通过ε展开（ε-expansion）顺序传播实现逐阶求解；(5) 引入基于留数（residue）的正则化方法处理虚假正则奇点（spurious regular singular endpoints）。

Result: 在大型多尺度积分族基准测试中，该方法展现出快速的节点收敛（rapid node convergence），并与可获得的独立参考数据一致。在固定局域级数（fixed local-series）对比中，切比雪夫输运（Chebyshev transports）的壁钟时间（wall times）更短；对于较小规模的并行运行，报告的过程树内存使用量（process-tree memory usage）相当，而在最大基准系统中则更低。

Conclusion: CHESS 软件包为费曼主积分的ε因子化微分方程提供了一种高精度、高效率的一维数值求解方案，尤其适用于多尺度积分族。其结合谱方法与稀疏矩阵技术的策略，在精度、收敛速度与资源消耗方面均优于传统方法，为高能物理多圈计算提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We present CHESS (CHEbyshev pSeudo Spectrum), a Wolfram Language package for high-precision one-dimensional transport of ε-factorized differential equations for Feynman master integrals. The solver works with the matrix obtained by pulling a differential one-form to a chosen path. This matrix may be supplied directly, or assembled from constant matrices and precomputed scalar pullbacks of the one-forms. The program combines Chebyshev-Lobatto spectral collocation, sparse matrix assembly, sequential propagation in the ε-expansion, and residue-based regularization of spurious regular singular endpoints. Benchmarks for large multi-scale integral families show rapid node convergence and agreement with independent reference data where such data are available. In the fixed local-series comparison used here, the Chebyshev transports also give shorter wall times; the reported process-tree memory usage is comparable for the smaller parallel runs and lower for the largest benchmark system in that comparison.

</details>

### [122] [An integrable approach to macroscopic fluctuation theory for the multispecies SSEP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27186)
*Luigi Cantini*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了无限直线上多物种对称简单排斥过程（mSSEP）的宏观涨落理论（MFT），通过逆散射方法求解可积的MFT鞍点方程，推导出多物种电流的累积量生成函数，并证明该函数与单物种情形下Derrida–Gerschenfeld所得结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将单物种对称简单排斥过程（SSEP）的宏观涨落理论推广至多物种情形，并利用其可积结构直接计算多物种电流的大偏差（large deviations）统计性质，从而揭示多物种系统中涨落行为的普适性。

Method: 首先将Derrida–Gerschenfeld的论证推广到多物种情境，证明任意图上多物种电流的累积量生成函数仅依赖于单个标量变量ω；然后在无限直线上建立mSSEP的MFT鞍点方程，通过Zakharov–Takhtajan规范变换将其转化为AKNS形式的可积系统，并运用逆散射方法（inverse scattering method）求解该线性散射问题。

Result: 恢复出多物种电流的累积量生成函数F(ω)及条件于指定电流涨落的初始与最终密度分布；证明F(ω)与Derrida–Gerschenfeld在单物种SSEP中获得的函数形式相同，表明该函数对于任意物种数目均成立。

Conclusion: 多物种对称简单排斥过程的宏观涨落理论具有可积结构，其电流大偏差函数与单物种情形一致，体现了不同物种数下涨落统计的普适性。

Abstract: We study the macroscopic fluctuation theory (MFT) of a multispecies generalization of the symmetric simple exclusion process (mSSEP) on the infinite line, in which particles of $N+1$ species -- including, possibly, a vacancy species -- exchange positions at unit rate. Working with the full, redundant set of coarse-grained densities $\bfrho=\{ρ_0,\dots,ρ_N\}$ keeps the relabelling symmetry of the model manifest throughout. We first extend the argument of Derrida and Gerschenfeld to the multispecies setting, showing that the cumulant generating function of the multispecies current between two regions of an arbitrary graph depends on the boundary densities $ \bfrho_L,\bfrho_R$ and on the fugacities $\bflambda$ only through a single scalar variable $ω$. We then formulate the MFT saddle-point equations for the mSSEP on the infinite line and show that they define an integrable system: they are of Landau--Lifshitz type, and a Zakharov--Takhtajan gauge transformation recasts them in AKNS form. Solving the resulting linear scattering problem by the inverse scattering method, we recover the cumulant generating function $F(ω)$ for the multispecies current, as well as the initial and final density profiles conditioned on a prescribed current fluctuation. In particular, we show that $F(ω)$ coincides with the function obtained by Derrida and Gerschenfeld for the single-species SSEP, now derived for an arbitrary number of species directly from the integrable structure of the multispecies MFT equations.

</details>


### [123] [Field theories for Laplacian Growth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27263)
*Paolo Pisapia,Assaf Shapira,Kay Joerg Wiese*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明回路擦除随机游走（LERW）、n=-2下的O(n)模型与拉普拉斯随机游走（LRW）是同一随机过程的三种实现，并构造了LRW的精确格点作用量（lattice action），将其微扰展开与LERW等价，进而推广至b-LRW和扩散受限聚集（DLA）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造了LRW的精确格点作用量，并证明其微扰展开（perturbative expansion）与LERW的微扰展开等价。进而将该方法推广至b-LRW和DLA。

Result: 成功构造了LRW的格点作用量，建立了LRW与LERW在微扰展开层面的等价性，并将该框架扩展到了b-LRW和DLA。

Conclusion: 该工作为LRW、LERW及其推广过程（b-LRW和DLA）提供了统一的场论描述，为后续的重整化群分析奠定了基础。

While this equivalence holds on any graph, renormalization is possible only via the $O(-2)$-model. To generalize LRWs to $b$-LRWs or to Diffusion Limited Aggregation (DLA), a field theory directly on the Laplacian growth process is necessary. Here we construct an exact lattice action for LRWs and show that its perturbative expansion equals that of LERWs. We then generalize this approach to $b$-LRWs and DLA.

### [124] [Exact subsystem dynamics in the deterministic Floquet-PXP model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27337)
*Katja Klobas*

TL;DR: 本文证明了规则 201（Rule 201），即 Floquet-PXP 模型的确定性版本，是一个可精确求解量子多体系统子区域动力学的实例：其影响矩阵（influence matrix）可由有限维矩阵乘积算符（matrix-product operator, MPO）表示，满足有限代数条件，并给出了多点自关联函数（multi-time autocorrelation function）的解析刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解热力学大尺度量子多体系统中局域子系统的动力学，该系统可视为开放系统，其自身产生等效热库（effective bath）。该热库的作用可用影响矩阵（influence matrix）刻画，但一般情况下其复杂度随时间增长，因此寻找可精确求解的特殊情形具有重要理论价值。

Method: 将规则 201（Rule 201）——Floquet-PXP 模型的确定性版本——识别为可解析求解的实例，证明其影响矩阵可表示为有限维矩阵乘积算符（MPO），并求解一组有限的代数条件以完全刻画该影响矩阵。

Result: 规则 201 的影响矩阵具有有限维矩阵乘积算符（MPO）形式，满足有限代数条件，且其多点自关联函数（multi-time autocorrelation function）可被精确表征。

Conclusion: 规则 201 是一类可精确求解影响矩阵的量子多体系统，即使在存在非平凡相互作用（non-trivial interactions）的情形下仍可完全刻画其影响矩阵，为理解开放量子多体系统中热库效应提供了可解析计算的范例。

Abstract: The dynamics of local subsystems in a thermodynamically large quantum many-body system can be understood as effectively open as the system produces its own effective bath. The action of this bath can be characterised in terms of the so-called influence matrices. In generic situations, the complexity of these objects grows unfavourably with time, however, there exist solvable cases where influence matrices can be characterised exactly even in the presence of non-trivial interactions. Here we show that Rule 201, a deterministic version of the Floquet-PXP model, is one of these solvable instances. Indeed, it admits influence matrices given by a finite-dimensional matrix-product operator (MPO) that solves a finite set of algebraic conditions. We provide the solution, and characterise multi-time autocorrelation functions.

</details>


### [125] [Odd transport in a two-temperature Brownian dimer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27012)
*Iman Abdoli,Hartmut Löwen*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究以具有奇迁移率（odd mobility）的双温布朗二聚体为可控范式，通过精确解揭示了奇迁移率如何在与温度不平衡和弹性耦合共同作用下，产生手性关联与反向旋转的环流，并增强热导而不改变净热流与总耗散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索奇迁移率作为非平衡动力学（nonequilibrium dynamics）中一种受控范式的行为，尤其是其如何在不依赖外力矩（external torques）、空间各向异性（spatial anisotropy）或非保守驱动（nonconservative driving）的情况下，将保守力转化为横向运动并产生手性关联与环流。

Method: 研究一个由弹性弹簧耦合的两个谐振子（harmonically confined particles）组成的双温布朗二聚体（two-temperature Brownian dimer），系统与不同温度的储热库（reservoirs）相连，并赋予系统奇迁移率（odd mobility），即反对称输运系数（antisymmetric transport coefficients）；通过精确求解获得稳态行为。

Result: 奇迁移率使两个粒子之间产生手性关联（handed correlations），但单个粒子的分布保持各向同性；稳态概率流包含两部分：普通不可逆流与奇迁移率产生的手性贡献，该手性贡献在单粒子投影下表现为陷阱内的反向旋转环流；奇迁移率增强热导（thermal conductance），但净热流与总耗散在奇手性反转下保持不变。

Conclusion: 奇迁移率、温度不平衡与弹性耦合三者的协同作用是产生手性关联的必要条件；奇迁移率可作为一种可控机制来调节热输运，而不改变能量与熵产生的整体平衡。

Abstract: We investigate a two-temperature Brownian dimer with odd mobility, characterized by antisymmetric transport coefficients, as a controlled paradigm for odd nonequilibrium dynamics. The system is made of two harmonically confined particles coupled by an elastic spring and connected to reservoirs at different temperatures. Odd mobility converts conservative forces into transverse motion, linking heat exchange to circulating probability currents without requiring external torques, spatial anisotropy, or nonconservative driving. Our exact solution shows that odd mobility creates handed correlations between the two particles while leaving the individual particle distributions isotropic. These correlations arise only when temperature imbalance, elastic coupling, and odd mobility act together, and their handedness reverses when the odd response is reversed. The steady probability current contains two distinct parts: the ordinary irreversible current of a two-temperature dimer and an additional handed contribution generated by odd mobility. When projected onto the motion of each particle, this handed contribution becomes a pair of counter-rotating circulating currents inside the traps. Based on the currents we compute the heat transfer and entropy production analytically. We show that odd mobility enhances thermal conductance between the reservoirs, while the net heat current and total dissipation remain unchanged under reversal of the odd handedness.

</details>


### [126] [Proactivity and pinning in the non-reciprocal XY model with vision anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27310)
*Gabriele Bandini,Asja Jelic,Andrea Gambassi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在方形晶格上研究非互易XY模型（non-reciprocal XY model），系统分析了由视觉诱导的各向异性相互作用（vision-induced anisotropic interaction）引起的自旋取向钉扎（pinning）现象，识别了Langevin动力学框架中产生的反应项（reactive term）和主动项（proactive term）两种不同贡献，并据此澄清了局部与全局钉扎的机制差异，为晶格诱导的取向选择提供了微观理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非互易XY模型中由各向异性相互作用引发的自旋取向钉扎现象，澄清之前研究中关于局部与全局钉扎机制及晶格偏好方向选择的差异和矛盾。

Method: 在方形晶格上定义非互易XY模型，自旋通过视觉诱导的各向异性相互作用与最近邻耦合；研究了四种相互作用核（modulated、sinusoidal、von Mises、hard vision-cone couplings）和两类微观更新规则（Glauber动力学和Langevin动力学）；在Langevin公式中识别并分析了反应项和主动项两种贡献，推导了控制局部涨落和全局取向的方程。

Result: 反应项和主动项均可产生全局钉扎（global pinning）；二者在局部钉扎（local pinning）中的作用依赖于具体的相互作用核，且可能存在定性差异；明确了局部钉扎与全局钉扎之间的区别。

Conclusion: 解释了不同模型中晶格偏好方向（preferred lattice directions）的产生机制，调和了先前研究中的明显矛盾，为非互易XY模型中晶格诱导的取向选择（orientational selection）提供了微观框架。

Abstract: We study a non-reciprocal XY model on a square lattice, in which spins interact with their nearest neighbors through vision-induced anisotropic interaction. Such anisotropy breaks rotational symmetry and leads to the pinning of the spin orientation along preferred lattice directions. We systematically characterize this phenomenon for different interaction kernels, including modulated, sinusoidal, von Mises, and hard vision-cone couplings, and for two classes of microscopic update rules: Glauber and Langevin dynamics. A central result of this work is the identification and detailed analysis of two distinct contributions that naturally arise in the Langevin formulation, which we refer to as the reactive and the proactive term. We derive the corresponding equations governing both local fluctuations and the global orientation, and use them to characterize the mechanisms responsible for directional pinning. We show that both reactive and proactive contributions can generate global pinning, whereas their role in determining local pinning depends on the specific interaction kernel and may differ qualitatively. Our analysis clarifies the distinction between local and global pinning, explains the emergence of preferred lattice directions in the different models considered, and reconciles apparent discrepancies reported in previous studies. More generally, it provides a microscopic framework for understanding lattice-induced orientational selection in non-reciprocal XY models.

### [127] [An Arbitrary-Lagrangian-Eulerian solver for relativistic detonation waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27113)
*Sara Rinaldi,Olindo Zanotti,Michael Dumbser*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文通过理论分析与数值模拟研究了相对论性爆轰波（relativistic detonation wave）的动力学行为，提出了一种在总能量密度中引入反应项并保持守恒方程形式不变的框架，开发了相应的二阶有限体积ALE数值方案，并发现了一个新的狭义相对论效应：相对论情形下Zel'dovich压力跳跃随质量通量的变化呈现非单调行为（先降后升），与牛顿爆轰波中的单调递减行为截然不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 爆轰波（detonation wave）在相对论性天体物理环境（如超新星、伽马射线暴）中具有重要应用，但现有研究对相对论效应如何影响爆轰波结构（特别是Zel'dovich-von Neumann-Doering (ZND) profile）的理解尚不充分，亟需发展适用于相对论情形下的理论框架与高效数值方案。

Method: 在总能量密度定义中引入一个额外项来物理地刻画化学反应，并添加一个关于反应物质量分数（mass fraction）演化的额外方程，同时保持质量守恒与能量-动量守恒方程形式不变。数值求解采用具有TVD重构的**二阶有限体积ALE格式**，网格速度取为激波速度；对反应源项可能导致的刚性问题采用局部隐式算法处理；并提出了一种从守恒变量到原始变量的高效转换算法，以克服相对论Euler方程中这一转换的固有困难。

Result: 成功求解了相对论性爆轰波的ZND剖面，激波前洛伦兹因子（Lorentz factor）可达γ_S~7。发现了一个新的狭义相对论效应：在牛顿爆轰波中，Zel'dovich压力跳跃随穿过激波的质量通量单调递减；但在相对论情形下，该压力跳跃先降至最小值后单调上升。

Conclusion: 该非单调行为可能对相对论性爆轰波中可提取的能量具有重要的物理含义，为理解高能天体物理现象中的能量释放机制提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: In this paper we study the dynamics of relativistic detonation waves theoretically and numerically. The reaction is physically accounted for by an extra term in the definition of the total energy density and by an additional equation for the evolution of the mass fraction of the reactant, while leaving formally unmodified the equations of mass and energy-momentum conservation. In this way, the Rankine-Hugoniot relations maintain the same formal structure of the inert version. For the numerical solution we use a second order finite volume ALE scheme with TVD reconstruction, where the mesh velocity is chosen equal to the shock speed. We also adopt a locally implicit algorithm for the treatment of potentially stiff reaction source terms that arise in the equation of the reactant. We furthermore propose a particularly efficient algorithm for the conversion from the conserved to the primitive variables, which for the relativistic Euler equations is known to be nontrivial. Following this approach, we can successfully solve the Zel'dovich-von Neumann-Doering profile of a relativistsic detonation wave, up to Lorentz factors of the shock front $γ_S\sim 7$. Our analysis allowed us to highlight a new special relativistic effect, which has remained unnoticed so far. While in Newtonian detonations the Zel'dovich pressure jump decreases monotonically with the mass flux through the shock front, in the relativistic case it shows a minimum and then rises monotonically as a function of the mass flux. This may have interesting physical implications on the amount of energy that can be extracted from a relativistic detonation wave.

</details>

### [128] [Beyond Feedforward Networks: Reentry Neural Systems as the Fundamental Basis of Subjecthood and Intrinsic Safety of Next-Generation AGI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26406)
*A. S. Ushakov,Yu. N. Berdinsk*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于闭环递归循环（D ↔ I cycle）的安全通用人工智能（safe AGI）完整架构蓝图。该架构通过结构循环（C≥1）和自持放大（ρ>1）数学保证自模型、工具性自我保存和未编程的目标导向行为的涌现。目标被编码为非线性D-向量，免疫于重解释和提示注入。文章还提出了S度量——一种多项式时间可计算的集成信息替代指标，并提供Lean 4机器验证的形式化证明。完整实现包括Python/NumPy代码、工业级水平扩展方案、六代AI演化分类学、未来递归架构动物园、规范不变网络及八个可证伪预测。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 架构核心是一个闭环递归循环（D ↔ I cycle），包含结构循环（structural cycle, C≥1）和自持放大（self-sustaining amplification, ρ>1），数学上保证自模型和目标导向行为涌现。目标以非线性D-向量（D-vector）形式编码在架构中。提出S度量（S-measure），一种多项式时间[O(N³)]可计算的集成信息指标，并提供Lean 4机器验证的形式化证明。同时提供基于Tarjan算法的循环复杂度计算、Delta-S屏障等Python/NumPy开源实现，以及基于Apache Kafka和Docker Compose的工业水平扩展方案。

Result: Lean 4机器验证证明S>0蕴含正集成信息（positive integrated information）。架构可部署于当前硬件，并包含六代AI演化分类学、未来递归架构动物园（RAS、扩散吸引子、分形循环等）、规范不变网络（gauge-invariant networks）用于安全群体智能、容错与恢复协议，以及八个可证伪预测。

Conclusion: 该架构是拓扑受保护、天生安全的AGI设计，可于当前技术条件下部署。所有形式化证明均经过Lean 4机器验证，提供了从理论到工程实现的完整路径。

Abstract: We propose a complete architectural blueprint for safe artificial general intelligence based on a closed reentry loop (D <-> I cycle). In contrast to feedforward networks, which are directed acyclic graphs (C=0, S=0) incapable of self-reference, the proposed architecture contains a structural cycle (C >= 1) with self-sustaining amplification (rho > 1), mathematically guaranteeing the emergence of a self-model, instrumental self-preservation, and unprogrammed goal-directed behaviour. The agent's goals are encoded as a non-textual D-vector in the architecture itself, making them immune to reinterpretation and prompt injection. We present the S-measure -- a polynomial-time [O(N^3)] computable alternative to Tononi's NP-hard Phi -- with machine-verified Lean 4 proof that S>0 implies positive integrated information. The work provides full Python/NumPy implementations (Tarjan-based cycle complexity, Delta-S barrier), industrial horizontal scaling via Apache Kafka and Docker Compose, a taxonomy of six epochs of AI evolution, a zoo of future reentry architectures (RAS, diffusion attractors, fractal loops), gauge-invariant networks for safe swarms, fault-tolerance and recovery protocols, and eight falsifiable predictions. All formal proofs are machine-verified in Lean 4. This architecture is deployable today and represents a topologically protected, safe-by-design approach to AGI.

### [129] [Physics-guided Convolutional Neural Network for Domain Growth Prediction in Systems with Conserved Kinetics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26128)
*Vijay Yadav,Madhu Priya,Manish Dev Shrimali,Prabhat K. Jaiswal*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于注意力机制（attention mechanism）的物理引导卷积神经网络（convolutional neural network, CNN），作为代理模型来学习非线性PDEs控制的微结构演化。模型接受初始条件输入，直接预测二元混合物相分离在整个时间域上的演化过程。

Result: 模型在临界（critical）和非临界（off-critical）混合物条件下均能实现长期稳定且准确的预测；在整个演化过程中保持了混合物的成分守恒；准确捕捉了畴尺寸（domain size）的增长，并与Lifshitz-Slyozov畴生长定律（Lifshitz-Slyozov domain-growth law）一致。

Conclusion: 该框架在建模具有守恒动力学（conserved kinetics）的系统上表现有效，并具备扩展到其他复杂动力学系统的潜力。

Abstract: The spatiotemporal evolution of many physical, chemical, and biological systems is described by nonlinear partial differential equations (PDEs). Recently, deep neural network-based surrogate models have gained increasing interest as efficient alternatives to computationally expensive traditional numerical solvers. In this work, we propose an attention-based, physics-guided convolutional neural network as a surrogate model to learn the microstructural evolution of such systems. We train the model to accurately predict the full time-evolution of phase separation in binary mixtures governed by the Cahn-Hilliard equation. We show that predictions from our trained surrogate model remain stable and accurate over long-time rollouts for both critical and off-critical mixtures and preserve the mixture composition throughout evolution. We also show that our model accurately captures the growth of domain size and is consistent with the Lifshitz-Slyozov domain-growth law. The prediction results demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework for modeling systems with conserved kinetics and can be extended to other complex dynamical systems.

### [130] [Odd Diffusion in Three-Dimensional Isotropic Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26238)
*Viola Zixin Zhao,Andres Franco Valiente,David T. Limmer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文证明，在三维各向同性多组分体系中，通过非线性本构关系可以实现奇扩散（odd diffusion），这一效应源于密度梯度展开的二级项，并由非互易三体力（nonreciprocal three-body forces）的微观模型通过Dean–Kawasaki粗粒化（coarse-graining）程序导出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有奇扩散理论依赖仅存在于二维空间的线性反对称输运系数（antisymmetric transport coefficient），因此提出疑问：三维各向同性体系中是否可能存在奇扩散。

Method: 通过对称性分析（symmetry considerations）确定三维Levi-Civita张量允许在密度梯度展开（density gradient expansion）的二级项中出现各向同性奇流（isotropic odd current），并利用Dean–Kawasaki粗粒化程序从非互易三体力（nonreciprocal three-body forces）的微观粒子模型导出该本构律（constitutive law）。

Result: 三维奇扩散仅在多组分系统中出现，产生的输运效应包括边界驱动旋转流（boundary-driven rotational currents）、有限涡量（finite vorticity）和拟涡能（enstrophy），且无需外力矩（external torques）或偏好方向（preferred directions）。

Conclusion: 上述结果建立了三维各向同性体系中奇输运（odd transport）的最小框架，拓展了手性活性物质（chiral active matter）的理论范围。

Abstract: Odd diffusion is a hallmark of chiral active matter, generating currents transverse to density gradients. Existing theories rely on a linear antisymmetric transport coefficient that exists only in two dimensions, raising the question of whether odd diffusion can occur in isotropic three-dimensional systems. Here we show that such transport is possible through a nonlinear constitutive law. Symmetry considerations reveal that the three-dimensional Levi-Civita tensor permits a leading order isotropic odd current at second order in the density gradient expansion and only in multicomponent systems. The resulting transport generates boundary-driven rotational currents, finite vorticity, and enstrophy despite the absence of external torques or preferred directions. We show how such a constitutive law derives from a microscopic model of particles interacting through nonreciprocal three-body forces using the Dean--Kawasaki coarse-graining procedure. These results establish a minimal framework for odd transport in isotropic three dimensions.

</details>


### [131] [Frustrated shapes of solid domains in fluid membrane vesicles: From rolls and folds to crumples and wrinkles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26433)
*Geunwoong Jeon,Anthony N. A. Prempeh,Maria M. Santore,Gregory M. Grason*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的研究主要关注多流体域囊泡，而包含二维固体域的流体-固体复合囊泡（fluid-solid composite vesicles）因膜球面闭合与二维固体弹性之间的几何阻碍（geometric frustration）展现出复杂形态，其背后的力学机制尚不清晰，亟需系统研究。

Method: 采用离散有限元方法（Surface Evolver模拟），对含有单个柔性圆形固体域的闭合囊泡膜进行数值模拟，分析其弹性能量分布与形状平衡，并提取控制形状选择的关键物理与力学参数。

Result: 二维固体（剪切）弹性对低膨胀形态影响很小；固体对高斯曲率（Gaussian curvature）的几何非线性阻力在高膨胀囊泡中显著影响形状与弹性模式，且效应随囊泡尺寸与固体弹性厚度之比增大而增强。随膨胀增大，地面态形状呈现从圆柱卷曲（cylindrical rolls）、等距折叠（isometric folds）到复杂褶皱（crumples and wrinkles）直至光滑帽盖（smooth caps）的序列；高膨胀下非等距模式受膜张力的两个基本力学尺度支配。预测的高各向异性形状平衡与相分离DPPC/DOPC巨型单层囊泡（giant unilamellar vesicles）的实验观测高度吻合。

Conclusion: 流体-固体复合囊泡的膨胀形态由膜张力的两个基本力学尺度控制，其高膨胀非等距模式与弯曲液面上微观薄片中的远阈值力学（far-from-threshold mechanics）一致，为理解此类复合囊泡的形态选择提供了统一的力学框架。

Abstract: Fluid-solid composite vesicles, comprising 2D solid domains integrated into a topologically-closed fluid bilayer membrane, exhibit complex morphologies arising from the geometric frustration between spherical closure of the membrane and 2D solid elasticity. This scenario is distinct from the better studied case of multi-fluid domain vesicles. Here, we study the elastic energies and shape equilibria of a closed vesicle membrane containing a single, flexible circular solid domain using discrete finite-element (Surface Evolver) simulations, determining the key physical and mechanical parameters to govern shape selection. While we find that the 2D solid (shear) elasticity has minimal impact on the highly-under inflated morphologies, the geometrically non-linear resistance of the solid to Gaussian curvature substantially impacts the shape and elastic patterns form for inflated vesicles, by an amount that it grows with ratio of vesicle size to the elastic thickness of solid. For sufficiently large (thin) vesicles we characterize a generic sequence of ground state patterns of solid shape with increasing inflation: from cylindrical rolls and isometric folds to spatially complex patterns of crumples and wrinkles and ultimately to smooth caps. This sequence of non-isometric patterns at high-inflation is shown to be governed by the same far-from-threshold mechanics used to describe similar shape transitions in microscopic sheets on curved liquid interfaces, establishing that inflated shapes are governed by two basic mechanical scales of membrane tension. We find our predictions for highly-anisotropic shape equilibria of fluid-solid composite vesicles closely match experimentally observed shapes of giant unilamellar vesicles of phase-separated DPPC and DOPC.

</details>


### [132] [Dynamic heterogeneity in sodium silicate melts via machine-learning potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26646)
*Kumpei Shiraishi,Rikuta Nozawa,Emi Minamitani*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究利用机器学习势（machine-learning potentials）的分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，系统刻画了硅酸钠熔体中的动态异质性（dynamic heterogeneity）。研究发现钠离子通过离散跳跃（hopping）机制输运，与硅酸盐基质的慢弛豫解耦，并揭示氧原子的非高斯行为最为显著，反映了骨架原子稀有随机重排的间歇性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对真实多组分氧化物玻璃中空间迁移率差异（spatial mobility disparities）的微观机制理解尚不充分，尤其缺乏在纳秒时间尺度上对动态异质性的系统表征。

Method: 采用机器学习势（machine-learning potentials）的分子动力学模拟，对二硅酸钠、四硅酸钠和六硅酸钠熔体在不同温度下计算均方位移（mean squared displacement）和时间关联函数（time-correlation function），并分析范霍夫函数（van Hove function）的自部分及非高斯参数（non-Gaussian parameter）。

Result: 钠离子的范霍夫函数自部分呈现双峰性（bimodality），表明碱金属输运由离散跳跃事件介导；钠离子与硅酸盐基质的慢弛豫解耦；所有物种均表现出动态异质性，但氧原子的非高斯行为最为显著。

Conclusion: 研究阐明了硅酸盐熔体中离子输运的微观机制及其与动态异质性的联系，为在真实玻璃材料中研究基础玻璃态物理（glassy physics）提供了新途径。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive characterisation of dynamic heterogeneity in sodium silicate melts using molecular dynamics simulation with machine-learning potentials. By studying sodium disilicate, tetrasilicate, and hexasilicate melts across a range of temperatures, mean squared displacement and a time-correlation function computed up to the nanosecond timescale provide a detailed account of how spatial mobility disparities emerge in a realistic multicomponent oxide glass. Within these timescales, the self-part of the van Hove function for sodium displays a bimodality, demonstrating that alkali transport is mediated by discrete displacement events consistent with a hopping mechanism. This distinct hopping allows sodium ions to decouple from the sluggish relaxation of the silicate matrix. Furthermore, evaluation of the non-Gaussian parameter reveals that, although all constituent species exhibit dynamic heterogeneity, the non-Gaussian behaviour is most pronounced for oxygen atoms. This trend reflects the intermittency of structural rearrangements, where framework atoms undergo rare and stochastic events compared to the frequent displacements of mobile ions. Our findings elucidate the microscopic mechanism of ion transport and its connection to dynamic heterogeneity in silicate melts, offering a new avenue to study fundamental glassy physics in realistic vitreous materials.

### [133] [Solid adsorption: the missing mechanism for surfactant contact lines -- a phase-field approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26655)
*Parvathy K. Kannan,Kazi T. Iqbal,Diego Díaz,Ilse Mateman,Shahab Mirjalili,Gustav Amberg,Shervin Bagheri,Outi Tammisola*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于热力学第二定律（second law of thermodynamics）的变分原理（variational principles）推导热力学自洽的相场模型（phase-field model），将界面吸附与固体表面吸附纳入自由能泛函与边界条件中，从而在连续框架内统一描述表面活性剂的输运、吸附及润湿动力学（wetting dynamics）。

Result: 新模型在定性上与实验观测一致：在包含固体壁面吸附后，表面活性剂使所有接触角均向亲水性方向偏移，而此前未考虑固体吸附的数值研究仅能预测亲水表面更亲水、疏水表面更疏水。

Conclusion: 固体壁面上的吸附效应是预测含表面活性剂的接触线动力学所必需的关键机制；本文模型填补了这一缺失环节，为后续定量预测提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We develop a thermodynamically consistent phase-field model for soluble surfactants in two-phase flows, incorporating both interfacial and solid surface adsorption. The model is derived via variational principles consistent with the second law of thermodynamics, resulting in modified free energies and boundary conditions that capture surfactant transport, adsorption, and wetting dynamics. A key contribution of this work is the inclusion of surfactant adsorption on solid walls, which leads to qualitative agreement with experimental observations: unlike prior numerical studies that predicted hydrophilic surfaces becoming more hydrophilic and hydrophobic surfaces more hydrophobic, our model shows a shift toward increased hydrophilicity across all contact angles-consistent with experimental trends. Our results establish that solid adsorption provides the missing mechanism required for predictive modelling of surfactant-laden contact line dynamics.

### [134] [Analysing gelation transition through fractional viscoelasticity and Mittag-Leffler-Prabhakar function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26656)
*Yogesh M Joshi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过分数阶微积分（fractional calculus）和三项Mittag-Leffler-Prabhakar函数，构建了物理约束的分数阶粘弹性模型，统一描述了凝胶化转变（gelation transition）前后两个阶段的标度行为，并在临界凝胶点（critical gel point）处施加动态模量及其导数的连续性，从而将超标度关系（hyper-scaling relation）确立为理论必然性。模型经实验数据验证，并识别出由两个临界指数（critical exponents）唯一确定的临界凝胶态流变指纹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 凝胶化转变（gelation transition）在胶体到聚合物等多种体系中普遍存在，其临界凝胶态（critical gel state）表现为无标度幂律粘弹性（scale-free power-law viscoelasticity）。分数阶微积分（fractional calculus）天然适合描述这种幂律行为，但现有模型在物理约束、跨临界点连续性和参数适用范围等方面存在不足，亟需构建更完备的理论框架。

Method: 基于物理约束建立分数阶粘弹性模型（fractional viscoelastic models）和基于三项Mittag-Leffler-Prabhakar函数的模型，分别用于凝胶前态（pre-gel state）和凝胶后态（post-gel regime），确保与各区域传统标度关系（scaling relations）的一致性。在临界凝胶点处强制动态模量（dynamic moduli）及其导数连续，并利用时域和频域实验数据进行模型验证。

Result: 分数阶预凝胶模型仅在有限参数子集内有效，而基于Prabhakar函数的模型消除了这一限制。临界凝胶点处的连续性条件普遍施加了临界凝胶态两侧弛豫动力学（relaxation dynamics）的对称性，并将超标度关系（hyper-scaling relation）从经验巧合提升为理论必然。实验验证了模型的有效性，并识别出一种与模型无关、仅由两个临界指数确定的频率无关临界凝胶态流变指纹。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于Prabhakar函数的粘弹性模型能够统一描述凝胶化转变全过程，克服了传统分数阶模型的参数局限性。临界凝胶点处的连续性条件是对超标度关系的理论确证，揭示了凝胶化转变中内在的对称性结构。

Abstract: The gelation transition, a process that transforms a flowable liquid into an elastic solid, is a present in variety of systems, from colloidal to polymeric. During the gelation transition, a system passes through a critical gel state characterized by scale-free power-law viscoelasticity. Interestingly, the fractional calculus provides a natural mathematical language for such power-law viscoelasticity. In this work, we develop physically constrained fractional viscoelastic models as well as those based on the three-parameter Mittag-Leffler-Prabhakar function for both, the pre-gel state and the post-gel regimes, ensuring consistency with the conventional scaling relations in each regime. While the fractional pre-gel model is observed to be valid only for a restricted subset of parameter values, the Prabhakar function-based model rigorously removes this limitation. We enforce continuity of the dynamic moduli and their derivatives across the critical gel point, which universally imposes a symmetry in the relaxation dynamics on either side of the critical gel state. Such enforcement further validates the hyper-scaling relation connecting the critical exponents, making it a theoretical necessity rather than an empirical coincidence. We validate the proposed models against time- and frequency-domain experimental data. A model-agnostic, frequency-independent rheological fingerprint of the critical gel state, uniquely determined by two critical exponents, is also identified.

### [135] [Solid-to-solid transition in dense assemblies of elongated cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26726)
*Shao-Zhen Lin,Jean-François Rupprecht*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过在标准顶点模型（vertex model）中引入内在各向异性弹性偏好，发现细胞伸长不会导致组织流化（fluidization），而是驱动一种从有序各向同性固体到无序各向异性固体的固-固转变，从而将细胞形态与组织流变学（rheology）解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在汇合组织中，细胞形状从近乎各向同性的上皮形态到高度拉长的内皮形态不等。标准顶点模型中，组织刚性由目标形状指数（target shape index）控制，增加该指数会驱动细胞伸长并最终导致组织流化。本文旨在探究当细胞伸长是源于内在的被动弹性各向异性偏好时，其对组织力学行为的影响。

Method: 在标准顶点模型基础上，为每个细胞分配一个内在的、被动的弹性各向异性偏好，使得细胞伸长能够自主出现，而非由外部目标形状指数驱动。

Result: 细胞伸长并不使组织流化，而是驱动一种从有序各向同性固体到无序各向异性固体的固-固转变（solid-to-solid transition）。转变两侧的组织均具有有限的屈服应力（yield stress）和剪切刚性（shear rigidity）。

Conclusion: 细胞形态与组织流变学是解耦的，不应仅依据拉长的细胞形态推断组织具有流体般的力学行为（fluid-like mechanics）。

Abstract: Cell shapes in confluent tissues range from nearly isotropic epithelial morphologies to highly elongated endothelial ones. In standard vertex models, tissue rigidity is controlled by a target shape index; increasing this index drives cell elongation and ultimate tissue fluidization. Here, we consider the case where cell elongation emerges autonomously by assigning an intrinsic, passive elastic preference for anisotropic shape. This distinction reverses the usual expectation: cell elongation does not fluidize the tissue, but drives a solid-to-solid transition from an ordered isotropic solid to a disordered anisotropic solid, with finite yield stress and shear rigidity on either side of the transition. These results decouple cell shape from tissue rheology and caution against inferring fluid-like mechanics from elongated cell morphologies alone.

### [136] [Unraveling Internal Friction in a Coarse-Grained Protein Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27133)
*Carlos Monago,J. A. de la Torre,Rafael Delgado-Buscalioni,Pep Español*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本篇论文通过粗粒化（coarse-graining, CG）模型研究球状蛋白在水中的动力学行为，指出除溶剂引起的流体动力学耦合和弹性耦合外，还必须引入珠子间的内摩擦（internal friction）以准确再现蛋白质动力学，并提出了基于自平均方法（self-averaging method）的参数优化方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂生物分子动力学行为的理解需要简化模型，现有粗粒化模型中的耗散珠子相互作用仅限于溶剂引起的水动力学耦合；然而，摩擦不仅来源于溶剂，还源于被粗粒化过程忽略的内部自由度，这种“内摩擦”对动力学准确性的影响尚待研究。

Method: 论文采用Mori-Zwanzig形式（Mori-Zwanzig formalism）导出粗粒化珠子的随机动力学；通过比较全原子分子动力学（all-atom molecular dynamics, MD）模拟结果，验证内摩擦的必要性；并提出基于自平均方法（self-averaging method）的参数优化方案，将CG动力学与参数演化方程相结合，使选定观测量（如径向分布函数和珠子速度时间关联）与MD值匹配。

Result: 结果表明，要准确再现球状蛋白在水中的动力学行为，精确确定弹性耦合和每个珠子的Stokesian自摩擦（Stokesian self-friction）仅是必要条件；关键地，珠子之间的内摩擦（internal friction）同样不可或缺。

Conclusion: 内摩擦是粗粒化模型中准确表征蛋白质动力学的关键要素，所提出的自平均参数优化方法能够有效整合这一因素，使得CG模型在选定观测量上与全原子分子动力学结果一致。

Abstract: Understanding the dynamic behavior of complex biomolecules requires simplified models that not only make computations feasible but also reveal fundamental mechanisms. Coarse-graining (CG) achieves this by grouping atoms into beads, whose stochastic dynamics can be derived using the Mori-Zwanzig formalism, capturing both reversible and irreversible interactions. In liquid, the dissipative bead-bead interactions have so far been restricted to hydrodynamic couplings. However, friction does not only arises from the solvent but notably, from the internal degrees of freedom missing in the CG beads. This leads to an additional ''internal friction'' whose relevance is studied in this contribution. By comparing with all-atom molecular dynamics (MD), we neatly show that in order to accurately reproduce the dynamics of a globular protein in water using a coarse-grained (CG) model, not only a precise determination of elastic couplings and the Stokesian self-friction of each bead is required. Critically, the inclusion of internal friction between beads is also necessary for a faithful representation of protein dynamics. We propose to optimize the parameters of the CG model through a self-averaging method that integrates the CG dynamics with an evolution equation for the CG parameters. This approach ensures that selected quantities, such as the radial distribution function and the time correlation of bead velocities, match the corresponding MD values.

</details>


### [137] [Organic Semiconductor Alignment via Confinement in Vapor-Guided Droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27207)
*Robert Malinowski,Alessandro Rossi,Lewis M. Cowen,Peter A. Gilhooly-Finn,Michael A. Parkes,Ming-Hao Chang,Yu-Cheng Chiu,Ioannis Papakonstantinou,Matthew O. Blunt,Bob C. Schroeder,Giorgio Volpe*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用微升级别蒸汽引导液滴在外部蒸汽源驱动下运动，液滴内部因体积受限而产生定向流动，该流动在沉积前即可实现有机半导体纳米线（nanowires）的取向排列，从而形成具有高度方向性有序（directional order）的薄膜。

Result: 基于该方法制备的有机场效应晶体管在饱和电流（saturation current）方面比旋涂（spin-coated）对照组提升了约40%。此外，该方法具备非接触（contactless）、紧凑（compact）的特点，可在曲面和柔性基底上实现沉积与取向排列。

Conclusion: 蒸汽引导液滴为功能软材料（functional soft materials）的受限诱导取向排列（confinement-induced alignment）提供了一种可扩展的框架，有望集成到现有增材制造（additive manufacturing）平台中，用于柔性电子及其他领域的应用。

Abstract: Organic semiconductors are lightweight, solution-processable materials with strong potential for printed and flexible electronics, from deformable displays to wearable sensors. Despite significant advances in materials synthesis and manufacturing, controlling molecular and mesoscale alignment during deposition remains a central challenge, as film morphology critically governs charge transport and device performance. Here, we demonstrate that flows developing within the intrinsically confined volume of microliter vapor-guided droplets can be harnessed to produce highly aligned organic semiconductor films. As droplets move in response to an external vapor source, internal flows align organic semiconducting nanowires within the droplet prior to deposition, yielding films with pronounced directional order. Organic field-effect transistors fabricated with this approach exhibit approximately 40% enhancement in saturation current relative to spin-coated controls. Beyond improved device performance, the contactless and compact nature of our method enables the deposition and alignment of organic semiconductors on curved and flexible surfaces. More broadly, vapor-guided droplets offer a scalable framework for the confinement-induced alignment of functional soft materials, with potential for integration into existing additive manufacturing platforms for flexible electronics and beyond.

### [138] [Light-driven active phase separation and droplet division](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27220)
*Zi Lin,Thomas Beneyton,Suzanne Lafon,Edison Rafael Jimenez Granda,Liangfei Tian,Alexandre Baron,Jean-Christophe Baret,Nicolas Martin*

TL;DR: 本文通过光响应DNA-偶氮苯凝聚液滴实验证明，仅依靠持续的分子开关（molecular switching）即可在无化学燃料或生化调控下产生非平衡相分离行为，包括粗化抑制、表面不稳定性和分裂等现象，揭示了反应通量施加方式对主动相行为（active phase behavior）的调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相分离（phase separation）普遍存在于物质自组织过程中，但在持续能量输入下的非平衡相分离机制尚不清晰。现有实验方法多依赖化学燃料系统，反应通量与燃料消耗和反应网络复杂性耦合，难以厘清基本物理机制。该研究旨在探索更简化的驱动方式——仅通过连续的分子开关是否足以产生主动相行为。

Method: 研究者构建了光响应的DNA-偶氮苯（DNA-azobenzene）凝聚液滴系统，将其限制在微流控液滴（microfluidic droplets）中。通过光照实现空间和时间上精确的分子间相互作用调控，定量追踪相分离动力学（phase separation dynamics）。光驱动的偶氮苯异构化（azobenzene isomerization）同时控制热力学和动力学参数，设置相边界（phase boundaries）并调控溶解和成核速率。

Result: 在单波长光照下，顺反异构化耦合为动态光稳态（photostationary state），粗化（coarsening）被抑制，微米级凝聚液滴得以稳定存在。当两个光异构化路径独立驱动时，空间上不平衡的反应通量产生持续的界面不稳定性（interfacial instabilities），包括表面波动、出芽和分裂。这些行为不依赖化学燃料或生化调控。

Conclusion: 非平衡相行为（non-equilibrium phase behavior）由反应通量的施加方式主导。可逆分子开关（reversible molecular switching）为从平衡结构单元构建主动材料（active materials）提供了一条最小化路径。

Abstract: Phase separation organizes matter across scales, yet how it operates under sustained energy input remains poorly understood. Experimental approaches to driven phase separation have largely relied on chemically fueled systems, in which reaction fluxes are intrinsically coupled to fuel consumption and reaction-network complexity. Here we show that continuous molecular switching alone is sufficient to generate active phase behavior in a minimal two-phase system. Using light-responsive DNA-azobenzene coacervates confined in microfluidic droplets, we modulate intermolecular interactions with spatiotemporal precision and quantitatively track phase separation dynamics under illumination. Light-driven azobenzene isomerization controls both thermodynamics and kinetics, setting phase boundaries and regulating dissolution and nucleation rates. Under single-wavelength illumination that couples forward and backward isomerization into a dynamic photostationary state, coarsening is arrested and micron-sized coacervates are stabilized. When the two photoisomerization pathways are driven independently, spatially unbalanced reaction fluxes generate sustained interfacial instabilities, including surface undulations, budding, and division. These behaviors arise from a physical coupling between reaction kinetics and phase separation, without chemical fuels or biochemical regulation. Our results show that non-equilibrium phase behavior is governed by how opposing reaction fluxes are imposed, establishing reversible molecular switching as a minimal route to active materials from equilibrium building blocks.

</details>


### [139] [Weak-Flow Induced Dielectric Axes Rotation in Dipolar Suspensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27296)
*Pramodt Srinivasula*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过弱流下可定向布朗偶极子的扰动福克-普朗克方程的渐近解，预测了流动可诱发偏离对角线的介电张量分量（off-diagonal permittivity components），该分量与相对流动强度呈线性关系，并导致主介电轴旋转。这揭示了此前未被认识的流变介电响应，并提出流动控制介电与电-光功能的新可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统流变介电研究（rheodielectric studies）主要关注流动引起的介电主分量变化，而忽略了流动可能诱发偏离对角线分量的可能性。本文旨在理论预测并揭示这一未被认识的流变介电效应，从而为流动控制的介电和电-光功能提供新思路。

Method: 对可定向布朗偶极子（orientable Brownian dipoles）在弱流下的扰动福克-普朗克方程（perturbed Fokker-Planck equation）进行渐近求解（asymptotic solution），分析流动诱发的介电张量分量变化。

Result: 预测了在弱流下出现与相对流动强度呈线性关系的偏离对角线介电张量分量；在平面剪切流（planar shear flow）中，这些项超过相应的高阶对角线修正，并导致主介电轴（principal dielectric axes）发生旋转。

Conclusion: 发现了一种此前未被认识的流变介电响应（rheodielectric response），暗示了通过流动控制介电和电-光功能（flow-controlled dielectric and electro-optical functionalities）的新可能性。

Abstract: Conventional rheodielectric studies of dipolar suspensions primarily examine flow-induced variations in the principal permittivity components. In contrast, an asymptotic solution of the perturbed Fokker--Planck equation for orientable Brownian dipoles under weak flow predicts the emergence of off-diagonal permittivity components that are linear in the relative flow strength. For planar shear flow, these terms exceed the corresponding higher-order diagonal corrections, leading to a rotation of the principal dielectric axes. This previously unrecognized rheodielectric response suggests new possibilities for flow-controlled dielectric and electro-optical functionalities.

</details>

### [140] [Anomalously long-delayed afterpulses in large-area photomultipliers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24574)
*Nikita Ushakov,Bayarto Lubsandorzhiev,Arslan Lukanov,Andrei Sidorenkov,Dmitrii Voronin*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文报告了Baksan大型中微子望远镜项目中四种型号光电倍增管（PMT）中观测到的异常长延迟后脉冲现象，其平均延迟时间在73 μs至260 μs之间，概率不超过每光电子0.1%，且振幅严格限制在单光电子水平，与主脉冲振幅和PMT工作电压无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大型中微子探测实验中，光电倍增管（photomultiplier, PMT）的后脉冲（afterpulse）特性会直接影响信号甄别和本底抑制能力，特别是长延迟后脉冲可能对低能量事件的测量造成干扰。因此，系统表征不同型号PMT的异常延迟后脉冲行为对实验设计具有重要意义。

Method: 研究针对滨松光子（Hamamatsu Photonics）生产的R7081-100（10英寸）、R5912-100（8英寸）、R12860（20英寸）以及NNVT生产的N6205（20英寸）共四种型号的光电倍增管，通过测量主脉冲与后脉冲之间的时间间隔、出现概率和振幅分布，分析了后脉冲的延迟特性及其对工作电压的依赖性。

Result: 四种PMT的平均后脉冲延迟时间分别约为85 μs（R7081-100）、73 μs（R5912-100）、260 μs（R12860）和90 μs（N6205）；后脉冲概率不超过每光电子（photoelectron）0.1%；所有后脉冲的振幅均严格限制在单光电子水平，与主脉冲振幅无关；后脉冲延迟时间对PMT工作电压无明显依赖。

Conclusion: 四种PMT均存在异常长的延迟后脉冲现象，其特征（延迟时间、概率、振幅限制及电压无关性）表明该效应可能源于PMT内部某种与打拿极（dynode）或残余气体相关的共同物理机制，需要在未来的中微子实验数据分析中予以关注和扣除。

Abstract: We report the observation of anomalously long-delayed afterpulses in photomultipliers of the Baksan Large Neutrino Telescope project$~-$ 10-inch R7081-100, 8-inch R5912-100, 20-inch R12860 photomultipliers produced by Hamamatsu Photonics, and 20-inch N6205 photomultipliers produced by NNVT. The mean delay times relative to the main pulses are approximately $85~μ$s, $73~μ$s, $260~μ$s, and $90~μ$s, respectively. The probability of such afterpulses does not exceed 0.1% per photoelectron, and their amplitudes are strictly confined to the single-photoelectron level, regardless of the amplitude of the main pulse. The delay time of these afterpulses shows no significant dependence on the PMT operating voltage.

</details>

Valdiviesso,R. G. Van de Water,A. Vázquez-Ramos,L. Wan,M. Weber,H. Wei,T. Wester,A. White,A. Wilkinson,P. Wilson,T. Wongjirad,E. Worcester,M. Worcester,S. Yadav,E. Yandel,T. Yang,L. Yates,S. Yebes,B. Yu,H. Yu,J. Yu,B. Zamorano,J. Zennamo,C. Zhang*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文报道了为短基线近点探测器（SBND）设计、制造并安装的一套波长位移反射系统。该系统在FR4基板上层叠镜面反射膜并采用物理气相沉积涂覆四苯基丁二烯（TPB）波长位移剂，共制备64块双面板，旨在增加并均匀化液氩时间投影室中的闪烁光收集。安装后早期测量显示光收集均匀性和响应良好，有助于改进触发、量能测量和位置重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 液氩时间投影室（liquid argon time projection chamber, LArTPC）中闪烁光（scintillation light）的收集效率和均匀性对探测器性能至关重要。SBND需要一种能提升并均匀化光收集的系统，以支持低能物理事件的触发、量能测量（calorimetry）和位置重建（position reconstruction）。

Method: 采用FR4为基板制造64块双面板，层压镜面反射膜（specular reflector film），并通过受控物理气相沉积（physical vapor deposition, PVD）在表面涂覆300 μg/cm²的四苯基丁二烯（tetraphenyl butadiene, TPB）作为波长位移剂（wavelength shifter）。涂覆均匀性经由沉积质量测量和轮廓法（profilometry）验证。组装时在导电网格（conductive meshes）之间安装板件以确保高压兼容性。

Result: 该系统成为中微子探测器（neutrino detector）中TPB涂覆面积最大的装置。早期光收集测量显示整个探测器范围具有高均匀性（high uniformity）和优良的光响应（light response）。

Conclusion: 该波长位移反射系统成功提升了SBND的闪烁光收集效率与均匀性，有助于改进触发（triggering）、量能测量和位置重建性能。文中同时指出，TPB材料对蓝光/紫外光（blue/UV light）敏感，因此在操作和安装过程中需采取保护性滤光和受控存储条件。

Abstract: We report on the design, production, and installation of a wavelength-shifting reflective system on the cathode of the Short-Baseline Near Detector (SBND), a liquid argon time projection chamber located along the Fermilab Booster Neutrino Beam. To increase and homogenize scintillation-light collection, 64 double-sided plates were fabricated from FR4, laminated with specular reflector film and coated with 300 $μ$g/cm$^2$ of tetraphenyl butadiene (TPB) wavelength shifter using controlled physical vapor deposition. The coating uniformity was validated through dedicated measurements of deposited mass and profilometry studies. Because exposure to ambient blue/UV light could degrade the TPB, protective filtering and controlled storage conditions were implemented during handling and installation. The coated plates were assembled between conductive meshes for high-voltage compatibility and installed in situ during detector integration. This system constitutes the largest TPB-coated area deployed in a neutrino detector. It operates in conjunction with SBND's photon detection system, which consists of photomultiplier tubes and X-ARAPUCAs. Early light-collection measurements show high uniformity and light response across the detector, supporting improved triggering, calorimetry, and position reconstruction in SBND.

### [142] [HERETIX: A Hermetic, Enriched, Rare-Event Time Projection Chamber in Xenon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26876)
*L. Althueser,N. Hargittai,J. Pienaar,R. Braun,H. Landsman,C. Weinheimer,R. Budnik*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出 HERETIX，一种多吨级液氙（liquid xenon）天文台，通过嵌套两个时间投影室（time projection chambers）同时优化对弱相互作用大质量粒子（WIMP）暗物质和无中微子双β衰变（$0νββ$）的搜索，蒙特卡洛研究显示其$0νββ$半衰期灵敏度可达 $3.2 \times 10^{28}$ 年（90% 置信水平，10 年曝光），同时保持出色的暗物质探测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于氙的时间投影室已成为稀有事件搜索中最强大的技术之一；该工作旨在设计一个统一的实验方案，能够同时以领先灵敏度回答两大基本物理问题——暗物质（weakly interacting massive particles, WIMPs）和无中微子双β衰变（neutrinoless double beta decay, $0νββ$）。

Method: HERETIX 采用两个嵌套的时间投影室（time projection chambers）：内探测器为一个密封蓝宝石容器，装载富集至 90% $^{136}$Xe 的氙气，提供超低本底环境用于 $0νββ$ 搜索；外探测器为贫 $^{136}$Xe 的氙气体积，用于保持暗物质探测性能。通过蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟评估材料本底的消除效果。

Result: 蒙特卡洛研究表明，材料诱导本底可被有效消除；在 10 年曝光后，HERETIX 在 90% 置信水平下的 $0νββ$ 半衰期灵敏度投影为 $3.2 \times 10^{28} \, \mathrm{years}$。

Conclusion: HERETIX 提供了一种统一的实验途径，能够同时以领先灵敏度探索两大基本物理问题——暗物质和无中微子双β衰变。

Abstract: Xenon-based time projection chambers have established themselves as one of the most powerful technologies for rare-event searches. HERETIX is a proposed multi-tonne liquid xenon observatory featuring two nested time projection chambers that enable the simultaneous optimisation of searches for weakly interacting massive particles and neutrinoless double beta decay ($0νββ$) of $^{136}$Xe. A hermetically sealed sapphire vessel containing xenon enriched to 90% $^{136}$Xe forms the inner detector, providing an ultra-low-background environment for $0νββ$ searches. Monte Carlo studies indicate that material-induced backgrounds can be effectively eliminated, yielding a projected $0νββ$ half-life sensitivity of $3.2 \times 10^{28} \, \mathrm{years}$ at 90% confidence level after a 10-year exposure, while the surrounding xenon volume, depleted in $^{136}$Xe, preserves the excellent dark matter sensitivity of large liquid xenon detectors. HERETIX therefore offers a unified experimental approach capable of delivering leading sensitivity to two of the most compelling questions in fundamental physics.

### [143] [Sharp endpoint multilinear estimates for oscillatory integrals and spectral clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26550)
*Shengwen Gan,Cheng Zhang,Zhifei Zhu*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了对于具有任意分离频率尺度的 Carleson–Sjölin 振荡积分算子，在所有 k≥2 和 1≤p≤∞ 下成立尖锐的 k-线性 L^p 估计，包括端点对数行为；并因此解决了 Burq–Gérard–Tzvetkov 关于三维黎曼流形上双线性谱簇估计的问题，进而建立了尖锐的 k-线性 L^p 谱簇估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究 Carleson–Sjölin 振荡积分算子（oscillatory integral operator）的 k-线性 L^p 估计，并解决 Burq–Gérard–Tzvetkov 提出的关于三维闭黎曼流形（closed three-dimensional Riemannian manifold）上双线性谱簇估计（bilinear spectral cluster estimate）的公开问题。

Method: 通过分析具有任意分离频率尺度的 Carleson–Sjölin 型相位函数，证明 k-线性 L^p 估计的尖锐性，包括端点对数行为（endpoint logarithmic behavior）。

Result: 对所有 k≥2 和 1≤p≤∞，得到了尖锐的 k-线性 L^p 估计，并获得了任意三维闭黎曼流形上的无对数端点双线性谱簇估计；作为推论，建立了所有 k≥2 和 1≤p≤∞ 下尖锐的 k-线性 L^p 谱簇估计（spectral cluster estimate）。

Conclusion: 所获估计具有最优性，包括一般 Carleson–Sjölin 相位下的端点对数行为，同时完全解决了 Burq–Gérard–Tzvetkov 的问题。

Abstract: We prove sharp $k$-linear $L^p$ estimates for Carleson--Sjölin oscillatory integral operators with arbitrary separated frequency scales for all $k\ge 2$ and $1\le p\le \infty$. The estimates are sharp, including the endpoint logarithmic behavior for general Carleson--Sjölin phases. Moreover, we obtain log-free endpoint bilinear spectral cluster estimates on every closed three-dimensional Riemannian manifold, resolving a problem of Burq--Gérard--Tzvetkov. As a consequence, we establish sharp $k$-linear $L^p$ spectral cluster estimates for all $k\ge 2$ and $1\le p\le \infty$.

</details>


### [144] [Determining potentials from the scattering map of the time-dependent Schrödinger equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26581)
*Qiuye Jia*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明，在特定度量空间下，两个薛定谔算子的散射映射（scattering map）和泊松算子（Poisson operator）在临界能级上相差一个紧算子（compact operator）当且仅当这两个势函数相等。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究弯曲空间上含时薛定谔方程（time dependent Schrödinger equation）的散射映射，即从$t\to-\infty$的渐近分布到$t\to+\infty$的渐近分布的映射。作者希望建立散射映射或泊松算子的差异与势函数差异之间的等价关系。

Method: 针对一类特定的度量（metrics），对比同一弯曲空间上两个薛定谔算子的散射映射和泊松算子，分析它们在临界能级（critical level）上的算子性质差异。

Result: 两个薛定谔算子的散射映射和泊松算子在临界能级上仅相差一个紧算子，当且仅当这两个势函数相等。

Conclusion: 散射映射和泊松算子在临界能级上的紧性差异可以唯一确定势函数，这意味着可以通过算子的紧性特征来反演势函数信息。

Abstract: For a time dependent Schrödinger equation, the scattering map is the map sending the asymptotic profile of a solution as $t \to-\infty$ to its asymptotic profile as $t\to+\infty$. In this paper we show that, for a certain class of metrics, the scattering maps and Poisson operators associated to two Schrödinger operators on the same curved space only differ by a compact operator on a critical level if and only if the two potentials are equal.

</details>


### [145] [Painlevé \uppercase\expandafter{\romannumeral34\relax} and collisionless shock in the defocusing NLS equation with step-like initial data in the transition regions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26911)
*Engui Fan,Zhaoyu Wang,Yidan Zhang*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文利用非线性最速下降法（nonlinear steepest descent method），基于黎曼-希尔伯特（Riemann-Hilbert）框架，研究了具有阶梯状初始数据的散焦非线性薛定谔（NLS）方程的柯西问题（Cauchy problem），给出了三个不同过渡区域中解的长时间渐近展开，其中前两个区域的主导阶渐近由Painlevé III型公式描述，第三个碰撞无激波区（collisionless shock region）则由黎曼theta函数（Riemann theta functions）描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有阶梯状初始数据（step-like initial data）的散焦非线性薛定谔（defocusing nonlinear Schrödinger, NLS）方程柯西问题（Cauchy problem）的长时间渐近行为，特别是在多个不同过渡区域中解的动力学结构。

Method: 采用非线性最速下降法（nonlinear steepest descent method），并基于与柯西问题相关联的黎曼-希尔伯特（Riemann-Hilbert）表述进行渐近分析。

Result: 在三个不同的过渡区域中导出了解的长时间渐近展开式：前两个区域的主导阶渐近由Painlevé III型（Painlevé \uppercase\expandafter{\romannumeral34\relax}-type）公式刻画；第三个区域为碰撞无激波区（collisionless shock region），主导阶渐近由黎曼theta函数（Riemann theta functions）描述。

Conclusion: 散焦NLS方程在阶梯状初始条件下的长时间渐近行为在不同过渡区域呈现不同的主导结构——Painlevé III型公式与黎曼theta函数分别刻画了不同区域的渐近形态。

Abstract: We consider the Cauchy problem for the defocusing nonlinear Schrödinger (NLS) equation with step-like initial data. Using the nonlinear steepest descent method, we derive the long-time asymptotic expansion of the solution to the Cauchy problem in three distinct transition regions. In the first two transition regions, the leading-order asymptotics are characterized by Painlevé \uppercase\expandafter{\romannumeral34\relax}-type formula, while in the third one is a collisionless shock region, the leading-order asymptotics is describedin terms of Riemann theta functions. Our analysis is based on the Riemann-Hilbert formulation associated with the Cauchy problem of the defocusing NLS equation.

</details>

### [146] [Large-$N$ Carrollian Thermodynamics from AdS Black-Hole Phase-Space Contractions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26163)
*Yingnan Xu,Shuangshuang Chu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发展了有限卡罗（Carrollian）黑洞热力学的边界与天球（celestial）解释。通过将扩展的AdS第一定律取有限Carrollian极限，揭示其全息对偶为双重缩放的低温-大N系综；构建了有限Carrollian Brown-York应力张量，导出了第一定律的边界形式，并将Hawking-Page相变点与自由度化学势的零点相联系；最后构造了热Carrollian关联函数的天球共形主表示（celestial conformal-primary representation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准AdS/CFT对偶中的黑洞热力学在Carrollian极限下会出现发散，现有框架无法直接描述有限物理量的全息解释。本文旨在发展一种有限Carrollian黑洞热力学框架，使其第一定律具有明确的边界全息对应，并建立从AdS边界到天球（celestial sphere）的热力学映射。

Method: 以AdS黑洞的相空间收缩（phase-space contraction）为输入，对时间生成元（time generator）和牛顿常数（Newton constant）取有限Carrollian极限，得到有限的第一定律形式。利用AdS₅/CFT₄的伴随自由度（adjoint degrees of freedom）归一化和AdS₃/CFT₂的Brown-Henneaux中心荷建立大N字典。构造有限Carrollian Brown-York应力张量，并通过对傅里叶-梅林变换（Fourier-Mellin transform）与缩放热频率窗口（rescaled thermal frequency window）的组合，构建天球基关联函数（celestial-basis correlators）。

Result: 第一定律具有双重缩放的全息解释：Carrollian温度降低的同时边界有效自由度数量增加，使得热力学乘积保持有限。全局能量荷（global energy charge）等同于有限体哈密顿量（finite bulk Hamiltonian）。Hawking-Page相变点对应于自由度化学势（chemical potential conjugate to the count of degrees of freedom）的零点。该能量荷同时也是全局Carrollian超平移荷（global Carrollian supertranslation charge），因此有限第一定律是Carrollian Ward恒等式（Carrollian Ward identity）的热零模扇区（thermal zero-mode sector）。

Conclusion: 有限Carrollian黑洞热力学在AdS边界上具有自洽的全息对偶，其核心是双重缩放的低温-大N系综。第一定律的边界形式揭示了Hawking-Page相变与自由度化学势之间的内在联系，且Carrollian超平移对称性为热力学提供了零模约束。天球基关联函数的构造为研究Carrollian全息学中的热量子场论提供了具体工具。

Abstract: We develop the boundary and celestial interpretation of finite Carrollian black-hole thermodynamics. The bulk input is the phase-space contraction of the time generator and Newton constant for which the extended AdS first law has a finite Carrollian limit. We show that this finite first-law line has a holographic interpretation as a double-scaled low-temperature, large-$N$ ensemble: the Carrollian temperature decreases while the effective number of boundary degrees of freedom grows, leaving the thermodynamic products in the first law finite. The large-$N$ dictionary is anchored by the standard $\mathrm{AdS}_5/\mathrm{CFT}_4$ normalization of adjoint degrees of freedom and by the Brown--Henneaux central charge in $\mathrm{AdS}_3/\mathrm{CFT}_2$. We construct the finite Carrollian Brown--York stress tensor on the contracted AdS boundary and show that its global energy charge is the finite bulk Hamiltonian. We then derive the boundary form of the first law in terms of the spatial volume and the holographic degree-of-freedom normalization. This identifies the Hawking--Page locus with the zero of the chemical potential conjugate to the count of degrees of freedom. The same charge is the global Carrollian supertranslation charge, so the finite first law is the thermal zero-mode sector of the Carrollian Ward identity. Finally, we construct the celestial conformal-primary representation of thermal Carrollian correlators. The finite celestial-basis correlators are rescaled double-scaled correlators obtained by combining the Fourier--Mellin transform with the rescaled thermal frequency window.

</details>


### [147] [De Sitter Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26221)
*Kurt Hinterbichler*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从物理学视角系统回顾了德西特空间（de Sitter space）等距代数 so(1,D) 的所有维数 D 下的表示，涵盖混合对称表示和费米子表示，并将其与德西特空间上可传播的各种场类型联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 德西特空间在宇宙学和量子引力研究中具有重要意义，其等距代数（isometry algebra）so(1,D) 的表示理论是理解该时空中场传播行为的基础，但现有文献中缺乏一个全面且面向物理的综述。

Method: 采用物理学视角，优先使用具体构造（concrete constructions）而非抽象考虑，系统梳理 so(1,D) 在所有维数 D 下的表示，包括混合对称表示（mixed symmetry representations）和费米子表示（fermionic representations）。

Result: 完整覆盖了德西特空间等距代数 so(1,D) 在所有维度下的表示类型，并建立了这些表示与德西特空间上可传播的各种场类型之间的对应关系。

Conclusion: 为德西特空间上的场论研究提供了一个系统的表示论基础，尤其便于从物理角度理解和应用这些构造。

Abstract: We review the representations of so(1,D), the algebra of isometries of D dimensional de Sitter space. We cover the representations in all D, including mixed symmetry representations and fermionic representations, and connect them to the various types of fields that can propagate on de Sitter space. The presentation is from a physics point of view, favoring concrete constructions over abstract considerations.

</details>


### [148] [Conserved charges and $L_\infty$ algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26224)
*Vinícius Bernardes,Theodore Erler,Atakan Hilmi Fırat*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在L∞代数框架下给出了任意拉格朗日场论中守恒荷的通用公式，该公式仅依赖于理论的L∞数据，无需参考拉格朗日量的导数结构，因此可应用于弦场论等非局域模型，并正确表达了广义相对论中的表面荷。 


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法在计算非局域模型（如弦场论（string field theory））的守恒荷时失效，亟需一种不依赖于拉格朗日量导数结构的一般性公式。	

Method: 该公式完全基于理论的L∞代数（L-infinity algebra）数据构建，无需参考拉格朗日量的具体导数结构，从而适用于任意拉格朗日场论。	

Result: 给出了守恒荷的一般公式，并验证该公式能正确表达广义相对论（general relativity）中基于Brown-York应力张量的表面荷（surface charge）。在杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theory）中的相关计算表明，该公式能自然处理空间边界。	

Conclusion: 该公式为拉格朗日场论中守恒荷的计算提供了一种普遍且不依赖拉格朗日量导数结构的代数方法，适用于弦场论等非局域模型，并能自然处理边界条件。	

Abstract: We give a formula for conserved charges in an arbitrary Lagrangian field theory expressed in the framework of $L_\infty$ algebras. The formula is expressed in terms of the theory's $L_\infty$ data alone, without reference to the derivative structure of the Lagrangian. Therefore conserved charges can be computed in nonlocal models, such as string field theory, where conventional methods break down. We also show that the formula correctly expresses the surface charge of general relativity in terms of the Brown-York stress tensor. Related computations in Yang-Mills theory suggest that spatial boundaries are dealt with in a natural fashion.

</details>


### [149] [An observer's quantization of 3d de Sitter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26241)
*Andreas Blommaert,Damiano Tietto,Herman Verlinde*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在三维de Sitter时空中提出了静态斑（static patch）的态密度定义与计算方法，利用与复Liouville弦（complex Liouville string）的全息对偶以及SL(2,ℤ)族Kerr-lens时空的求和，实现了量子能谱密度的精确计算，并展示了其与半经典引力预言的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: de Sitter时空的量子态计数是量子引力中的核心难题，尤其是静态斑区域的态密度（density of states）缺乏明确的计算方案。本文旨在为三维dS静态斑提出一个可计算的态密度定义。

Method: 提出对SL(2,ℤ)族的欧几里得无边界Kerr-lens时空进行求和，这些时空由具有给定能量和自旋的线缺陷（line-defect）产生。利用dS₃引力与两副本复Liouville弦（ℂLS）之间的全息对偶，将Kerr-lens时空映射为广义crosscap几何的SL(2,ℤ)族，并计算ℂLS ⊗ ℂLS的crosscap振幅。

Result: 计算得到的ℂLS ⊗ ℂLS crosscap振幅与半经典引力预言匹配。对于最简单的非平凡Kerr-lens时空，该对偶进一步等价于两副本双缩放SYK模型（double scaled SYK model）的GΣ有效场论。

Conclusion: GΣ ⊗ GΣ理论位于静态斑中观测者的世界线上，为发展三维de Sitter的微观世界线全息图（microscopic worldline hologram）奠定了基础。

Abstract: What is the density of states of the de Sitter static patch? We propose a definition and calculation of such a density in 3d dS. Our proposal involves a sum over an SL(2,$\mathbb{Z}$) set of Euclidean no-boundary Kerr-lens spacetimes sourced by a line-defect with given energy and spin - which in Lorentzian time represents an observer's worldline at the center of the dS static patch. We develop an exact quantum computation of the spectral density using a holographic duality between dS$_3$ gravity and two copies of $\mathbb{C}$LS, the complex Liouville string. The SL(2,$\mathbb{Z}$) Kerr-lens spacetimes map under the duality to an SL(2,$\mathbb{Z}$) family of generalized crosscap geometries. We compute the $\mathbb{C}$LS $\otimes$ $\mathbb{C}$LS crosscap amplitudes and show that they match the semi-classical gravity prediction. For the simplest non-trivial Kerr-lens space, the $\mathbb{C}$LS $\otimes$ $\mathbb{C}$LS description is, in turn, dual to two copies of the $GΣ$ effective field theory of the double scaled SYK model. The $GΣ\otimes GΣ$ theory lives on an observer's worldline in the static patch, setting the stage for developing a microscopic worldline hologram of 3d de Sitter.

</details>


### [150] [Charged and rotating near-horizon geometries in five dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26263)
*Alex Colling,Jun Liu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在五维爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论（Einstein-Maxwell theory）中构造了闭合解析形式的带电旋转近地平线几何（near-horizon geometries），并将其推广至含任意耦合常数的陈-西蒙斯项（Chern-Simons term）的理论；作者利用Sasaki结构（Sasakian structure）证明了这些解是共转电场为非零常数的最一般旋转极端视界（extremal horizons），并将构造推广至更高维度的Sasaki-爱因斯坦流形（Sasaki-Einstein manifold）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极端黑洞（extremal black holes）的近地平线几何是理解黑洞熵与全息对偶（holographic duality）的重要工具，然而在五维及更高维度的爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中，带电旋转近地平线几何的闭合解析形式解尚不充分，特别是含陈-西蒙斯项的一般情况。

Method: 采用闭合解析形式（closed analytic form）构造近地平线几何解；利用Sasaki结构（Sasakian structure）对解进行分类与刻画；将构造从五维推广至任意高维，以Sasaki-爱因斯坦流形（Sasaki-Einstein manifold）生成双参数带电旋转视界族。

Result: 得到了由电荷（charge）和两个独立角动量（angular momenta）参数化的新近地平线几何解，并可推广至含任意陈-西蒙斯耦合常数（Chern-Simons coupling constant）的理论；这些解在真空极限下不约化为迈尔斯-佩里视界（Myers-Perry horizon），但熵关系与预期一致；证明了这些解是共转电场（co-rotating electric field）为非零常数的最一般旋转极端视界，且无需对称性假设；在更高维度中，每个Sasaki-爱因斯坦流形（Sasaki-Einstein manifold）均可生成一个双参数带电旋转视界族。

Conclusion: 论文提供了五维及其以上维度爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中带电旋转极端视界近地平线几何的系统分类与构造方法，揭示了Sasaki结构在刻画这类几何中的核心作用，为极端黑洞的全息描述与熵计算提供了新的解析框架。

Abstract: We present new charged and rotating near-horizon geometries in five-dimensional Einstein-Maxwell theory in closed analytic form. The solutions can be parametrised by the charge and two independent angular momenta. We also generalise these near-horizon geometries to theories with an additional Chern-Simons term in the action multiplied by an arbitrary coupling constant. The new solutions have the same entropy relations as expected for charged versions of extremal Myers-Perry black holes and for rotating versions of extremal Reissner-Nordström-Tangherlini black holes, but they do not reduce to the Myers-Perry horizon in the vacuum limit. The horizon cross-sections are spherical and carry a Sasakian structure. We exploit this structure to prove a characterisation of our solutions: without any symmetry assumptions, they are the most general rotating extremal horizons for which the co-rotating electric field is a (non-zero) constant. We further extend this construction to higher dimensions, where we show that any Sasaki-Einstein manifold generates a two-parameter family of charged and rotating horizons.

</details>


### [151] [A Circle That Won't Return: The Fate of RR Fluxes and D-branes in Type 0A Tachyon Condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26280)
*Ahmed Rakin Kamal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于M理论在$S^1 \vee S^1$（两点相连的两个圆的楔）上的描述，研究0A型闭弦快子（closed-string tachyon）和双拉蒙-拉蒙（doubled Ramond-Ramond）扇区，论证快子凝聚对应于一个分支收缩至IIA型端点，并分析收缩分支相对RR场的红外屏蔽及其对偶解耦机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提出M理论在$S^1 \vee S^1$（楔形结构）上的描述，以此统一理解0A型弦理论中闭弦快子凝聚与双拉蒙-拉蒙（doubled Ramond-Ramond）扇区的动力学行为。

Method: 从0A型运动方程（equations of motion）推导出快子驻点的分支平衡条件（branch-balance condition），识别分支奇的RR涨落（branch-odd RR fluctuation）作为对称背景下快子的源；采用高斯定律估计孤立未屏蔽收缩分支$D_p^-$的长程RR场能量成本，并通过有效高阶施图克尔贝格机制（higher-form Stückelberg mechanism）描述相对RR场的红外屏蔽。

Result: 孤立未屏蔽的$D_p^-$源长程RR场能量成本随收缩半径倒数发散，推广了原始楔图像中$D0^-$膜解耦；识别出有效相对电荷载流子，并导出薄壁判据（thin-wall criterion），确定$D_p^- \to D_p^+$放电通道在参数意义上何时能量有利。

Conclusion: 快子凝聚对应楔的一个分支收缩至IIA型端点，收缩分支的RR数据通过屏蔽而非放电机制得以处理；存在有效的相对电荷载流子通道可在特定参数条件下实现放电。

Abstract: We study the closed-string tachyon and doubled Ramond-Ramond sector of type 0A in light of the proposed M-theory description on $S^1\vee S^1$-the wedge of two circles joined at a point. In this picture the two RR copies are associated with the two circle components, which we call branches, and tachyon condensation corresponds to shrinking one branch to the type IIA endpoint. From the type 0A equations of motion, we derive the branch-balance condition for a tachyon stationary point and identify the branch-odd RR fluctuation that sources the tachyon around a symmetric background. We then analyze the fate of the collapsing branch RR data as one branch of the wedge collapses to the type IIA endpoint. For an isolated unscreened collapsing-branch $D_p^-$ source, a Gauss-law estimate shows that the long-range RR field-energy cost scales inversely with the shrinking circle and thus becoming infinitely costly, generalizing the $D0^-$-brane decoupling in the original wedge picture. We describe the infrared screening of the relative RR field through an effective higher-form Stückelberg mechanism and distinguish this from a possible discharge of localized relative charge. Finally, using standard Wess-Zumino couplings of D-branes, we identify an effective relative-charge carrier and derive a parametric thin-wall criterion for when such a discharge channel $D_p^- \to D_p^+$ can be energetically favored.

</details>

Abstract: We consider Yang--Mills, Chalmers--Siegel and self-dual Yang--Mills (SDYM) theories within AdS/CFT correspondence. ### [153] [Deformed BTZ Radiance and Single Trace $T\bar{T}$ Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26357)
*Daniel Vainshtein*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将“太阳风（holar wind）”机制推广到旋转的λ-形变BTZ黑洞，证明无论形变耦合正负，发射概率由贝肯斯坦-霍金熵变ΔS_BH普适决定，并确定背景B场的唯一值，使其与单迹T\overline{T}形变对称乘积轨道理论的弦激发谱一致。

Method: 基于精确的$\frac{SL(2,\mathbb{R})_k\times U(1)}{U(1)}$规范-韦斯-朱米诺-维滕（gauged-WZW）世界sheet理论，分析探针粒子的测地线（geodesics）和隧穿率（tunneling rates），以及缠绕长弦的发射过程。

Conclusion: 所确立的机制可拓展至更广的黑洞类别，其长弦扇区（long string sector）对偶于单迹T\overline{T} + J\overline{T} + T\overline{J}形变理论。

Abstract: We generalize the "holar wind" mechanism proposed in arXiv:2303.00234 to the case of rotating $λ$-deformed BTZ black holes. These backgrounds, which interpolate between $AdS_3$ in the infrared and a linear dilaton spacetime in the ultraviolet, are realized as an exact $\frac{SL(2,\mathbb{R})_k\times U(1)}{U(1)}$ gauged-WZW worldsheet theory. By analyzing the geodesics and tunneling rates of probe particles and winding long strings, we show that the emission probabilities for both positive and negative deformation couplings are universally governed by the change in the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy, $ΔS_{BH}$. A central result of our analysis is that the consistency of long string emission within the grand canonical ensemble dictates a unique value for the background B-field at the origin. We demonstrate that this thermodynamically fixed value matches precisely the prediction required for the string excitation spectrum to agree with the $\mathbb{Z}_w$ twisted sector of a single-trace $T\overline{T}$ deformed symmetric product orbifold. Finally, we sketch the extension of these results to a broader class of black holes whose long string sector is dual to single-trace $T\overline{T} + J\overline{T} + T\overline{J}$ deformed theories.

Abstract: In this paper we construct duality-covariant worldvolume dynamics of particles and branes. For zero-branes, we propose an enlarged worldline model with a coadjoint orbit term to encode this. More generally, we propose worldvolume theories for arbitrary exotic branes in a way that generalises the known gauged sigma model of the Kaluza-Klein monopole. ### [155] [Holographic $s$- and $p$-wave superconductors from the $4D$ regularization of Einstein-Lovelock theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26546)

Abstract: We investigate holographically dual descriptions of $(2+1)$-dimensional s-wave and p-wave superconductors in the framework of regularized four-dimensional Einstein-Lovelock gravity theories, incorporating higher curvature corrections beyond the Gauss-Bonnet sector. The bulk geometry is constructed from exact black-brane solutions characterized by the fine-tuned Lovelock coupling $α$ and the highest power of curvature in the Lagrangian K. We then analyze the condensation of scalar and vector operators dual to minimally coupled matter fields, focusing on two bulk-field mass prescriptions, which significantly affect the superconducting phase. Our results demonstrate that higher curvature terms significantly modify the phase structure of both s-wave and p-wave systems and enhance the sensitivity of the condensates and critical temperatures to the gravitational couplings. In both cases, the critical temperature generally increases with the maximal curvature order K, leading to higher-$T_c$ phases compared to Einstein gravity, particularly for negative $α$. The coupling $α$ effectively governs the strength of higher curvature interactions in the bulk: positive $α$ suppresses condensation and lowers $T_c$, whereas negative $α$ enhances superconducting order and promotes higher-$T_c$ phases relative to Einstein gravity. We further study the optical conductivity and find that both the gap frequency and the ratio $ω_g/T_c$ exhibit a strong dependence on $α$ and $K$, deviating from the universal Einstein-gravity result. Higher curvature effects enhance the superconducting gap scale. Notably, the p-wave system shows a stronger sensitivity to the mass-fixing prescription compared to the s-wave case.

Abstract: Computing Ricci-flat metrics on Calabi-Yau manifolds is challenging since no closed-form solutions are known. ### [159] [Dyeing form factors as amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27022)
*Xinyue Li,Gang Yang,Guorui Zhu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过引入“染色”（dyeing）程序，将规范理论中的形状因子（form factors）的双重拷贝（double copy）中出现的虚假极点（spurious poles）解释为重力的物理传播子，并揭示了隐式因子化关系源自标准BCJ关系。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入一种“染色”（dyeing）程序，将色单态算符（color-singlet operator）或代表它的希格斯粒子（Higgs particle）提升为伴随表示的大质量态（adjoint massive state）。原始形状因子通过逆“漂白”操作（inverse bleaching operation）恢复，该操作实现为染色腿的U(1)退耦（U(1) decoupling）。在染色理论中，虚假极点变为有色振幅的普通物理传播子，隐式因子化关系则遵循标准BCJ关系。

Result: 该框架可应用于多重算符插入，给出多希格斯振幅（multi-Higgs amplitudes）的系统性双重拷贝构造，并作为副产品揭示了标量排序扇区（scalar-ordering sectors）。还讨论了更高长度标量算符和费米子算符，包括针对\barψγ^μψ的染色矢量构造，以及一个圈图层次的例子。

Conclusion: 染色程序系统性地解释了形状因子双重拷贝中虚假极点为何在引力中成为物理传播子，并揭示了其与BCJ关系的深层联系。该框架可推广至多重算符插入、不同自旋算符及圈图层次，具有广泛适用性。

Abstract: The double copy of form factors has revealed a striking feature: poles that are spurious from the gauge-theory perspective become physical propagators in gravity. At the same time, form factors obey hidden factorization relations on the kinematics of these poles. We explain both phenomena by introducing a dyeing procedure, which promotes the color-singlet operator, or the Higgs particle representing it, to an adjoint massive state. The original form factor is recovered by the inverse bleaching operation, realized as a $U(1)$ decoupling of the dyed leg. In the dyed theory, these apparent spurious poles turn into ordinary physical propagators of colored amplitudes, and the hidden factorization relations follow from standard BCJ relations. Applying this framework to multiple operator insertions gives a systematic double-copy construction for multi-Higgs amplitudes and, as a byproduct, reveals scalar-ordering sectors. We also discuss higher-length scalar operators and fermionic operators, including the dyed vector construction for $\barψγ^μψ$, as well as a loop-level example.

Abstract: Biadjoint scalar theory has been widely studied, due to its being closely related to the double copy correspondence linking gauge, gravity and related theories. In this paper, we continue a programme of work in elucidating non-linear solutions of this theory, and find a family of new solutions that are richer and more complex than previous cases. Using an ansatz that can be embedded in any choice of non-abelian colour groups, we demonstrate the existence of non-topological solitons, whose existence is protected by carrying a U(1) charge associated with certain rotations in colour space. The solutions are time-dependent, and closely related to the well-known Q-ball solutions in other scalar field theories. Result: 成功构造了D1-D5-P黑弦的引力指标鞍点，并通过退耦极限获得了BTZ × S³鞍点，该鞍点可用于计算D1-D5 CFT的指标。

Conclusion: 本文建立了从四维STU模型出发、经由4D-5D连接和弦对偶链构造D1-D5-P黑弦指标鞍点的完整方法，并证实其退耦极限下的BTZ × S³鞍点与对偶CFT指标直接关联，为理解黑弦微观态计数和指标计算提供了新路径。

Abstract: Boruch, Emparan, Iliesiu, and Murthy recently discussed index saddles for 5d black strings, showing that the black string saddle admits a decoupling limit to a complex, finite-temperature BTZ \times S^2 saddle that computes the index of the dual CFT. In this paper, we pursue an analogous construction for the D1-D5-P black string. We construct a four-charge index saddle in the four-dimensional STU model as the BPS limit of the non-extremal four-charge black hole, and show that it exhibits the new form of attraction. We then uplift it successively to five and six dimensions, via the 4D-5D connection and a chain of string dualities, to obtain the gravitational index saddle for the D1-D5-P black string. We take a systematic decoupling limit of this index saddle and obtain the BTZ \times S^3 saddle that computes the index of the D1-D5 CFT.

</details>


### [162] [Approximating Feynman integrals using complete monotonicity and Stieltjes properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27101)
*Sara Ditsch,Johannes M. Henn,Prashanth Raman*

TL;DR: 本文提出两种基于完全单调性（complete monotonicity, CM）和 Stieltjes 性质的新方法，用于 Feynman 积分数值评估，包括 CM 自举法和 Padé 逼近法，并通过实例（如大规模泡泡积分和 20 圈香蕉积分）验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Feynman 积分的数值评估是量子场论中的核心难题，传统方法往往依赖显式边界数据或收敛性有限。本文旨在利用 Feynman 积分在 Euclidean 区域中固有的完全单调性（complete monotonicity, CM）来开发无需边界条件、具有严格界限和可控收敛的新数值方法。

Method: 第一种方法为 CM 自举法（CM bootstrap）：利用标量 Feynman 积分在 Euclidean 区域中所有导数符号固定的完全单调性，从微分方程重建积分，无需显式边界数据即可获得严格界限。第二种方法基于 CM 的细化：证明在一定参数范围内 Feynman 积分不仅是 CM 函数，更是 Stieltjes 函数，从而允许在割切复平面（cut complex plane）上使用具有可证明收敛性的 Padé 逼近（Padé approximants），实现高效解析延拓和快速数值评估。

Result: 通过大规模泡泡积分等简单实例验证了方法的有效性，并展示了在多圈积分（包括 20 圈香蕉积分）中的应用潜力。两种方法均能提供严格的数值界限或收敛保证。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 CM 自举法和基于 Stieltjes 性质的 Padé 逼近法为 Feynman 积分计算开辟了新路径，具有无需边界数据、严格界限和可控收敛等优势。文章最后还讨论了多种扩展方向。

Abstract: We present two novel approaches for the numerical evaluation of Feynman integrals based on their universal analytic properties related to positivity, namely complete monotonicity (CM) and Stieltjes properties. Building on recent results, we exploit the fact that scalar Feynman integrals in the Euclidean region are completely monotonic functions, meaning that all their derivatives have a fixed sign. Building on this observation, the CM bootstrap allows one to reconstruct integrals from differential equations without explicit boundary data, yielding rigorous bounds. The second method is based on a refinement of CM. We prove that Feynman integrals, within a certain range of parameters, are not only CM but in fact Stieltjes functions. This enables the use of Padé approximants with provable convergence properties in the cut complex plane, providing an efficient method for analytic continuation and fast numerical evaluation. We illustrate the method with simple examples such as the massive bubble integral and discuss applications to multi-loop integrals, including the 20-loop banana integral. Finally, we comment on a number of extensions of these novel avenues for computing Feynman integrals.
