### [163] [The gauge invariance of non-perturbative vertex prescriptions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27213)
*M. E. Carrington,A. R. Frey,B. A. Meggison*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估不同非微扰连续方法（如施温格-戴森（Schwinger-Dyson）方程和3粒子不可约（3PI）有效作用量）在规范理论中的规范不变性（gauge invariance）表现，以判断其可靠性与适用范围。

Method: 在三维量子电动力学（quantum electrodynamics in three dimensions, QED₃）中，分别采用施温格-戴森（Schwinger-Dyson, SD）积分方程组和3粒子不可约（3-particle irreducible, 3PI）有效作用量自洽方程构建顶点；在朗道规范（Landau gauge）下计算，通过检验沃德恒等式（Ward identity）的满足程度来评估规范不变性。

Result: 大耦合下两种方法均对沃德恒等式（Ward identity）造成较显著违例，但3粒子不可约（3PI）有效理论略优于施温格-戴森（SD）顶点；与Ball-Chiu ansatz（Ball-Chiu ansatz）对比发现，小耦合下吻合良好，大耦合下偏差显著增大。

Conclusion: 非微扰连续方法在大耦合区域的规范不变性存在局限，Ball-Chiu ansatz亦不能完全替代严格非微扰顶点；研究结果对理解规范理论中的相变（phase transitions）可能具有启示意义。

Abstract: We study the gauge invariance of different continuum methods to include non-perturbative effects in gauge theories. We work with three dimensional quantum electrodynamics and implement vertices using two different methods: a set of coupled Schwinger-Dyson (SD) integral equations, and the self-consistent equations obtained from the 3-particle irreducible (3PI) effective action. We work in Landau gauge and assess the extent to which results are gauge invariant by checking how well the Ward identity is satisfied. Our results show that there is a fairly significant violation of the Ward identity at large coupling, although the 3PI effective theory is slightly better than the SD vertex. We also compare the results of both calculations with the commonly used Ball-Chiu ansatz and show that the agreement of the ansatz with both non-perturbative vertices is fairly good at small coupling but deviates more significantly at large coupling. We compare results for the two point functions of the theory and discuss the possible implications for phase transitions.

### [164] [Causality and the Equivalence Principle for Higher Energy Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27222)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究表明散射振幅的高能行为具有普遍性，与电荷无关，从而将等效原理（equivalence principle）拓展到引力子极点之外。本文旨在通过研究彩色散射的雷吉极限，推导出对这种行为更严格的因果性约束。

Method: 将轨迹参数化为 s^{α(t)}，其中 α(0)=2-δ，分析不可约散射通道中的 Shapiro/Wigner--Smith 时间延迟。关键点在于：eikonal 相位在 t 通道不可约表示中自然组织，而物理时间延迟是其在 s 通道中的本征值。

Result: 任何非单态轨迹若满足 δ<1/2，都会产生增长且符号不确定的时间延迟（δ=1/2 为边际情况，依赖于维度），该延迟在弱引力（weak gravity）机制下的雷吉扩散区（Regge diffusion region）占据主导。

Conclusion: 非单态交换（non-singlet exchange）会重新耦合到物理通道中，且两种符号均会出现，从而至少在某个通道中不可避免地产生负的时间延迟，这违反了因果性，因此对高能行为的普遍性施加了更严格的约束。

Abstract: Recently, it was proposed that the leading high-energy behavior of scattering amplitudes is universal, independent of charge, thereby extending the equivalence principle beyond the graviton pole. In this Letter, we derive a sharper causality constraint on such behavior by studying the Regge limit of colored scattering. Parameterizing a trajectory by $s^{α(t)}$ with $α(0)=2-δ$, we analyze the Shapiro/Wigner--Smith time-delays in the irreducible scattering channels. We show that any non-singlet trajectory with $δ< 1/2$ produces a growing sign-indefinite time-delay (with $δ=1/2$ a marginal, dimension-dependent case), which becomes dominant in the Regge diffusion region in the weak-gravity regime. The essential point is that, while the eikonal phase is naturally organized in $t$-channel irreducible representations, the physical time-delays are its eigenvalues in the $s$-channel. A non-singlet exchange therefore recouples into the physical channels with both signs, inevitably producing a negative time-delay in at least one channel.

### [165] [Characteristic Lightcone Sources in SO(1,3) Yang-Mills Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27241)
*Kaushlendra Kumar*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Yang-Mills理论的SO(1,3)对称约化中，应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）在类时与类空Lorentz轨道上光滑，但在分隔两区域的光锥（lightcone）上发散。作者试图理解这一奇异性所对应的物理源（source）是什么。

Method: 作者提出对奇异分母进行实平移（real shift），但发现该操作仅将奇异支撑（singular support）移至光锥外的双曲面，无法同时保持源的守恒性与无迹性。转而采用光锥上的完备化（completion），通过匹配条件（matching condition）将解确定至一个参数χ，该参数具有未来与过去光锥相对权重的因果解释。

Result: 平移操作无法同时保持源的守恒（conserved）与无迹（traceless）性质；而光锥上的完备化可以同时满足这两条约束。完备化的源在正则等时切片（constant-time slice）上的总四动量（four-momentum）为零，其物理内容表现为一个由曲率响应（curvature response）推断出的残存因果荷。

Conclusion: 光锥上的完备化是消除Yang-Mills理论中SO(1,3)对称约化奇异性的自然方案，该完备化源虽然总四动量为零，但携带一个由参数χ表征的残存因果荷，可能具有深刻的因果结构意义。

Abstract: The SO(1,3)-symmetric reduction of Yang-Mills theory on Minkowski space yields a stress-energy tensor that is smooth on the timelike and spacelike Lorentz orbits but diverges on the lightcone that separates the two regions. We ask what consistent source this singularity represents. A natural cure is a real shift of the singular denominator. This does not regularize the source but instead moves the singular support onto a hyperboloid off the cone, where the corresponding source cannot remain both conserved and traceless. Our analysis shows that the displaced support cannot retain both properties, whereas a completion on the lightcone can. The matching condition fixes this completion up to one parameter $χ$, which has a causal interpretation as the relative weight of the future and past cones. On regular constant-time slices, the completed source carries zero total four-momentum, so its physical content is a residual causal charge inferred from its curvature response.

### [166] [Universal Lichnerowicz Lifting of Near-Horizon Soft Modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27308)
*Peng Cheng,Yu-Qi Liu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文揭示了近极端黑洞（near-extremal black holes）低温量子热力学中普适性的Lichnerowicz谱起源：近地平线张量零模式（tensor zero modes）在温度微扰下发生一阶升移（first-order lift），且经投影后局部几何细节抵消，最终由边界重参化动力学（boundary reparametrization dynamics）即Schwarzian软扇区（Schwarzian soft sector）决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 针对含二维极大对称喉咙（maximally symmetric throat）的极端近地平线几何，构造与近地平线重参化（near-horizon reparametrizations）相关的归一化横迹无张量零模式（normalizable transverse-traceless tensor zero modes）；通过Lichnerowicz算子的一阶形变（first-order deformation）分析小温度如何使零模式升移；在静态球对称及旋转背景下计算本征值移位，并对比投影后结果。

Result: 局域矩阵元依赖于母几何细节，但这些细节在投影到归一化张量模式后相互抵消，留下普适结果。对于静态球对称背景，本征值移位与傅里叶模数和温度成正比；旋转背景下角向扭曲因子仅改变整体投影因子。该升移体积谱正是Schwarzian软扇区的Lichnerowicz实现。

Conclusion: 近极端黑洞低温量子热力学的普适一阶结果可追溯至近地平线张量零模式与边界重参化动力学之间的红外体-边界匹配（infrared bulk-boundary matching）。

Abstract: A remarkable universality appears in the low-temperature quantum thermodynamics of near-extremal black holes, where distinct parent geometries often lead to the same logarithmic temperature dependence at one loop. In this work, we study the Lichnerowicz spectral origin of this infrared universality and understand why the relevant spectral data become insensitive to the details of the parent geometry. For extremal near-horizon geometries containing a two-dimensional maximally symmetric throat, we construct the normalizable transverse-traceless tensor zero modes associated with near-horizon reparametrizations. Turning on a small temperature lifts these zero modes through the first-order deformation of the Lichnerowicz operator. Although the local matrix element depends on detailed parent-geometry data, these data cancel after projection onto normalized tensor modes, leaving the universal result. For static spherically symmetric backgrounds, the eigenvalue shift is universally proportional to the Fourier mode number and temperature, and the same structure persists for rotating backgrounds, where angular warp factors only modify the overall projection factor. We further show that this lifted bulk spectrum is the Lichnerowicz realization of the Schwarzian soft sector. Thus, the universal first-order result is traced to an infrared bulk-boundary matching between near-horizon tensor zero modes and boundary reparametrization dynamics.

### [167] [Laplace Space for Cosmological Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27309)
*Nathan Belrhali,Arthur Poisson,Sébastien Renaux-Petel*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）的通用方法，将视界内部（deep inside the horizon）的宇宙学模（cosmological mode）分解为平面波（flat-space plane wave）的叠加，从而将弯曲时空中的宇宙学关联子（cosmological correlator）计算转化为平坦时空费曼图（flat-space diagram）的积分表示，并给出了封闭解析解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学关联子的计算在弯曲时空中通常非常复杂，现有方法需要针对不同运动学区域拼凑不同的展开式，缺乏统一且简洁的解析框架。本文旨在发展一种通用且计算高效的方法，以简化早期宇宙理论中关联子的计算。

Method: 利用拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform），将每个弯曲时空模分解为平面波（plane wave）的叠加，并通过一个编码了时空几何（spacetime geometry）、场内容（field content）和动力学（dynamics）的核（kernel）进行 dressing，从而将时间积分约化为平坦时空积分。该方法进一步提供了简单的图解规则（diagrammatic rules），将宇宙学关联子图（cosmological correlator diagram）转化为平坦空间对应图在拉普拉斯空间核上的积分。

Result: 在典型的单交换图（massive single exchange）例子中，该积分表示使得能量奇点（energy singularities）清晰呈现，并以单一快速收敛级数（rapidly convergent series）的形式在整个运动学域（kinematic domain）内给出了封闭解析解，无需对不同区域进行分块展开。

Conclusion: 拉普拉斯方法（Laplace approach）在概念上和计算上均能有效简化几乎任何早期宇宙理论中的宇宙学关联子计算，为相关研究提供了新的统一视角。

Abstract: Deep inside the horizon, every cosmological mode oscillates as a flat-space plane wave. A Laplace transform turns this fact into a general method: it resolves each curved-space mode into a superposition of plane waves dressed by a kernel that encodes the spacetime geometry, field content and dynamics, collapsing the time integrals onto flat-space ones. This provides simple diagrammatic rules that turn cosmological correlator diagrams into their flat-space counterparts integrated against Laplace-space kernels. On the paradigmatic massive single exchange, this integral representation makes the energy singularities manifest and evaluates in closed form as a single, rapidly convergent series valid throughout the kinematic domain, with no patching of separate expansions. The Laplace approach sheds conceptual and computational light on cosmological correlators in virtually any theory of the early universe.

### [168] [Massive Cosmological Correlators from Flat Space: a Laplace-Space Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27311)
*Nathan Belrhali,Arthur Poisson,Sébastien Renaux-Petel*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）的宇宙学关联子（cosmological correlators）新计算方法，将弯曲时空中的模式函数分解为平空间平面波（flat-space plane wave）的连续叠加，从而将弯曲时空的积分简化为平空间基本积分，并给出简洁的图解规则（diagrammatic rules）。该方法以共形耦合场在德西特时空中交换大质量标量粒子为例进行了说明，并指出可推广至原初宇宙学（primordial cosmology）的绝大多数情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弯曲时空中的宇宙学关联子计算通常复杂，现有方法难以直观揭示其物理结构与奇异性。本文旨在利用“哈勃半径内部模式振荡可近似为平空间平面波”这一物理事实，发展一种计算工具，使弯曲时空效应仅通过一个核函数（kernel）体现，从而简化计算并揭示关联子的能量奇异性（energy singularities）从平空间出发的透明来源。

Method: 该方法的核心是拉普拉斯变换：将弯曲时空中的模式函数（mode function）表示为由对偶变量标记的平空间平面波的连续叠加，并由一个编码时空几何、场内容和动力学的核函数进行修饰。经过该变换，所有时间积分均退化为平空间的基本积分，从而导出简单的图解规则。

Result: 以大质量单交换关联子（massive single-exchange correlator）为例，拉普拉斯表示使得总能量奇异性（total-energy singularities）和部分能量奇异性（partial-energy singularities）从平空间角度变得透明，并在整个运动学区域（kinematic domain）内给出一个单一的闭式快速收敛级数（closed-form, rapidly convergent series）。

Conclusion: 该方法虽以共形耦合场在德西特（de Sitter）时空中交换大质量标量粒子为例进行构建，但其框架本质上可直接适用于原初宇宙学中几乎所有感兴趣的情形。

Abstract: We develop a new approach to cosmological correlators, built on a simple physical fact: deep inside the Hubble radius every mode oscillates as a flat-space plane wave, the curvature of spacetime making itself felt only as the mode is stretched towards the horizon. A Laplace transform turns this observation into a computational tool, resolving each curved-space mode function into a continuous superposition of plane waves labelled by a dual variable and dressed by a kernel that encodes the spacetime geometry, field content and dynamics. Every time integral then reduces to an elementary flat-space one, yielding simple diagrammatic rules for cosmological correlators. We illustrate the construction on the massive single-exchange correlator. The Laplace representation makes its total- and partial-energy singularities transparent ''from flat space'', and yields a single closed-form, rapidly convergent series valid throughout the entire kinematic domain. Although developed for conformally coupled fields exchanging massive scalars in de Sitter, the approach carries over essentially unchanged to virtually all situations of interest in primordial cosmology.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于p≠3的Dp-膜，超引力解中非恒定膨胀子轮廓在全息对偶下对应着SYM耦合常数的跑动。而对于D-瞬子（p=-1），IKKT矩阵模型缺乏时空维度，使得这种全息解释难以直接建立，因此需要一种新的方法来实现这一对应。

Method: 论文基于两个密切相关的方法：一是库仑支方法（Coulomb branch method），通过将IKKT作用量中主导修正项的系数与弦耦合常数（string coupling）相关联，计算其对库仑支位置（Coulomb branch position）的依赖关系；二是BZJ重整化群流（BZJ RG flow），将其应用于IKKT配分函数（partition function），考察耦合常数g随矩阵模型秩N的跑动。

Result: 通过库仑支方法，矩阵理论与超引力在库仑支位置的依赖关系上实现了匹配。通过BZJ流，耦合常数g随秩N的跑动重现了超引力中轴-膨胀子场对N的依赖关系。

Conclusion: 两种方法均有效建立了D-瞬子矩阵模型与超引力之间的全息对应，特别是BZJ重整化群流成功将矩阵模型的秩N解释为重整化群标度，为IKKT矩阵模型的全息对偶提供了新视角。

Abstract: Supergravity solutions describing stacks of D$p$-branes with $p\neq 3$ feature a non-constant dilaton profile, which is holographically mapped to the running of the SYM coupling in $(p+1)$ dimensions. For D-instantons ($p=-1$), the lack of space and time in the IKKT matrix model makes such an interpretation difficult at first. In this letter, we propose a method to achieve this based on two closely related concepts: the IKKT method of integrating out heavy strings in a Coulomb branch vacuum and the matrix RG flow of Brézin and Zinn-Justin (BZJ). The notable difference between the two is that the BZJ RG flow also integrates over the Coulomb branch position. We first apply the Coulomb branch method and by relating the coefficient of the leading correction to the IKKT action with the string coupling, we can compute its dependence on the Coulomb branch position, finding a match between matrix theory and supergravity. Next, we apply the BZJ-flow to the IKKT partition function, which leads to a running of the coupling constant $g$ with the rank $N$ of the matrix model, reproducing the $N$-dependence of the axio-dilaton field in supergravity.

</details>


### [170] [Probing Probability Geometry with Schwinger--Dyson Identities: Score Mismatch, Fisher Information, and Configurational Temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27360)
*Anosh Joseph*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过引入单一"分数失配场"（score-mismatch field δs），建立了Schwinger-Dyson恒等式的几何解释框架，统一描述了非平衡采样、配置温度（configurational temperature）和Fisher信息（Fisher information）之间的几何结构关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为Schwinger-Dyson恒等式（Schwinger-Dyson identities）提供几何化的理解，并揭示其与Fisher信息、配置温度和非平衡采样之间的深层联系。

Method: 定义分数失配场 δs = ∇ log(Q/P_eq) 作为偏离平衡的度量，将每个Schwinger-Dyson恒等式解释为该场在构型空间（configuration space）探针方向上的投影，并将相对Fisher信息（relative Fisher information）定义为该场的平方范数。

Result: 建立了Fisher信息与完整Schwinger-Dyson恒等式层级之间的普适界限（universal bound），表明Fisher信息的收敛可恢复所有Schwinger-Dyson恒等式；获得了相对Fisher信息的变分刻画；揭示了配置温度作为一类特殊Schwinger-Dyson探针（Schwinger-Dyson probe）的地位。

Conclusion: 分数失配场为理解Schwinger-Dyson恒等式、配置温度、Fisher信息以及随机过程中的非平衡采样提供了统一的几何语言；Stein算子（Stein operators）和得分函数方法（score-function methods）自然地源于这一概率-几何结构。

Abstract: We develop a geometric interpretation of Schwinger--Dyson identities by showing that their violations are controlled by a single score-mismatch field $δs$. For an arbitrary sampled probability distribution $Q$ and equilibrium measure $P_{\rm eq}$, every Schwinger--Dyson violation is determined by $δs = \nabla \log (Q / P_{\rm eq})$, which characterizes the departure from equilibrium. Each Schwinger--Dyson identity measures a projection of this field onto a probe direction in configuration space. The relative Fisher information is its squared norm. This gives a universal bound relating Fisher information to the complete Schwinger--Dyson hierarchy, thus implying that convergence in Fisher information restores all Schwinger--Dyson identities. We further obtain a variational characterization of the relative Fisher information in terms of Schwinger--Dyson violations, leading to a natural tomographic interpretation in which increasingly rich families of probe fields encode progressively more information about the underlying probability distortion. The configurational temperature, within this framework, emerges as a distinguished Schwinger--Dyson probe. The Stein operators and score-function methods arise naturally from the same probability-geometric structure. The score-mismatch field, therefore, provides a unified geometric language for understanding Schwinger--Dyson identities, configurational temperature, Fisher information, and non-equilibrium sampling in stochastic processes.

</details>

### [171] [On the deformation theory of chiral quantizations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27341)
*Dylan Butson,Sujay Nair*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种操作化方法（operadic approach）用于顶点泊松代数（vertex Poisson algebras）的形变量子化（deformation quantization），这是泊松代数（Poisson algebras）形变量子化问题的手性类比。主要结果为一个逐阶形变-障碍理论（order-by-order deformation-obstruction theory），由手性泊松上同调（Poisson cohomology）控制。在仿射辛簇（affine symplectic varieties）弧空间上的顶点泊松代数量子化特例中，该形变-障碍理论由德拉姆上同调（de Rham cohomology）控制。此外，证明边界Virasoro极小模型在形变下是刚性的（rigid）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典泊松代数形变量子化问题推广至手性（chiral）情形，即顶点泊松代数的形变量子化，以建立更广泛的量子化理论框架。

Method: 采用操作化（operadic）方法，并建立逐阶形变-障碍理论，利用手性泊松上同调作为控制形变的障碍对象。

Result: 形变-障碍理论由手性泊松上同调控制；在仿射辛簇弧空间函数对应的顶点泊松代数量子化中，该障碍由德拉姆上同调控制；边界Virasoro极小模型在形变下是刚性的。

Conclusion: 本文为顶点泊松代数的形变量子化提供了系统的形变-障碍理论，并在特殊情形下将其简化为德拉姆上同调，同时揭示了某些共形场论模型（conformal field theory models）的刚性性质。

Abstract: We give an operadic approach to deformation quantization of vertex Poisson algebras, a chiral analogue of the traditional problem of deformation quantization of Poisson algebras. Our main result is an order-by-order deformation-obstruction theory for such quantizations, controlled by the chiral analogue of Poisson cohomology. In the special case of chiral quantizations of affine symplectic varieties, quantizations of the vertex Poisson algebras of functions on their arc spaces, we prove that this deformation-obstruction theory is controlled by their de Rham cohomology. As another application, we prove that the boundary Virasoro minimal models are rigid under deformations.

</details>

### [172] [The odd fermion at the edge: odd-even staggering in the trapped, unitary Fermi gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26225)
*Silas R. Beane,Domenico Orlando,Susanne Reffert*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过大N Bogoliubov-de Gennes（BdG）描述和大电荷有效场论（large-charge EFT）两种方法，研究了谐振阱中 unitary 费米气体在大粒子数 Q 下的奇偶交错（odd-even staggering）现象，发现奇数粒子数下的额外费米子形成边缘局域准粒子，并推导出奇偶分裂能的标度律和通用边缘系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解谐振阱中 unitary 费米气体在大电荷极限下的奇偶交错机制，即奇数与偶数粒子数系统之间的能量差异。

Method: 采用大N BdG 描述（large-N BdG description）和大电荷有效场论（large-charge EFT）两种互补方法，将微观 BdG 问题在边缘极限下约化为通用耦合 Airy 系统（coupled Airy system），并通过数值计算验证标度律（scaling）和局域化（localization）性质。

Result: 奇数粒子数下的额外费米子形成托马斯-费米面（Thomas-Fermi surface）附近的边缘局域准粒子（edge-localized quasiparticle）而非体激发。奇偶分裂能（odd-even splitting energy）由最低正本征值决定，标度形式为 χ ξ^(1/6) (24Q)^(1/9) ħω + ...，其中 ξ 为 Bertsch 参数，χ 为通用边缘系数（universal edge coefficient）。EFT 描述边界上的费米子模式与超流 Goldstone 场（superfluid Goldstone field）的耦合，再现相同 Q 标度并引入两个低能常数（low-energy constants）的依赖。数值谱确认了标度律和局域化性质。

Conclusion: 大电荷极限下 unitary 费米气体的奇偶交错由边缘局域的准粒子激发主导，其能量标度律由通用边缘系数和 Bertsch 参数共同决定，两种理论方法（BdG 和 EFT）互相印证。

Abstract: We investigate the odd-even staggering in the harmonically-trapped unitary Fermi gas at large particle-number charge $Q$. Using both a large-$N$ BdG description and a complementary large-charge EFT method, we show that for odd particle number the extra fermion forms an edge-localized quasiparticle near the Thomas-Fermi surface rather than a bulk excitation. In the edge limit, the microscopic BdG problem reduces to a universal coupled Airy system whose lowest positive eigenvalue fixes the leading odd-even splitting energy, $χ\,ξ^{1/6}(24Q)^{1/9}\,\hbarω+ \cdots$ where $ξ$ is the Bertsch parameter, and $χ$ is a universal edge coefficient. The associated EFT describes a fermionic mode confined to the boundary and coupled to the superfluid Goldstone field, reproducing the same $Q$ scaling while introducing a dependence on two low-energy constants. Finally, we numerically compute the spectrum and confirm the predicted scaling and localization properties.

</details>


### [173] [Non-ergodic dynamical phase transition via a zero-mode exceptional point in a non-Markov atomic Josephson junction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26394)
*Koichiro Furutani*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在头尾耦合的玻色-约瑟夫森结（Bose-Josephson junction）中发现了一种由非马尔可夫摩擦导致的零模例外点（zero-mode exceptional point）所驱动的非遍历动力学相变，该相变在马尔可夫极限下不存在，并且对量子涨落具有宏观鲁棒性，为耗散环境中的长寿命量子存储器提供了潜在平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放量子系统通常因环境退相干（decoherence）而丧失初始记忆并最终热化，本文旨在挑战这一传统范式，探索是否存在非马尔可夫（non-Markov）动力学机制能够打破热化预期并维持非遍历行为。

Method: 采用内在动量耦合的Caldeira-Leggett模型描述头尾耦合的玻色-约瑟夫森结，通过精确非马尔可夫朗之万模拟（non-Markov Langevin simulations）进行分析，并结合等效驱动XXZ自旋链的数值量子模拟进行验证。

Result: 发现了一种新型非遍历动力学相变（non-ergodic dynamical phase transition），系统可进入一个持续运行状态（running state），该相变在马尔可夫极限下不存在；揭示了该相变由非马尔可夫摩擦产生的零模例外点（zero-mode exceptional point）所驱动，其拓扑特征表现为响应函数的缠绕（winding）。在等效XXZ自旋链的数值模拟中，这一例外点导致的动力学特征在强量子涨落和环境动态反作用下仍稳健存在，表现为动力学交叉（dynamical crossover）。

Conclusion: 该例外点起源的动力学相变具有宏观鲁棒性（macroscopic robustness），为在耗散环境中实现长寿命量子存储器（long-lived quantum memories）提供了有前景的平台。

Abstract: Open quantum systems typically lose their initial memory due to the environmental decoherence resulting in thermalization. We demonstrate a striking breakdown of this paradigm in a head-to-tail Bose-Josephson junction, which is described by an intrinsically momentum-coupled Caldeira-Leggett model. Through exact non-Markov Langevin simulations, we discover a novel type of non-ergodic dynamical phase transitions into a running state, which has no counterpart in Markov limit. Crucially, we reveal that this transition is fundamentally governed by a zero-mode exceptional point emerging from the non-Markov friction. This topological origin is characterized by the winding of the response function. Finally, numerical quantum simulations of an equivalent driven XXZ spin chain confirm that this exceptional-point-induced signature robustly survives as a dynamical crossover against strong quantum fluctuations and the dynamical backreaction of the environment. This macroscopic robustness offers a promising platform for long-lived quantum memories in dissipative environments.

</details>


### [174] [Binary Dipolar Condensates of Dysprosium Isotopes with Tunable Spatial Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26606)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实现了相互作用控制的互溶-相分离转变（miscibility transition），伴随凝聚体界面从核-壳状（core–shell-like）依次重构为并列状（side-by-side）和交换核-壳状（exchanged core–shell-like）几何结构；在固定相互作用下，种群不平衡通过重塑有效平均场压力提供了第二个连续调控相分离序的控制旋钮。

Conclusion: 镝同位素混合物为工程化偶极量子物质中的互溶性、界面和空间序建立了一个紧凑平台，直接关联到密度-自旋耦合物理和二元超固体（binary supersolidity）等方向。

Abstract: Dipolar quantum mixtures provide a unique route to interaction-driven many-body phases, where long-range anisotropic interactions intertwine the density, spin and spatial order. Here we realize binary Bose--Einstein condensates of the highly magnetic isotopes $^{162}$Dy and $^{164}$Dy in a technically minimal, single-species-like apparatus. Their nearly identical single-particle properties yield naturally matched trapping potentials, while dense intra- and inter-species Feshbach spectra provide strong interaction tunability. We use this platform to drive an interaction-controlled miscibility transition of a dipolar binary condensate, accompanied by a reconfiguration of the condensate interface from core--shell-like to side-by-side and exchanged core--shell-like geometries. At fixed interactions, population imbalance provides a second control knob by reshaping the effective mean-field pressures and continuously tuning the phase-separated order. These results establish dysprosium isotope mixtures as a compact platform for engineering miscibility, interfaces, and spatial order in dipolar quantum matter, with direct connections to coupled density--spin physics and binary supersolidity.

### [175] [In situ cryogenic characterization of proton damage in thick p-channel skipper CCDs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26409)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对p-channel Skipper CCD在低温工作温度下进行辐射硬度测试，评估浮栅输出级和全局CCD参数（包括电荷转移效率、暗电流、热像素和电荷陷阱）的性能变化。

Conclusion: 首次证实p-channel Skipper CCD在真实的深空热辐射环境中保持辐射硬度，为将其应用于长期深空天文任务提供了实验依据。

Abstract: Skipper charge-coupled devices (CCDs) are an offshoot of standard silicon pixel detectors and are capable of performing repeated non-destructive charge measurements, enabling deeply sub-electron readout noise. This capability has opened the door to single-photon counting from the near-infrared ($\sim$1.1\,$μ$m) to the soft X-ray (several keV), making these devices strong candidates for future astronomical instruments operating in the photon-starved limit. Furthermore, the p-channel architecture used to fabricate Skipper CCDs on n-type silicon has been demonstrated to have an increased hardness to the intense radiation environment of space. Building upon previous irradiation campaigns on room-temperature sensors, here we describe the first radiation-hardness tests of p-channel skipper CCDs at their cryogenic operating temperatures. We assess the performance of the floating-gate output stage and global CCD parameters (charge transfer inefficiency, dark current, hot pixels, and charge traps). We find that these devices maintain excellent performance after displacement damage doses equivalent to ${\sim}$10 years at the Earth/Sun L2 Lagrange point, demonstrating for the first time that these sensors remain radiation-hard in realistic deep-space thermal and radiation environments.

### [176] [Onsager--Machlup functionals for McKean--Vlasov SDEs via Euler-type approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26929)
*Ying Chao,Pingyuan Wei*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文通过引入基于经典无分布随机微分方程的欧拉近似格式，克服了系数固有分布依赖性带来的困难，成功将Onsager–Machlup作用量泛函推广至McKean–Vlasov随机微分方程，并推导出显式表达式，该构造性方法可适用于一大类分布依赖型随机系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Onsager–Machlup作用量泛函（action functional）为非平衡涨落（nonequilibrium fluctuations）研究中随机系统最可能转移路径的表征提供了变分框架。然而，将其推广至McKean–Vlasov随机微分方程（McKean–Vlasov SDE）时，系数内在的分布依赖性（distribution dependence）构成了技术难点。

Method: 提出一种基于经典无分布随机微分方程（distribution-free stochastic differential equations）的欧拉型逼近方案（Euler-type approximation scheme）；再将经典Onsager–Machlup理论与逼近序列的收敛性论证（convergence argument）相结合。

Result: 推导出了与McKean–Vlasov SDE相关联的Onsager–Machlup泛函的显式表达式（explicit expression）。

Conclusion: 该构造性方法（constructive approach）可扩展至一大类分布依赖型随机系统（distribution-dependent stochastic systems）。

Abstract: The Onsager--Machlup action functional provides a variational framework for characterizing the most probable transition paths of stochastic systems and plays an important role in the study of nonequilibrium fluctuations. Its extension to McKean--Vlasov stochastic differential equations is complicated by the intrinsic distribution dependence of the coefficients. In this paper, we address this difficulty by introducing an Euler-type approximation scheme based on classical, distribution-free stochastic differential equations. Combining the classical Onsager--Machlup theory with a convergence argument for the approximation sequence, we derive an explicit expression for the Onsager--Machlup functional associated with the McKean--Vlasov SDE. The proposed approach is constructive and extends to a broad class of distribution-dependent stochastic systems.

</details>
